\newcommand{\passing}{After you play this card, pass it to the player on your left, who adds it to their hand.}

\begin{document}
\title{The Unofficial Agricola Compendium}
\date{\normalsize Version 9.0 (2010-12-17)}
\maketitle

This is a complete list of minor improvements and
occupations in the game Agricola.

Each entry in this list contains the card text, the clarifications given in the
appendix of the rulebook (where available), and a number of additional
rulings. Many of these rulings are based on clarifications by Uwe
Rosenberg, the game author, and Hanno Girke of Lookout Games. New
rulings will be added when they're posted on BoardGameGeek or the
Lookout-Games.de forums.

Some of the rulings have been made up entirely by me. These rulings are
entirely unofficial, and can be changed at all times, for example when
the game author contradicts them. These unofficial rulings are enclosed
in hooks \ecp{like this}, and can be accepted or ignored as you wish.

This document is based on the German second edition of the game. The
translation is based on (but not the same as) the translation by Melissa
Rogerson.

\section{Improvements}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\card{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}{(1VP. Cost 2C/3C.)}
{At any time, you may convert goods to food as follows: vegetable $\rightarrow$ 2 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 2 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 2 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 3 food. Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You can own more than one Fireplace.}
\item \ecp{With this card, you can convert several animals and vegetables to food at the same time. When you bake bread you can convert as many grain as you want. You may bake bread and convert other goods to food at the same time, in order to activate the \cardref{Gypsy's Crock}{Dreibeinkessel}{E19}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}{(1VP. Cost 4C/5C or fireplace.)}
{At any time, you may convert goods to food as follows: vegetable $\rightarrow$ 3 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 2 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 3 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 4 food. Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you upgrade the \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2} major improvement, the card is returned to the major improvements board. If the minor improvement \cardref{Simple Fireplace}{Einfache Feuerstelle}{E20} is upgraded, it is removed from the game.}
\item \apx{You can own more than one Cooking Hearth.}
\item \ecp{With this card, you can convert several animals and vegetables to food at the same time. When you bake bread you can convert as many grain as you want. You may bake bread and convert other goods to food at the same time, in order to activate the \cardref{Gypsy's Crock}{Dreibeinkessel}{E19}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Oven}{Lehmofen}{A5}{(2VP. Cost 3C 1S.)}
{Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you can turn \changed{exactly} 1 grain into 5 food. When you take this card, you can also \changed{bake bread immediately}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you may bake bread with all of your ovens and other suitable improvements.}
\item \apx[Baker's Oven]{Is an oven.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Oven}{Steinofen}{A6}{(3VP. Cost 3S 1C.)}
{Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you can turn up to 2 grain into 4 food each. When you take this card, you can \changed{bake bread immediately}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you may bake bread with all of your ovens and other suitable improvements.}
\item \apx[Baker's Oven]{Is an oven.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}{(2VP. Cost 2W 2S.)}
{In each harvest, you can use the Joinery to convert \changed{exactly} 1 wood to 2 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1/2/3 bonus points for 3/5/7 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{At the end of the game, wood on the \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} and the \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278} counts.} \apx[2nd ed, Beckenbauer]{Wood on the \cardref{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273} \ecp{and \cardref{Resource Seller}{Werkstoffhðndler}{K310}} does not count.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8}{(2VP. Cost 2C 2S.)}
{In each harvest, you can use the Pottery to convert \changed{exactly} 1 clay to 2 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1/2/3 bonus points for 3/5/7 clay.}

\card{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9}{(2VP. Cost 2R 2S.)}
{In each harvest, you can use the Basketmaker's Workshop to convert \changed{exactly} 1 reed to 3 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1/2/3 bonus points for 2/4/5 reed.}

\card{Well}{Brunnen}{A10}{(4VP. Cost 3S 1W.)}
{Place 1 food \changed{from the general supply} on each of the next 5 round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.}

\card{Field}{Acker}{E11}{(Cost 1F.)}
{When you play this card, immediately plough 1 field. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may not use a plough or the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68} when you play this card.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fishing Rod}{Angel}{E12}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, you receive 1 additional food. From round 8 \changed{onwards}, you receive 2 additional food.}

\card{Axe}{Axt}{E13}{(Cost 1W 1S.)}
{Whenever you add a room to your wooden hut, you only pay 2 wood and 2 reed.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/341957]{If you build more than one room, you can use the Axe for each room.}% Also http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1168
\item \apx[Zimmermann]{This card sets a new base cost for a room. If you also have another card that sets a new base cost (e.g.\ \cardref{Carpenter}{Zimmermann}{E218}), you may only use one such card at the same time.} \ecp{If you build more than one room, you can choose the same or a different card for each room.}
\item \ecp{After you've used the Axe, you may then also use any card that changes the cost of a room (e.g.\ \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36}, \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91}, \cardref{Stonecutter}{Steinschneider}{E211}, and \cardref{Wood Carver}{Schnitzer}{K301}).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Baker's Oven}{Backofen}{E14}{(3VP. Return 1 oven.)}
{Whenever you use \changed[the ``Bake bread'']{a bread baking} action, you can use the Baker's Oven to convert up to 2 grain into 5 food each. When you play this card, you can also \changed[take the ``Bake bread'' action]{bake bread immediately}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The old oven is returned: the \cardref{Clay Oven}{Lehmofen}{A5} and \cardref{Stone Oven}{Steinofen}{A6} are returned to the major improvements, the \cardref{Wood-fired Oven}{Holzofen}{E27} is removed from the game.}
\item \ecp{Is both an oven and a baking improvement.}
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you may bake bread with all of your ovens and other suitable improvements.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Baking Tray}{Backtrog}{E15}{(Cost 1W.)}
{The \cardref{Clay Oven}{Lehmofen}{A5} and \cardref{Stone Oven}{Steinofen}{A6} are minor improvements for you. The Clay Oven, Stone Oven and \cardref{Wood-fired Oven}{Holzofen}{E27} cost you 1 building resource (of your choice) less.}

\card{Building Material}{Baumaterial}{E16}{}
{You receive either 1 wood or 1 clay when you play this card. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17}{(2VP. Cost 3W 1S.)}
{At any time, you can convert grain to 2 food (without having to bake bread).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Using the Windmill does not count as baking.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3651107]{The grain that you want to convert into 2 food may not be on fields; it must be taken from your personal supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}{(1VP. Req 2 occ.)}
{When you sow, you can plant vegetables on this card as though it were a field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Does not count as a field when scoring.} \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/482652]{Vegetables on this card do count for the score at the end of the game.}
\item \apx{When you sow on the Bean Field, you may use the \cardref{Potato Dibber}{Kartoffelstecher}{E32}, \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}, and \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} to plant extra vegetables.}% Contradicted by the Smallholder entry in the appendix.
\item If you have vegetable markers on the Bean Field, it counts as a prerequisite for the \cardref{Herb Garden}{Krðutergarten}{K130} and the \cardref{Strawberry Patch}{Erdbeerbeet}{I69}.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3183411]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow on the Bean Field.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Gypsy's Crock}{Dreibeinkessel}{E19}{(1VP. Cost 2C.)}
{Whenever you convert any 2 goods to food at one time using a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4} or \cardref{Cooking Corner}{Kochecke}{I85}, you receive 1 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you convert 4 goods at once, you receive 2 additional food; for 6 goods, 3 additional food, etc.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=653.0]{Goods includes animals.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/333169]{Baking bread counts as converting goods to food.}
\item \ecp{Is also activated if you convert two different types of goods, or use two different improvements at the same time. You may bake 1 bread and convert 1 other good at the same time; this also activates the Gypsy's Crock.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Simple Fireplace}{Einfache Feuerstelle}{E20}{(1VP. Cost 1C.)}
{At any time, you may convert goods to food as follows: vegetable $\rightarrow$ 2 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 1 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 2 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 3 food. Whenever you use \changed[the ``Bake Bread'']{a bread baking} action, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=683.0]{The Simple Fireplace counts as a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}; for example, it can be upgraded to a \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}, and playing the Simple Fireplace activates the \cardref{Charcoal Burner}{K—hler}{E182}.}
\item \apx[2nd]{Is removed from the game when upgraded to a Cooking Hearth.}
\item \apx{You can own more than one Fireplace.}
\item \ecp{With this card, you can convert several animals and vegetables to food at the same time. When you bake bread you can convert as many grain as you want. You may bake bread and convert other goods to food at the same time, in order to activate the \cardref{Gypsy's Crock}{Dreibeinkessel}{E19}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) This card never counts as a major improvement.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Half-timbered House}{Fachwerkhaus}{E21}{(Cost 1W 1C 1R 2S.)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each room in your stone house.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{In total, you receive 3 points instead of 2 per room.}
\item \apx{If you do not renovate to a stone house, or if you have also played the \cardref{Mansion}{Villa}{K144}, there is no advantage.}
\item The Half-timbered House's bonus points are in addition to the extra points from the \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Raft}{FloÔ}{E22}{(1VP. Cost 2W.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, you receive an additional 1 food or 1 reed.}

\card{Manger}{Futtertrog}{E23}{(Cost 2W.)}
{At the end of the game, if your pastures occupy 6/7/8/9+ farmyard spaces, you receive 1/2/3/4 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The deciding factor is the number of fenced spaces in the farmyard. It is irrelevant how many pastures there are.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Pen}{Gehege}{E24}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 4 occ.)}
{Place 2 food on each remaining round space. At the start of each round, you receive the food.}

\card{Spices}{Gew■rze}{E25}{}
{Whenever you convert vegetables to food using a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4} or \cardref{Cooking Corner}{Kochecke}{I85}, you receive 1 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you convert several vegetables to food at the same time, you receive 1 food for each vegetable.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/561224]{Is not activated when you use a \cardref{Cookhouse}{Kochnische}{M013/014}, \cardref{Open Grill}{Grillplatz}{M028}, or any other improvement, or when you convert vegetables to 1 food without an improvement.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Plane}{Hobel}{E26}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you turn 1 wood into food using the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, \cardref{Sawmill}{Holzmanufaktur}{K122} or \cardref{Cabinetmaker}{Tischler}{I258}, you receive 1 additional food. You can choose instead to turn a second wood into exactly 2 food.}

\card{Wood-fired Oven}{Holzofen}{E27}{(2VP. Cost 3W 1S.)}
{Whenever you use \changed[the ``Bake bread'']{a bread baking} action, you can use the Wood-fired Oven to turn any number of grain into 3 food each. When you play this card, you can also \changed[take the ``Bake bread'' action]{bake bread immediately}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you may bake bread with all of your ovens and other suitable improvements.}
\item \apx[Baker's Oven]{Is an oven.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clogs}{Holzpantoffel}{E28}{(Cost 1W.)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for a clay hut, or 2 bonus points for a stone house.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{This card is worth 2 points even if you receive bonus points for the \cardref{Half-timbered House}{Fachwerkhaus}{E21} or the \cardref{Mansion}{Villa}{K144}.}
\item \apx{If you have the \cardref{Chief's Daughter}{Hðuptlingstochter}{E173} as well, you get points for both cards.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Shepherd's Pipe}{Hornfl—te}{E29}{(Req 1 sheep.)}
{You can hold up to 2 additional sheep in each of the pastures where you keep sheep. You can keep up to 2 sheep in each unfenced stable.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you also have the \cardref{Stablemaster}{Stallmeister}{E208}, the Shepherd's Pipe has no effect on the unfenced stable for which the Stablemaster is used,} \ecp{but it still affects your other unfenced stables.}
\item \ecp{Also increases the capacity of the \cardref{Animal Yard}{Tierhof}{E58} and the \cardref{Wildlife Reserve}{Tiergarten}{I102}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Canoe}{Kanu}{E30}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, you receive an additional 1 food and 1 reed.}

\card{Carp Pond}{Karpfenteich}{E31}{(1VP. Req 2 impr 1 occ.)}
{Place 1 food on each remaining odd-numbered round space. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Only improvements and occupations that are open in front of you count.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Potato Dibber}{Kartoffelstecher}{E32}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you sow fields with vegetables, place 1 additional vegetable \changed{from the general supply} on each \changed[field that you Sow]{newly sown stack of vegetables}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Additional vegetables are also placed on \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} and \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ceramics}{Keramik}{E33}{(Cost 1C. Req 1 oven.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 2 food. From now, the \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8} is a minor improvement for you and costs you nothing.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/430620]{You still have to take a minor improvement action to take the Pottery. You cannot take the Pottery if another player already has taken it.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/497755]{The Pottery still counts as major improvement as well, e.g.\ for \cardref{Nosebag}{-}{M022} or \cardref{Administration}{-}{M070}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Basket}{Korb}{E34}{(Cost 1R.)}
{Whenever you use a person's action to take wood \changed{that is on an action space}, you can leave 2 of \changed{that} wood on the action space and receive 3 food in exchange.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/334611]{If you also have the \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, you can use both cards to leave 3 wood to receive 5 food.}% See also http://www.meinvz.net/Forum/ThreadMessages/34b2193c2307016d/3cc544cef137cbed
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2743417]{You may use this card only once per action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/451697]{You can use an action space with only 2 wood on it, and only take 3 food (and no wood). This still counts as taking wood, and activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Berry Picker}{Beerensammler}{E152}, \cardref{Wood Cart}{Holzfuhre}{I79}, and \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}.}
\item \ecp{If there is less than 2 wood on the action space, for example because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}, you may not use the Basket; not even if you receive additional wood from e.g. the Wood Cart.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Corn Scoop}{Kornschaufel}{E35}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} \changed{action space}, you receive 1 additional grain.}

\card{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36}{(1VP. Req 1 occ.)}
{You can replace 1 or 2 reed with the same amount of clay whenever you extend or renovate your home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{When building a room, you may choose to use 1 reeds and 1 clay instead of the 2 reeds required.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/405790]{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Clay Roof for the same action. These cards may even affect the clay cost introduced by the Clay Roof; e.g. with Clay Roof and \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272} you can add a room to your wooden hut for 6 wood.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Supports}{Lehmstake}{E37}{(Cost 2W.)}
{Whenever you add a room to your clay hut, you can pay 2 clay, 1 wood and 1 reed instead of 5 clay and 2 reed.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/324084]{If you build more than one room at the same time, you may use the Clay Supports for all of the rooms, or, alternatively,} \apx{you may build some rooms for 5 clay \& 2 reeds and other rooms for 2 clay, 1 wood, and 1 reeds.}
\item \apx{This card sets a new base cost for a room. If you also have another card that sets a new base cost (e.g.\ \cardref{Clay Plasterer}{Lehmdecker}{I241} or \cardref{Carpenter}{Zimmermann}{E218}), you may only use one such card at the same time.} \ecp{If you build more than one room, you can choose the same or a different card for each room.}
\item \ecp{After you've used the Carpenter, you may then also use any card that changes the cost of a room (e.g.\ \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36}, \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91}, and \cardref{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243}).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}{(2VP. Return 2 impr.)}
{The Madonna Statue has no effect.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You must discard 2 improvements that are on the table in front of you. You may not discard cards from your hand.}
\item \cardtext{It is irrelevant whether you discard major or minor improvements.}
\item If a discarded improvement would have given you something (resources, food, etc.) in a later round, you lose that claim.\comment{Added in pimp-box}
\item \ecp{If you discard a major improvement, it is returned to the major improvements board. If you discard a minor improvement, it is removed from the game.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Market Stall}{Marktstand}{E39}{(Cost 1 grain.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 1 vegetable. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The grain that you pay to play this card may not come from a field.
\item \apx{Activates the \cardref{Market Woman}{Marktfrau}{K292} when played, but not the \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}.}
\item \apx{You may not play this card without grain in your personal supply --- not even in combination with the Market Woman.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mini Pasture}{Miniweide}{E40}{(Cost 2F.)}
{When you play this card, immediately fence one space in your farmyard. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You do not need to pay wood for the fences.}
\item \apx{Activates the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207} and \cardref{Animal Breeder}{Tierz■chter}{K307} when played.}
\item \ecp{The space must be unfenced before playing this card. It may contain a stable.}
\item \ecp{You must follow the usual rules for building fences: if you already have pastures,} \apx{the new pasture must border an existing one.} \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/392399]{If you build more fences this turn, e.g.\ with the Hedge Keeper, you only check at the end of your turn if the pastures are legal.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Millstone}{M■hlstein}{E41}{(Cost 1S.)}
{Whenever you bake 1 or more grain into bread, you receive 2 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{With the \cardref{Baker}{Bðcker}{E150}, you receive at most 2 additional food from the Millstone in each harvest.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use a baking improvement (with the ``baking'' symbol) to convert grain to food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/382609]{Is not activated if you use the \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} action space, but don't bake.}
\item \apx[Brotverkðufer]{Bread is not baked if schnaps is distilled or beer is brewed, or when a \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17} or \cardref{Hand Mill}{Handm■hle}{I75} is used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Helpful Neighbours}{Nachbarschaftshilfe}{E42}{(Cost 1W or 1C.)}
{When you play this card, you receive either 1 stone or 1 reeds. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}

\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Fruit Tree}{Obstbaum}{E43}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}

\card{Outhouse}{Plumpsklo}{E44}{(2VP. Cost 1W 1C.)}
{The Outhouse has no effect. You can only build it if at least one other player has fewer than 2 occupations.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item It is irrelevant how many occupations you have played \changed{yourself}.
\item \ecp{In a 1-player game, you can only build the Outhouse if you have fewer than 2 occupations yourself.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/519235]{The Academic counts as 2 occupations.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}
{On this card, you can plant vegetables as you would on a field. Vegetables on this field can be converted to 4 food when harvested.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Does not count as a field when scoring.} \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/482652]{Vegetables on this card do count for the score at the end of the game.}
\item \apx{To receive the 4 food for the harvested vegetable, you have to convert the vegetable to food immediately after harvesting.} \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=962]{You don't need a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2} or \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4} to do this.}
\item \apx[R■benacker]{When you sow on the Lettuce Patch, you may use the \cardref{Potato Dibber}{Kartoffelstecher}{E32}, \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}, and \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} to plant extra vegetables.}% Contradicted by the Smallholder entry in the appendix
\item \apx[R■benacker]{If you have vegetable markers on the Lettuce Patch, it counts as a prerequisite for the \cardref{Herb Garden}{Krðutergarten}{K130} and the \cardref{Strawberry Patch}{Erdbeerbeet}{I69}.}
\item \ecp{Using the Lettuce Patch to convert a vegetable to food does not activate the \cardref{Spices}{Gew■rze}{E25}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3183411]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow on the Lettuce Patch.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reed Pond}{Schilfteich}{E48}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}
{Place 1 reed each on the next 3 \changed{remaining} round spaces. At the start of each round, you receive the reed.}

\card{Writing Desk}{Schreibpult}{E49}{(1VP. Cost 1W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you take an ``occupation'' action \changed{on an action space}, you may play 2 occupations one after another. The second occupation costs you 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You pay the normal cost for the first occupation.}
\item \apx[B■cherregal]{If you also have the \cardref{Bookshelf}{B■cherregal}{K112} and/or the \cardref{Patron}{Mðzen}{E192}, you receive food for both occupations that you play.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you use the ``1 occupation or family growth'' action space in the 5-player game, and you choose the family growth.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1853]{Is not activated when you don't use an action space to play an occupation (e.g.\ using the \cardref{Scholar}{Gelehrter}{K279} or \cardref{Puppeteer}{Puppenspieler}{I249}).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Builder's Trowel}{Spachtel}{E50}{(Cost 1W.)}
{You can renovate your wooden hut to a clay hut at any time without using a ``Renovate'' action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \changed{You must still pay for the renovation.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/337102]{You cannot renovate in the middle of an action, e.g. to use the clay received in an action to renovate to a clay hut, in order to profit from an improvement such as the \cardref{Stump-Jump Plough}{Australischer Springpflug}{Z313} in the same turn.}
\item \ecp{You may not use both the \cardref{Conservator}{Restaurator}{E200} and the Builder's Trowel to renovate your wooden hut to a stone house out of turn.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Butter Churn}{Stampfbutterfass}{E53}{(Cost 2W.)}

{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} \changed{action space}, you receive an additional 3 stone.}

\card{Stone House Extension}{Steinhausanbau}{E55}{(Cost 1R 3S.)}
{When you play this card, immediately extend your stone house by 1 room. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{The new room is free. You only have to pay the costs of this minor improvement.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{Cards that change the costs of minor improvements, such as \cardref{Golden Hands}{Goldene Hðnde}{\v{C}13}, can be used to change the cost of the Stone House Extension. Cards that change the costs of a new room, such as \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91} or \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272}, cannot be used to change its cost.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{Playing the Stone House Extension counts as building a room, and activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Animal Yard}{Tierhof}{E58}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 1 occ.)}
{\changed{This card can hold} up to two animals of your choice. They need not be the same type of animal.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Does not count as a pasture for scoring.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/334857]{You do not receive animals from the general supply when you play this card.}% See also http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331174
\item \ecp{The capacity of the Animal Yard is increased by the \cardref{Drinking Trough}{Trðnke}{E59}.}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Shepherd's Pipe}{Hornfl—te}{E29}, you can keep 4 sheep or up to 3 sheep and 1 other animal on the Animal Yard.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Drinking Trough}{Trðnke}{E59}{(1VP. Cost 2W.)}
{Each pasture (with or without a stable) can hold up to 2 more animals.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Does not increase the capacity of an unfenced stable.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/556122]{For pastures with stables, the capacity increase from the Drinking Trough is not doubled by the stables; a pasture of 1 farmyard space that contains a stable can hold 6 animals with the Drinking Trough.}
\item \ecp{Also increases the capacity of the \cardref{Animal Yard}{Tierhof}{E58} and the \cardref{Wildlife Reserve}{Tiergarten}{I102}.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Riding Plough}{Wagenpflug}{E61}{(Cost 4W. Req 3 occ.)}
{Twice during the game, when you use either the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} or \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} \changed{action space}, you can plough 3 fields instead of 1.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may choose to plough only 2 fields instead of 3 at once.}
\item \apx{You can place two field tiles on this card when you play it, to show that you may use the plough 2 times.}
\item \apx{This is a plough. Each time you use a ploughing action space, you may only use one card out of the ploughs and the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Turnwrest Plough}{Wendepflug}{E62}{(Cost 3W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Once during the game, when you use either the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} or \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} \changed{action space}, you can plough 3 fields instead of 1.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may choose to plough only 2 fields instead of 3 at once.}
\item \apx{You can place 1 field tile on this card when you play it, to show that you may use the plough 1 more time.}
\item \apx{This is a plough. Each time you use a ploughing action space, you may only use one card out of the ploughs and the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Moldboard Plough}{Abstechpflug}{I63}{(Cost 2W. Req 1 occ.)}

{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Is not activated when you use the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action space.}

\item This is a plough. Each time you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} action space, you may only use one card out of the ploughs and the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}.

\card{Alms}{Almosen}{I64}{(Req no occ.)}
