\card{Baker's Kitchen}{Backstube}{I65}{(4VP. Cost 2S. Return oven.)}
{Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you can use the Baker's Kitchen to convert up to 2 grain into 5 food each. When you play this card, you can also \changed{bake bread immediately}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is a baking improvement, but not an oven.} \apx{It may not be upgraded to a \cardref{Bakehouse}{Backhaus}{K106}.}
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you may bake bread with all of your ovens and other suitable improvements.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Village Well}{Dorfbrunnen}{I66}{(5VP. Return Well.)}
{Place 1 food each on the next 3 remaining round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10} major improvement is returned to the major improvements board and may be bought again --- even by the owner of the Village Well.}
\item \apx{The Well gives 1 food per round for 5 rounds. These food remain on the board even when the 3 additional food from the Village Well are distributed, and are distributed again if the Well is purchased a second time.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Threshing Board}{Dreschschlitten}{I67}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} or \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} \changed{action spaces}, you can \changed{additionally bake bread}.}

\card{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}{(Cost 2W.)}
{Once during the game, when you use either the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} or the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} \changed{action space}, you can plough 2 fields instead of 1. Each other player can also do this once during the game, but must pay you 2 food to do it.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Other players that use the Harrow may only plough 2 fields at once if they use one of the ploughing action spaces.}
\item \apx{The Harrow may not be combined with any of the ploughs.}
\item \apx{You may not deny other players the right to use the Harrow.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Strawberry Patch}{Erdbeerbeet}{I69}{(2VP. Req 2 veg fields.)}
{Place 1 food on each of the next 3 round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Vegetable fields are fields on which there is at least 1 vegetable marker. An empty, harvested field does not count as a vegetable field.}
\item \apx{The \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}, and \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} count as prerequisites for the Strawberry Patch, if there are vegetable markers on those cards.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Seed Trader}{Saatguthðndler}{Z332}, \cardref{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184}, \cardref{Giant Pumpkin}{Riesenk■rbis}{Z323} and \cardref{Pumpkin Seed Oil}{K■rbiskern—l}{Z319} do not count as prerequisites.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Punner}{Erdstampfer}{I70}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever another player uses the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68} or a plough, you can immediately plough 1 field as well.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you use the Harrow or a plough yourself, you do not get any advantage.}
\item \apx{If the other player does not plough more than 1 field on his action, you do not receive a field.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Holiday House}{Ferienh■tte}{I71}{(8VP. Cost 3W or 3C, 2R.)}
{In round 14, you cannot place any \changed{people}. Play this card at the latest during round 13.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The effects of this card are not optional! Prepare to play two harvests in a row.}
\item \apx{This costs either 3 wood \& 2 reeds or 3 clay \& 2 reeds.}
\item \apx{You may not use the \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36}, \cardref{Brushwood Roof}{Reisigdach}{K136} or \cardref{Straw-thatched Roof}{Strohdach}{I99} when building the Holiday House.}
\item \apx{You do not participate in the work phase (phase 3) in round 14, but you still can profit from the start-of-round phase (phase 1).}
\item \ecp{You may not place a guest in round 14 that you could otherwise have used.}
\item You do not get points for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227} if you have built the Holiday House.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Goose Pond}{Gðnseteich}{I72}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}
{Place 1 food each on the next 4 remaining round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.}

\card{Guest}{Gast}{I73}{(Cost 2F.)}
{When you play this card, you receive a guest token, which you may place once in the next round as you would a person. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{To represent the guest, you take a claim marker and turn it over to show the word ``Guest''. The token is used as a family member disc.}
\item \apx{If you already have 5 family members, you can use the guest to play a round with 6 actions.}
\item \apx{A guest is not counted in checking whether there is enough room in the hut or house.}
\item \cardtext{The action performed by a guest counts for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}.}\comment{Cardtext of Church Warden.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/410238]{The guest does not need to be fed during harvest time.}
\item \ecp{A guest does not count as family member in the final scoring, even if you use the guest in the last round.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\item \ecp{You can play this card in round 14, but you cannot use the guest marker you receive and it does not count in scoring.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Grain Cart}{Getreidefuhre}{I74}{(Cost 2W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} action space, you receive 2 additional grain.}

\card{Hand Mill}{Handm■hle}{I75}{(Cost 1S.)}
{During the feeding phase of the harvest, you can use the Hand Mill to turn either 1 grain into 2 food or 2 grain into 4 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Using the Hand Mill does not count as baking.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3651107]{The grain that you want to convert into food may not be on fields; it must be taken from your personal supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Rake}{Harke}{I76}{(Cost 1W.)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 2 bonus points if you have at least 5 fields. If you have played the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}, \cardref{Punner}{Erdstampfer}{I70}, \cardref{Yoke}{Joch}{K124} or a plough, you need to have at least 6 fields.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Fields on cards, such as \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18} and \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, do not count. Fields with more than one stack of grain because of the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324} count as only 1 field.}% Same as Village Farmer.
\item \apx[2nd ed]{If you also played a plough, \ecp{Harrow, Punner, or Yoke,} but you discarded it for the \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}, they do not count for the Rake.}
\item \ecp{If you played more than one of the listed improvements, you still need only 6 fields.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Shepherd's Crook}{Hirtenstab}{I77}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you fence a new pasture that covers at least 4 farmyard spaces, \changed{you receive} 2 sheep and place them in the new pasture.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you divide a pasture of more than 4 spaces into several smaller pastures, these do not count as a new pasture,} \ecp{unless the number of pastures of at least 4 spaces increases.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3829726]{If you fence 2 large pastures in one action, you receive 4 sheep.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 1 occ.)}
{When you sow, you can plant wood on this card. \changed{There can be up to 2 stacks of wood on this card, as shown.} The wood is treated the same as sown grain and is harvested during the field phase.\comment{Changed text in pimp-box}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The Copse does not count as a field when scoring.
\item \apx{If you receive for example 4 grain on your fields when sowing, you can also receive 4 wood once or twice on the Copse card.}
\item \apx[Kleinbauer]{The \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} may not be used to plant extra wood.}
\item \apx[English ed.]{In each harvest, you take one wood from each of the stacks.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3183411]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow wood on the Copse.}
\item \ecp{Wood on this card does not count for the \cardref{Storehouse Clerk}{Lagerhalter}{K287}. At the end of the game, it does count for the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7} or the \cardref{Sawmill}{Holzmanufaktur}{K122}.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=453]{The Copse is not considered to be adjacent to any farmyard space or other card, regardless of its location, and does not benefit from the \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wood Cart}{Holzfuhre}{I79}{(Cost 3W. Req 3 occ.)}
{Whenever you use a person to take wood that is on an action space, you receive 2 additional wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Is not activated when you use the \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} action space in the 5-player game.}
\item \ecp{If you use an action space that contains wood, and you leave all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, you still receive the wood from the Wood Cart, but (if you have more than one of those cards) you cannot leave wood received from the Wood Cart on the action space to use another of those cards.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Spinney}{Holzgarten}{I80}{(1VP. Cost 1W. Req 3 occ.)}
{Whenever another player uses the \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood} action space, they must give you one of the wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Is not activated when someone uses the \actionref{4 Wood}{4XWood} action space in the 5-player game.
\item \apx{When you demand the 1 wood from another player, the other player is entitled to change his mind and select a different action instead --- it is easy to overlook the Spinney.}
\item \ecp[http://www.trictrac.net/jeux/forum/viewtopic.php?t=57027]{You only get 1 wood, regardless of the amount of wood currently on the action space.}
\item \ecp{The Spinney is activated before the other player's \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, or any player's \cardref{Wood Buyer}{Holzaufkðufer}{I234}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wooden Hut Extension}{Holzh■ttenanbau}{I81}{(Cost 1R 5W.)}
{When you play this card, immediately extend your wooden hut by 1 room. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{The new room is free. You only have to pay the costs of this minor improvement.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{Cards that change the costs of minor improvements, such as \cardref{Golden Hands}{Goldene Hðnde}{\v{C}13}, can be used to change the cost of the Wooden Hut Extension. Cards that change the costs of a new room, such as \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91} or \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272}, cannot be used to change its cost.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{Playing the Wooden Hut Extension counts as building a room, and activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{When using the \actionref{Family Growth and Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement} action space, it is not possible to build this improvement first, and then use the new room to grow your family in.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wooden Crane}{Holzkran}{I82}{(1VP. Cost 3W.)}
{Whenever you use one of the \actionref{1 Stone}{1XStone} action spaces that are placed in \changed{rounds 5--7 and 10--11}, you receive 1 additional stone. If you pay 1 food, you can take 2 \changed{additional} stone instead of 1.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Is not activated when you use any other action space to take stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wooden Path}{Holzweg}{I83}{(Cost 1W.)}
{The player with the most valuable street receives 2 bonus points when scoring.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The \cardref{Paved Road}{Pflasterauffahrt}{I94} is more valuable than the \cardref{Clay Path}{Lehmzufahrt}{I89}, which is more valuable than this Wooden Path.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3795478]{Even if the other streets have also been played, only one bonus of 2 points is be awarded per game (not 2 bonus points per played street).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Chicken Coop}{H■hnerstall}{I84}{(1VP. Cost 2W or 2C, 1R.)}
{Place 1 food each on the next 8 remaining round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{May be built with either 2 wood \& 1 reeds or with 2 clay \& 1 reeds.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cooking Corner}{Kochecke}{I85}{(3VP. Return 1 cooking hearth.)}
{At any time, you may convert goods to food as follows: vegetables $\rightarrow$ 4 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 2 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 3 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 4 food. Whenever you use \changed{a bread baking action}, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you upgrade the \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4} major improvement, the card is returned to the major improvements board. If the minor improvement \cardref{Cooking{ }Hearth}{Kochstelle}{K128} is upgraded, it is removed from the game.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}{(1VP. Cost 2W or 2C, 2R.)}
{Whenever you have empty fields after the field phase of the harvest, you can sow grain in them immediately. Place 1 fewer grain from the supply on these fields.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Is built with either 2 wood \& 2 reeds or 2 clay \& 2 reeds.}% Changed for new edition; used to be 1 reed. http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3913801
\item \apx{Is used during the harvest at the same time as the \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103} and before the \cardref{Harvest Helper}{Erntehelfer}{I223}.}
\item \apx[Feldarbeiter]{Activates the \cardref{Field Worker}{Feldarbeiter}{I224} when used.}
\item \ecp{The effect of the Corn Storehouse is optional. You may choose to sow fewer fields than you're able to sow.}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1095]{You may use the Corn Storehouse to sow on the \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105}, but not on fields for other goods than wood (e.g.\ \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} and \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}).}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2176]{Activates the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324} when used, but not the \cardref{Scythe}{-}{G103}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Flagon}{Krug}{I87}{(Cost 1C.)}
{Whenever the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10} is built or upgraded to a \cardref{Village Well}{Dorfbrunnen}{I66}, you receive 4 food, and the other players receive 1 food each. If the Well has already been built, everyone receives the food when the Flagon is played.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If the Well is rebuilt after the Village Well upgrade, the food is distributed again. If the Village Well is already on the table when the Flagon is played, the food is not distributed in double quantities. If both the Village Well and the Well are on the table when the Flagon is played, the double amount of food is distributed immediately.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Lasso}{Lasso}{I88}{(Cost 1R.)}
{You can place exactly two people immediately after one another, if at least one of them uses the \actionref{1 Wild Boar}{1XWildXBoar}, \actionref{1 Cattle}{1XCattle} or \actionref{1 Sheep}{1XSheep} action space.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Is not activated when you use the \actionref{Sheep, Wild Boar, or Cattle}{SheepXXWildXBoarXXorXCattle} action space in the 5-player game.}
\item \apx{If you place 2 people the first time it's your turn in the work phase, you may play your third person the second time; you do not have to skip a turn.}
\item \apx[English ed.]{You cannot place more than two people immediately after one another turn with the Lasso.}
\item \apx{If you have 4 or more people, you may use the Lasso more than once in the same round.}
\item \ecp{You can use the animal action space with your first or second family member.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/364805]{When you play this card, you can immediately use it to place another family member on one of the three animal action spaces.}
\item \ecp{Using the Lasso counts as two turns.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Path}{Lehmzufahrt}{I89}{(1VP. Cost 3 C.)}
{The player with the most valuable street receives 2 bonus points when scoring.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The \cardref{Paved Road}{Pflasterauffahrt}{I94} is more valuable than this Clay Path, which is more valuable than the \cardref{Wooden Path}{Holzweg}{I83}.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3795478]{Even if the other streets have also been played, only one bonus of 2 points is be awarded per game (not 2 bonus points per played street).}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/364139]{The bonus points are in addition to the 1 normal point you get for playing this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}{(Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you sow, each of the fields you sow that is orthogonally adjacent to a room in your home gets \changed[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368508]{additional goods from the general supply: 2 extra grain on grain fields, and 1 extra vegetable on vegetable fields}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Not optional; you must plant the extra grain and vegetables.}
\item \apx{When a room is built next to a field that has already been sown, you do not get additional goods until the next time you sow the field.}
\item \ecp{If a field contains 2 stacks because of the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324}, both stacks get an extra grain.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=453]{Minor improvements are never adjacent to a farmyard space, unless the minor improvement itself contains farmyard spaces (e.g.\ \cardref{Moor Enclosures}{-}{M124}). Improvements such as \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} and \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} do not benefit from the Planter Box, not even from an improvement that is used as a room (e.g.\ \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138}).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91}{(Cost 2W.)}
{You need 1 less reed to extend or renovate your home or to build the \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Half-timbered House}{Fachwerkhaus}{E21}, \cardref{Chicken Coop}{H■hnerstall}{I84}, \cardref{Holiday House}{Ferienh■tte}{I71}, \cardref{Mansion}{Villa}{K144}, or \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Ladder for the same action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3456758]{The Ladder has no effect if the number of reeds required is already lowered to 0, e.g.\ by using both \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36} and \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272} when building a new room.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Manure}{Mist}{I92}{(Req 2 animals.)}
{At the end of each round that does not end with a harvest, you can take 1 grain or vegetable from each of your fields and place it in your personal supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The effect of the Manure is optional, but if you harvest, you must harvest all of your fields.}
\item \apx{You have a field phase (harvest phase 1) after each round, except that outside a regular harvest the \cardref{Milking Shed}{Molkerei}{I93}, \cardref{Spindle}{Spinnrocken}{E51}, \cardref{Butter Churn}{Stampfbutterfass}{E53}, \cardref{Milking Stool}{Melkschemel}{K133}, \cardref{Loom}{Webstuhl}{K146}, \ecp{and \cardref{Milking Hand}{Melker}{I246}} do not earn any additional food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/451271]{Using the Manure activates the \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}, \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103} (only for you), and \cardref{Gardener}{Gðrtner}{I226}, but not the \cardref{Cube Cutter}{W■rfelschnitzer}{Z335}.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=728.0]{Improvements, such as the \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120} and \cardref{Horse}{Pferd}{K135}, do not count as animals for the requirement to play this card.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/337775]{You also harvest the \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, and \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Milking Shed}{Molkerei}{I93}{(2VP. Cost 3S 2C.)}
{In each harvest, at the beginning of the field phase, count the total number of sheep and cattle in all the players' farms. You receive 1 food for each fifth sheep and for each third cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The total number of sheep and cattle is counted.\comment{added in pimp-box}
\item \apx{Pets and live animals on improvement cards also counted.} \ecp{Animals on the \cardref{Tanner}{Gerber}{K280} and the \cardref{Taxidermist}{Prðparator}{Z330} do not count.}
\item \apx{At harvest time, the Milking Shed is processed before the \cardref{Spindle}{Spinnrocken}{E51}, \cardref{Butter Churn}{Stampfbutterfass}{E53}, \cardref{Milking Stool}{Melkschemel}{K133} and \cardref{Loom}{Webstuhl}{K146}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Paved Road}{Pflasterauffahrt}{I94}{(2VP. Cost 5S.)}
{The player with the most valuable street receives 2 Bonus points when scoring.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This Paved Road is more valuable than the \cardref{Clay Path}{Lehmzufahrt}{I89}, which is more valuable than the \cardref{Wooden Path}{Holzweg}{I83}.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3795478]{This card always scores 2 bonus points. Even if the other streets have also been played, only one bonus of 2 points is be awarded per game (not 2 bonus points per played street).}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/364139]{The bonus points are in addition to the 2 normal points you get for playing this card.}% see also http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=649
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fish Trap}{Reuse}{I95}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space or receive reed on an action space, you receive 1 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which reed is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no reed (e.g.\ when you have the \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}.)}
\item \ecp{Is activated by the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take reed.}
\item \ecp{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood} in 4-player games.}
\item \apx{Is not activated when you play the \cardref{Reed Exchange}{Schilftausch}{I96} or \cardref{Helpful Neighbours}{Nachbarschaftshilfe}{E42}, or use the \cardref{Reed Buyer}{Schilfaufkðufer}{I251}, \cardref{Reed Collector}{Schilfsammler}{E205},} \ecp{or any other occupation or improvement to get reed.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you use the \cardref{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248} to collect the food from the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reed Exchange}{Schilftausch}{I96}{(Cost 2W or 2C.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 2 reeds. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may not exchange 1 wood or 1 clay for only 1 reed, or exchange 1 wood and 1 clay for 2 reeds.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=684.0]{Playing the Reed Exchange does not activate the \cardref{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Slaughterhouse}{Schlachthof}{I97}{(2VP. Cost 2S 2C.)}
{Whenever another player \changed{converts} 1 or more animals to food, you receive 1 food from the supply. During the feeding phase of the harvest, you are the last player to take a turn.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you convert an animal yourself, you receive no advantage.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368106]{If both the Slaughterhouse and the \cardref{Slaughterman}{Schlachter}{K299} are on the table, the owners of these two cards feed their families in current turn order (which is the turn order of the next round).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Schnaps Distillery}{Schnapsbrennerei}{I98}{(2VP. Cost 1 veg 2S.)}
{During the feeding phase of the harvest, you can use the Schnaps Distillery to convert at most 1 vegetable into 4 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point each for your 5th and 6th vegetables.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The vegetable that is used to buy the Schnaps Distillery and vegetables that you want to convert into 4 food may not be on fields; they must be taken from your personal supply.}
\item \ecp{Distilling schnaps does not count as baking and does not activate the \cardref{Spices}{Gew■rze}{E25}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Straw-thatched Roof}{Strohdach}{I99}{(1VP. Req 3 grain fields.)}
{You no longer need reed when you extend or renovate your home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Grain fields are fields or improvement cards on which there is at least 1 grain marker. An empty, harvested field does not count as a grain field.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Straw-thatched Roof for the same action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Tavern}{Taverne}{I100}{(2VP. Cost 2W 2S.)}
{The Tavern is an additional action space. Whenever another player uses it, they receive 3 food. Whenever you use it, you can choose either to take 3 food or to score 2 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If another player uses the Tavern, you yourself do not receive anything from it.}
\item \apx{As on every other action space, at most one person may use the Tavern in each round.}
\item \apx{If you take this action yourself and you choose the bonus points, write them on the scoring pad.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461716]{The Tavern counts as played improvement, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Village Elder}{Dorfðltester}{I221} or as prerequisite for the \cardref{Carp Pond}{Karpfenteich}{E31}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Feed}{Tierfutter}{I101}{(Req 4 planted fields.)}
{Immediately before scoring, you receive 1 additional animal of each type that you already have.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This does not apply to the \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120} and the \cardref{Horse}{Pferd}{K135} minor improvement.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/481793]{(\MOOR) It does apply to horses (that are not minor improvements).}
\item \apx{For the prerequisites, it does not matter whether the fields are planted with grain or vegetables.}
\item \apx{The \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}, and \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} count as prerequisites for the Animal Feed, if there are vegetable markers on those cards.} \ecp{The \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} counts for the number of fields planted on it.}
\item \apx{The \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, \ecp{\cardref{Giant Pumpkin}{Riesenk■rbis}{Z323}, and \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}} do not count as prerequisites.}
\item \apx{You may return animals to the general supply in order to make room for the new arrivals.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=769.0]{As the game is over at this point, you may not convert the new animal to food, for example to pay for the \cardref{Hide Farmer}{Hufenbauer}{I236}.}
\item \ecp{If you also have played the \cardref{Tenant Farmer}{Viehpðchter}{E215}, Animal Feed is used before returning the borrowed animals.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wildlife Reserve}{Tiergarten}{I102}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 2 occ.)}
{This card can hold up to 1 sheep, 1 wild boar and 1 cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Does not count as a pasture when scoring.}
\item \ecp{The capacity of the Wildlife Reserve is increased by the \cardref{Shepherd's Pipe}{Hornfl—te}{E29} and the \cardref{Drinking Trough}{Trðnke}{E59}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}{(2VP. Cost 1W 2C 1R 2S.)}
{After the field phase of a harvest, each player can use the Water Mill to convert up to 1 grain to 3 food. Each player that uses the Water Mill must give you 1 of the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Using the Water Mill does not count as baking.}
\item \ecp{You may use the Water Mill yourself for free.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3651107]{The grain that is to be converted into 3 food may not be on fields; it must be taken from the player's personal supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Weekly Market}{Wochenmarkt}{I104}{(Cost 3 grain.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 2 vegetables. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The grain that you pay for the vegetables may not come from a field.}
\item \apx{Activates the \cardref{Market Woman}{Marktfrau}{K292} when played, but not the \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105}{(Req 1 occ.)}
{When you sow, you can plant grain on this card. \changed{There can be up to 2 stacks of grain on this card, as shown.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This card does not count as a field when scoring.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3100898]{The Acreage counts as 2 fields towards prerequisites of minor improvements.}
\item \apx[Ackermann]{You may choose to only sow one grain field on this card.} \ecp{You may then in a later sowing action sow another grain here.}
\item \ecp{In each harvest, you take one grain from each of the stacks.}
\item \apx{If you receive 4 grain on fields when sowing because of occupations such as \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219} and \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}, you also receive 4 grain in each stack on the Acreage.}% Contradicted by appendix on Smallholder, but confirmed by card art for Acreage
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3183411]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow on the Acreage.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=453]{The Acreage is not considered to be adjacent to any farmyard space or other card, regardless of its location, and does not benefit from the \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bakehouse}{Backhaus}{K106}{(5VP. Cost 3S. Return 1 oven.)}
{Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you can use the Bakehouse to convert up to 2 grain into 5 food each. When you play this card, you can also \changed{bake bread immediately}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The old oven is returned: the \cardref{Clay Oven}{Lehmofen}{A5} and \cardref{Stone Oven}{Steinofen}{A6} are returned to the major improvements, the \cardref{Wood-fired Oven}{Holzofen}{E27} and \cardref{Baker's Oven}{Backofen}{E14} are removed from the game. The \cardref{Baker's Kitchen}{Backstube}{I65} may not be upgraded to a Bakehouse.}
\item \ecp{Is a baking improvement, but not an oven.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you may bake bread with all of your ovens and other suitable improvements.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Lumber}{Bauholz}{K107}{(Cost 1S.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 3 wood. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Beehive}{Bienenstock}{K108}{(1VP. Req 2 impr 3 occ.)}
{Place 2 food on each remaining even-numbered round space. At the start of these rounds, you \changed{receive} the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Only the improvements and occupations that lie open in front of you count.} \ecp{Discarded improvements (because of upgrading or \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}) do not count.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Spit Roast}{BratspieÔ}{K109}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you convert at least 1 animal to food during the feeding phase of the harvest, you receive 1 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You get a maximum of 1 food per harvest.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Brewery}{Brauerei}{K110}{(2VP. Costs 2 grain 2S.)}
{During the feeding phase of the harvest, you can use the Brewery to convert at most 1 grain to 3 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for your ninth grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The grain that is used to buy the Brewery and grain that you want to convert into 3 food may not be on fields; they must be taken from your personal supply.
\item Brewing beer does not count as baking.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bread Paddle}{Brotschieber}{K111}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you play an occupation, you may also \changed{bake bread}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Puppeteer}{Puppenspieler}{I249} or \cardref{Educator}{Ausbilder}{K271}.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{When you play more than one occupation in one action, you can bake bread more than once too.}
\item \apx[2nd]{You can also bake bread if you play an occupation during the turn of another player.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=831.0]{You may not use the food from the baking to pay for the occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bookshelf}{B■cherregal}{K112}{(1VP. Cost 1W. Req 3 occ.)}
{Whenever you play 1 occupation, you receive 3 food before you pay the costs of the occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you also have the \cardref{Patron}{Mðzen}{E192}, you can use both to receive 5 food for each occupation you play.}
\item \apx{When used with the \cardref{Writing Desk}{Schreibpult}{E49} to play two occupation cards, the additional 3 food is distributed twice.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Flail}{Dreschflegel}{K113}{(Cost 1W. Req 1 occ.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} or \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} \changed{action spaces}, you can \changed{additionally bake bread}.}

\card{Duck Pond}{Ententeich}{K114}{(1VP. Req 2 occ.)}
{Place 1 food on each of the next 3 round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.}

\card{Swing Plough}{Furchenpflug}{K115}{(Cost 3W. Req 3 occ.)}
{Twice during the game, when you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} \changed{action space}, you can plough 3 fields instead of 1.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Is not activated when you use the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action space.}
\item \apx{You may choose to plough only 2 fields instead of 3 at once.}
\item \apx{You can place two field tiles on this card when you play it, to show that you may use the plough 2 times.}
\item \apx{This is a plough. Each time you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} action space, you may only use one card out of the ploughs and the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Granary}{Getreidespeicher}{K116}{(1VP. Cost 3W or 3C.)}
{Place 1 grain on \changed[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1621]{each remaining space} for rounds 8, 10 and 12. At the start of these rounds, you receive the grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may not build the Granary with 2 wood \& 1 clay or with 1 wood \& 2 clay.}
\item \apx{Taking the grain does not activate the \cardref{Grain Cart}{Getreidefuhre}{I74}, \cardref{Corn Scoop}{Kornschaufel}{E35}, \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}, \cardref{Sycophant}{Getreideschmuser}{I229}, \cardref{Seed Seller}{Samenhðndler}{K296}, \cardref{Greengrocer}{Gem■sehðndler}{E168}, \cardref{Market Crier}{Marktschreier}{I245} or \cardref{Field Watchman}{Feldh■ter}{I225}.}
\item \cardtext{You do not receive grain for the current round, or any of the earlier rounds.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Greenhouse}{Gewðchshaus}{K117}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 1 occ.)}
{Add 4 and 7 to \changed{the number of} the current round and place 1 vegetable on each corresponding round space. At the start of these rounds, you can pay 1 food to take the vegetable.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you do not wish to pay the 1 food to buy the vegetables, the vegetable is returned to the general supply.}
\item \ecp{Food that you receive at the start of a round (e.g. because of the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10}) can be used to pay for the vegetable immediately.}% Compare Scholar
\item \ecp{You must pay the food before you take the vegetable.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}{(Req 4 animals.)}
{Whenever you sow, place 1 additional grain or vegetable from the general supply on \changed{each new stack you sow}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Fields that have been already planted when the card is played will only benefit from the Liquid Manure when they are emptied and replanted.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368508]{You can only put an extra grain on grain fields, and an extra vegetable on vegetable fields.}
\item \apx{You also place extra grain or vegetables when using the \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}.}
\item \apx{The additional grain or vegetable from the Liquid Manure is added to additional goods from the \cardref{Potato Dibber}{Kartoffelstecher}{E32}, \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}, \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219} and \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}.}
\item \apx{You also place extra grain or vegetables on the \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} and \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}.}
\item \apx[Holzacker]{If you plant wood on the \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} \ecp{or \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}}, you place 1 additional wood for each wood you plant.} \ecp{You also plant additional food on the \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=728.0]{Improvements, such as the \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120} and \cardref{Horse}{Pferd}{K135}, do not count as animals for the requirement to play this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Crooked Plough}{Hakenpflug}{K119}{(Cost 3W. Req 1 occ.)}
{Once during the game, when you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} \changed{action space}, you can plough 3 fields instead of 1.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Is not activated when you use the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action space. }
\item \apx{You may choose to plough only 2 fields instead of 3 at once.}
\item \apx{You can place 1 field tile on this card when you play it, to show that the plough may be used 1 more time.}
\item This is a plough. Each time you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} action space, you may only use one card out of the ploughs and the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120}{(1VP.)}
{In each feeding phase, you receive 1 food. Apart from the goat, you cannot hold any other animal in your home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you have the House Goat, the \cardref{Animal Tamer}{Tierzðhmer}{K306} has no effect.}
\item \apx{The goat may not be discarded in order to make room for a different animal.}
\item \apx{You may place 1 food on this card for each remaining harvest, to ensure that you do not forget to take the food.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=728.0]{The House Goat does not count as an animal, e.g.\ for prerequisites of minor improvements.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=470]{If you already have played the \cardref{Sheepdog}{-}{G108}, you cannot play the House Goat, and vice versa.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sawhorse}{Holzbock}{K121}{(Cost 2W.)}
{The next stable you place in your farmyard, as well as your 3rd, 6th, 9th, 12th and 15th fence, costs you nothing.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you build free fences in another way (e.g. with the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}) you may not save the free fences from the Sawhorse for another turn.} \ecp{Free fences from the Sawhorse are built before the free fences from the Hedge Keeper.}
\item \cardtext{Fences may only be built to form completed pastures.}\comment{Added in pimp-box}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sawmill}{Holzmanufaktur}{K122}{(3VP. Return Joinery.)}
{Each harvest, you may convert up to 1 wood to 3 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1/2/3 bonus points for 2/4/5 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{After the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7} has been upgraded, it may be bought again by any player.}
\item \cardtext{If you have both the Sawmill and the Joinery at the end of the game, you do not get any bonus points for wood from the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7},} \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/442277]{even if you have more wood than you need to receive maximum bonus points for the Sawmill. You do get the regular points for both cards: 2 for the Joinery, 3 for the Sawmill.}
\item \ecp{At the end of the game, wood on the \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} and the \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278} counts. Wood on the \cardref{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273} and \cardref{Resource Seller}{Werkstoffhðndler}{K310} does not count.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wooden Strongbox}{Holzschatulle}{K123}{(Cost 1W.)}
{At the end of the game, you get 2 bonus points if your home contains 5 rooms, or 4 bonus points if you have 6 or more rooms.}

\card{Yoke}{Joch}{K124}{(Cost 1W. Req 1 cattle.)}
{When you play this card, you can immediately plough 1 field for each plough or \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68} that has been played by any player.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may choose to plough fewer fields.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/513651]{If a plough or Harrow has been discarded, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}, it does not count.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Broom}{Kehrbesen}{K125}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Discard all the remaining minor improvements in your hand, and draw 7 new minor improvements. You can play 1 more minor improvement immediately.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You must pay the costs of the new improvement and, where appropriate, meet the conditions for playing it.}
\item \apx{If the players are only playing with the complex (K) deck of cards, the new cards are also drawn from the complex deck.} \ecp{If a specific mix of cards from several decks was dealt at the start of the game, use the same mix when drawing the replacement cards.}
\item \ecp{The improvements are drawn from the cards that were removed from the game at the start. This does not include cards that were discarded during the game, e.g. for upgrades or to play the \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Landing Net}{Kescher}{K126}{(Cost 1R.)}
{Whenever you receive reed on an action space, you receive an additional 2 food. This is reduced to 1 food if you receive other building resources as well as reed.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which reed is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no reed (e.g.\ when you have the \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}.)}
\item \ecp{Is activated by the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take reed.}
\item \cardtext{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood} in 4-player games, but you receive only 1 food.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you receive reed because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\item \apx{If the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} placed wood on the \actionref{1 Reed}{1XReed} action space, that space only provides 1 additional food.}
\item \ecp{Food is reduced when you receive other resources through improvements or occupations.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Other building resources are wood, clay, and stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you use \changed{one of the family growth action spaces} (or if you already have \changed{used one of these spaces in this round} when you play the Clapper), place 1 additional grain on all of your fields that already contains at least 1 grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Take the grain from the general supply.}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=900]{If there is more than one stack of grain on a field, on the \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} or because of the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324}, you place 1 grain on each of the stacks.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you use the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}, \cardref{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325}, or \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291}.}
\item \ecp{If you use the \cardref{Mother of Twins}{Zwillingsmutter}{Z336} for the same action, you still only get 1 additional grain per field.}
\item \ecp{In the 5-player game, there is an action space that gives players a choice of actions, including family growth. From round 5 onwards, the Clapper is activated by using this space, even if you choose the other action.}
\item \ecp{Also place additional wood on the \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} or the \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, and additional food on the \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}.}
\item \ecp{Using the Clapper does not count as sowing.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cooking{ }Hearth}{Kochstelle}{K128}{(1VP. Return 1 fireplace.)}
{At any time, you can convert goods to food as follows: vegetables $\rightarrow$ 3 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 2 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 3 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 4 food. Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you upgrade the \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2} major improvement, the card is returned to the major improvements board. If the minor improvement \cardref{Simple Fireplace}{Einfache Feuerstelle}{E20} is upgraded, it is removed from the game.}
\item \apx{You can own more than one Cooking Hearth.}
\item \ecp{With this card, you can convert several animals and vegetables to food at the same time. When you bake bread you can convert as many grain as you want. You may bake bread and convert other goods to food at the same time, in order to activate the \cardref{Gypsy's Crock}{Dreibeinkessel}{E19}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/459110]{Is identical in all respects to the major improvement \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}, except that it can be played as a minor improvement, and that it cannot be paid for with clay.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{(\MOOR) After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Corn Sheaf}{Korngarbe}{K129}{}
{When you play this card, \changed{you receive} 1 grain. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Herb Garden}{Krðutergarten}{K130}{(1VP. Req 1 veg field.)}
{Place 1 food on each of the next 5 round spaces. At the start of each round, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Vegetable fields are fields on which there is at least 1 vegetable marker. An empty, harvested field does not count as a vegetable field.}
\item \apx{The \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}, and \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} count as prerequisites for the Strawberry Patch, if there are vegetable markers on those cards.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Seed Trader}{Saatguthðndler}{Z332}, \cardref{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184}, \cardref{Giant Pumpkin}{Riesenk■rbis}{Z323} and \cardref{Pumpkin Seed Oil}{K■rbiskern—l}{Z319} do not count as prerequisites.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Pit}{Lehmgrube}{K131}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, you receive 3 additional clay.}

\card{Clay Hut Extension}{Lehmh■ttenanbau}{K132}{(Cost 1R 4C.)}
{When you play this card, immediately extend your clay hut by 1 room. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{The new room is free. You only have to pay the costs of this minor improvement.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{Cards that change the costs of minor improvements, such as \cardref{Golden Hands}{Goldene Hðnde}{\v{C}13}, can be used to change the cost of the Clay Hut Extension. Cards that change the costs of a new room, such as \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91} or \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272}, cannot be used to change its cost.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{Playing the Clay Hut Extension counts as building a room, and activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Milking Stool}{Melkschemel}{K133}{(Cost 1W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you have cattle during the field phase of a harvest, you receive food: \changed{1 food if you have 1 or 2 cattle; 2 food if you have 3 or 4 cattle; 3 food if you have 5 or more cattle}. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for every 2 cattle.}

\card{Ox Team}{Ochsengespann}{K134}{(1VP. Cost 3W. Req 2 cattle.)}

{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may choose to plough fewer fields.}
\end{explanationlist}}
