\card{Horse}{Pferd}{K135}{}
{You receive 2 bonus points for any one type of animal missing from your farm at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you are missing several types of animal, you still only get 2 bonus points from the Horse, and you still receive 1 minus point for every missing type of animal.}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=963]{The score for the missing type of animal still counts as negative for the \cardref{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276} and \cardref{Yeoman Farmer}{Freibauer}{E165}.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=701.0]{The Horse does not need to be placed in the farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=728.0]{The Horse does not count as an animal for prerequisites of minor improvements.}
\item \ecp{(\MOOR) The Horse does not count as a horse, but horses can be the type of animal for which the Horse gives you points.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Brushwood Roof}{Reisigdach}{K136}{(Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you extend or renovate your home, you can replace 1 or 2 reed with the same amount of wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room.}
\item \apx{When building a room, you may choose to use 1 reeds and 1 wood instead of the 2 reeds required.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Brushwood Roof for the same action. For example, if you also have the \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36}, you may use both to replace 2 reeds with 1 wood and 1 clay.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}
{When you sow, you can plant vegetables on this card as you would on a field. When you play this card, you can also \changed{carry out a sowing action}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may use the sowing action for all of your empty fields.}
\item \cardtext{Does not count as a field when scoring.} \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/482652]{Vegetables on this card do count for the score at the end of the game.}
\item \apx{Whenever you sow on the Turnip Field, you may use the \cardref{Potato Dibber}{Kartoffelstecher}{E32}, \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}, and \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} to plant extra vegetables.}% Contradicted by the Smallholder entry in the appendix
\item If you have vegetable markers on the Turnip Field, it counts as a prerequisite for the \cardref{Herb Garden}{Krðutergarten}{K130} and the \cardref{Strawberry Patch}{Erdbeerbeet}{I69}.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3183411]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow on the Turnip Field.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138}{(1VP. Cost 4R 1W.)}
{Place one family member token that you have not yet brought into the game onto this card, where it will live for the rest of the game. It can take actions and must be fed, but it is not worth any points while living in the Reed Hut.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{The new person can be used in the current round, as it is put in ``its own room'' immediately when playing this card.}% http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=696.0
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=867.0]{The occupant of the Reed Hut is placed after your family members} \ecp{and the guest from the \cardref{Guest}{Gast}{I73} minor improvement, but before the guest received from the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}.}
\item \ecp{Playing the Reed Hut does not count as a family growth action.}
\item \apx{The person in the Reed Hut is not counted when checking if family growth is allowed. They do not count as part of the family.}
\item \cardtext{You can move this person into your home with a family growth action later.} \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=867.0]{That family growth action must be taken by another family member.} \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=963]{The former occupant of the Reed Hut counts as newborn, and may not take an action that round, unless you use the \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267}.}
\item \ecp{You can play this card even if you do not have a family member token left in your supply, but you don't get an extra person.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1887]{If you discard the Reed Hut because of the \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}, you must discard the occupant of the Reed Hut immediately if you haven't yet placed it this round. If you've already placed the occupant of the Reed Hut, discard it in the return home phase of this round.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sleeping Corner}{Schlafecke}{K139}{(1VP. Cost 1W. Req 2 grain fields.)}
{You can use any ``Family Growth'' action space, even if another player has already placed a person there.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{This works for all spaces that include a family growth action.}
\item \ecp{In the 5-player game, there is an action space that gives players a choice of actions, including family growth. From round 5 onwards, you may always use this space, even if you choose the other action.}
\item \apx{Grain fields are fields on which there is at least 1 grain marker. An empty, harvested field does not count as a grain field.} \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1830]{Fields with other resources or food, such as \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} and \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}, do not count.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} and fields on which a second grain has been planted using the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324} count for the number of grain planted on them.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2760626]{You cannot use the action space if it is occupied by one of your own family members.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Swan Lake}{Schwanensee}{K140}{(2VP. Req 4 occ.)}
{Place 1 food each on the next 5 remaining round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.}

\card{Boar Breeding}{Schweinezucht}{K141}{(Cost 1F.)}
{When you play this card, \changed{you receive} 1 wild boar. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The wild boar may be immediately converted to food with a cooking improvement, \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247} or \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Cart}{Steinkarre}{K142}{(Cost 2W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Place 1 stone on each remaining even-numbered round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the stone.}

\card{Stone Exchange}{Steintausch}{K143}{(Cost 2W or 2C.)}
{When you play this card, \changed{you receive} 2 stone. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may not exchange 1 wood or 1 clay for only 1 stone, or exchange 1 wood and 1 clay for 2 stone.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mansion}{Villa}{K144}{(Cost 3W 3C 2R 3S.)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 2 bonus points for each room in your stone house. In total, you receive 4 points per room instead of the usual 2 points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx[Fachwerkhaus]{If you also have the \cardref{Half-timbered House}{Fachwerkhaus}{E21}, you only get the bonus points from the Mansion.}
\item If you also have the \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172}, you get the bonus points for both cards.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Forest Pasture}{Waldweide}{K145}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}
{This card can hold an unlimited number of wild boar.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Does not count as a pasture when scoring.}
\item \apx{The wild boar on this card are included when scoring wild boar.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Loom}{Webstuhl}{K146}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever you have sheep during the field phase of a harvest, you receive food: \changed{1 food if you have 1 to 3 sheep; 2 food for 4 to 6 sheep; or 3 food for 7 or more sheep.} At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for every 3 sheep.}

\card{Clay Deposit}{Lehmh■gel}{I337}{(Req 3 occ.)}
{This card is an additional action space. A player who uses this action space must pay you 1 food and receives 5 clay. If you use the Clay Deposit yourself, you may choose to take 2 bonus points instead of the clay.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=740.0]{If you use the Clay Deposit yourself, you do not need to have or to pay any food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461716]{The Clay Deposit counts as played improvement, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Village Elder}{Dorfðltester}{I221} or as prerequisite for the \cardref{Carp Pond}{Karpfenteich}{E31}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Feed Pellets}{Kraftfutter}{E338}{}
{During the feeding phase of each harvest, you may trade 1 vegetable for 1 of any type of animal that you already have in your farmyard.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2744309]{You may use this card only once per harvest.}% see also http://www.trictrac.net/jeux/forum/viewtopic.php?t=53889
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pelts}{Tierfelle}{K339}{(Req 3 occ.)}
{For each animal that you \changed{convert to food} and return to the general supply, you may place 1 food from your personal supply in 1 of your rooms. You may have a maximum of 1 food in each room. You cannot use these food any more, but each is worth 1 bonus point at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You can take the food from your supply \emph{after} you've received the food from slaughtering the animal.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{If you also have the \cardref{Tanner}{Gerber}{K280}, \cardref{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273}, \ecp{\cardref{Taxidermist}{Prðparator}{Z330}, and/or \cardref{Brush Maker}{B■rstenbinder}{E156},} you may use those cards as well as the Pelts for each converted animal.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/300894
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stump-Jump Plough}{Australischer Springpflug}{Z313}{(Cost 2W.)}
{Once you live in a clay hut or stone house, whenever you use a \changed{person's} action to take wood you can pay 1 food to \changed{also} plow 1 field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{This is a plough.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which wood is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no wood (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}).}
\item \ecp{Is activated even if you leave all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space that contains wood because of the Wood Distributor.}
\item \ecp{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games, and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take wood.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you receive wood because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Once all the \changed{people} have been placed in this round, you may place a guest marker to carry out an additional action. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The guest is played after all family members, other guests, and the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138}, but before moving a person (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}).}
\item \ecp{The action performed by a guest counts for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/410238]{The guest does not need to be fed during harvest time.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/356298]{This card is passed to the left immediately when it has been played. The next player may use the Keg the same round.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/356298]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Brewer's Copper}{Braukessel}{Z315}{(1VP. Cost 1 grain 1S.)}
{During the feeding phase of each harvest, you can use the Brewer's Copper to convert at most 1 grain to 2 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point if you have at least 7 grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Using the Brewer's Copper does not count as baking.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bust}{B■ste}{Z316}{(2VP. Cost 1S.)}
{This card cannot be played once all other players have 2 or more occupations (3 occupations in a 3-player game, 4 occupations in a 2-player game).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{In a 1-player game, you can always play this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Family Portrait}{Familiengemðlde}{Z317}{}
{Pay 2 food for each of your family members, and receive \changed{a total of} 4 bonus points. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \changed{Write the bonus points on the scoring pad.}
\item \ecp{You do not have to pay for guests or the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Barbecue}{Grillfest}{Z318}{}
{When you play this card, you can convert as many animals to food as you have family members. For each sheep, you receive 3 food; for each wild boar, 4; and for each cattle, 5. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368280]{You do not need a cooking improvement to convert the animals to food.}
\item \ecp{Is not a cooking improvement. Does not activate the \cardref{Schnitzel Mallet}{Schnitzelklopfer}{ø18}.}
\item \ecp{Guests or the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} do not count as family members.}
\item \ecp[http://www.trictrac.net/jeux/forum/viewtopic.php?t=53936]{You may choose to convert fewer animals to food than you have family members.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pumpkin Seed Oil}{K■rbiskern—l}{Z319}{(Req 1 veg field.)}
{Three times during the game (but at most once per round), you can place 1 vegetable from your personal supply on this card and receive 3 food in exchange. The vegetables on this card are counted in the scoring at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You do not need a cooking improvement to exchange the vegetable for food.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2368]{A harvest counts as part of the preceding round.}
\item \ecp{Placing a vegetable on this card does not count as sowing.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/527606]{The vegetables on this card are not considered to be in your personal supply.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}, and \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} count as prerequisites for the Pumpkin Seed Oil, if there are vegetable markers on those cards.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Giant Pumpkin}{Riesenk■rbis}{Z323}, \cardref{Seed Trader}{Saatguthðndler}{Z332}, and \cardref{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184} do not count as prerequisites.}
\item \ecp{Placing a vegetable on this card does not activate the \cardref{Spices}{Gew■rze}{E25}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Maypole}{Maibaum}{Z320}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Play this card before the end of round 4. When you play this card, place one of your unbuilt fences upright on an unused farmyard space. If you have not knocked it over by the end of the game, it is worth 2 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The farmyard space counts as used, even if the fence is knocked over, \ecp{in which case, it remains on the farmyard space. You cannot reclaim it for use as a fence.}
\item \ecp{The farmyard space cannot be used for anything else until the end of the game. In the scoring at the end of the game, the farmyard space counts as used, even if the fence has been knocked over.}
\item If another player knocks the fence over, you can re-place it.
\item \ecp{Placing the Maypole does not count as building fences.}
\item \ecp{You cannot play this card after round 4, or after you've built all of your fences.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ranch}{Ranch}{Z321}{(Req no unused spaces.)}
{For each round that has not yet begun when you play this card, you receive 1 bonus point and 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Write down the bonus point(s) on the scoring pad immediately.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Dozing Bull}{Randalierender Bulle}{Z322}{}
{As long as you have at least 1 cattle in your farm, you can knock down your fences and rebuild them at any time, for no cost.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Your animals do not run away.}
\item \cardtext{Fences must always be placed according to the rules.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2840062]{Rebuilding fences does not activate the \cardref{Animal Breeder}{Tierz■chter}{K307},} \ecp{\cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}, and \cardref{Shepherd's Crook}{Hirtenstab}{I77}, or another player's \cardref{Fencer}{Zaunbauer}{I264}.}
\item \ecp{When you rebuild the fences, you must use the same number of fences. You may not remove fences from your farm.}
\item \ecp{You can only rearrange those fences that have been placed as fences; not those used by the \cardref{Wagenburg}{Wagenburg}{\v{C}16}, \cardref{Hop Field}{Hopfenfeld}{\v{C}18} or \cardref{Maypole}{Maibaum}{Z320}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Giant Pumpkin}{Riesenk■rbis}{Z323}{}
{Place 1 vegetable from your own supply on this card. At any time, you can harvest this vegetable and convert it to food. If it is still on the card at the end of the game, you receive 2 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can count the vegetable in scoring at the end of the game.}
\item \ecp{You have to place the vegetable immediately when you play the Giant Pumpkin; you cannot play this card if you do not have a vegetable.}
\item \ecp{You may not place another vegetable on this card after you have harvested the first.}
\item \ecp{When you harvest the vegetable, you have to convert it to food immediately. You may not add it to your supply or sow it.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/425630]{The Giant Pumpkin does not count as a field, and is not harvested during the field phase of a harvest. You cannot use the \cardref{Gardener}{Gðrtner}{I226} for the Giant Pumpkin.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324}{(Req 2 empty fields.)}
{Whenever you sow, you can pay 1 wood and sow 2 grain instead of 1 on an empty field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You can use this card once for every sowing action.}
\item \ecp{You may not sow an extra stack of grain on a field that is not empty.}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}, \cardref{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}, \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}, or \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}, you may add extra grain to both stacks when you sow. The field for which you use the Scarecrow counts as 2 fields for the Fieldsman and Smallholder.}
\item \ecp{In each harvest, you take one grain from each of the stacks.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}, and \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} count as prerequisites for the Scarecrow, if there are no vegetables on them. The \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} counts as two empty fields if there are no markers on it, and as one empty field if there is one field planted on it.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}, and \cardref{Giant Pumpkin}{Riesenk■rbis}{Z323} do not count as prerequisites.}
\item \ecp{You cannot use the Scarecrow to sow extra grain on the Acreage, or extra goods on the Copse, Forester, or Vineyard.}
\item \ecp{Fields that have two stacks of grain on them count as two fields for prerequisites. They count as 1 field during the final scoring.}
\item \ecp{When both stacks of grain have been completely harvested, you can only sow 1 grain on the field with your next sowing action, unless you use the Scarecrow again for that field.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Coffee House}{Kaffeehaus}{ø13}{(2VP. Cost 1W 1C 1S.)}
{The Coffee House is an action space for all players. Whenever a player uses the Coffee House, that player and the card's owner each receive 1 food from the general supply. In the next round, the person from this space can be placed before the starting player places his first person.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you use this card yourself, you receive 2 food.}
\item \ecp{The person from the Coffee House is placed before using the \cardref{Taster}{Vorkoster}{I260}. The taster still pays food to the original starting player.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461716]{The Coffee House counts as played improvement, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Village Elder}{Dorfðltester}{I221} or as prerequisite for the \cardref{Carp Pond}{Karpfenteich}{E31}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Spielefest}{Spielefest}{ø14}{(2VP. Cost 2W 3F. Req 3 occ.)}
{The Spielefest is an action space for all players. Whenever a player visits the Spielefest, he pays the owner of this card 1 food and receives 2 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can visit the Spielefest yourself.} \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=740.0]{If you do, you do not need to have or to pay any food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461716]{The Spielefest counts as played improvement, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Village Elder}{Dorfðltester}{I221} or as prerequisite for the \cardref{Carp Pond}{Karpfenteich}{E31}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Farmers' Ball}{Bauernball}{ø15}{(1VP. Req 3 occ.)}
{When this card is played, each player who immediately pays 5 food into the general supply receives 3 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Before paying 5 food, each player has the chance to convert goods to food.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Neutrality}{Neutralitðt}{ø16}{(Req 2 occ.)}
{In the next round, you can only place your people after the other players have placed all of theirs. For each person that you place late, you receive 1 bonus point.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you would have placed a number of your people after all other player's people anyway, e.g.\ because you are last in player order or because you have more family members than anyone else, you do not receive bonus points for them.}
\item \ecp{You place your people after all guests of other players, including the one from the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}, but before moving a person (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}).}% See Neutrality.
\item \ecp{You may not use the \cardref{Taster}{Vorkoster}{I260} next round. If you use the \cardref{Coffee House}{Kaffeehaus}{ø13} this round, you may not place that person first.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Guest Worker}{Gastarbeiter}{ø17}{(1VP. Req more rooms than people.)}
{Take a Guest marker. From the next round, you can place this as you would a family member. The guest worker can use the most recent round card even if it has already been taken. He occupies a room in your home and must be fed with 2 food during the feeding phase of each harvest.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The most recent round card is always the one corresponding to the current round, even if the \cardref{Chamberlain}{Kðmmerer}{I238} has been played.}
\item \ecp{The guest worker may also be placed on another available action space, but in that case it has to be unoccupied.}
\item \ecp{The guest worker does not count as a family member when scoring or for the \cardref{Ratcatcher}{Rattenfðnger}{E198}, \cardref{Midwife}{Hebamme}{I232}, \cardref{Barbecue}{Grillfest}{Z318}, or \cardref{Family Portrait}{Familiengemðlde}{Z317}, but its action does count for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}.}
\item \ecp{Playing the Guest Worker is not a family growth action.}
\item \ecp{The guest worker is placed as one of the ordinary family members, before the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} and the guest received from the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461716]{If the most recent round card is \actionref{1 Stone}{1XStone}, \actionref{1 Sheep}{1XSheep}, \actionref{1 Wild Boar}{1XWildXBoar}, or \actionref{1 Cattle}{1XCattle}, and there are no animals on the space because another player took them earlier in the round, you cannot use that action in this round.}% see also http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/425431
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Schnitzel Mallet}{Schnitzelklopfer}{ø18}{(1S. Req 2 occ.)}
{For each cattle that you turn to food using a cooking improvement, you receive 1 additional food and 1 bonus point.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{A cooking improvement is an improvement with a ``cooking'' symbol.}
\item \ecp{Is activated by using the \cardref{Horse Butcher}{-}{M087}, but not by \cardref{Barbecue}{Grillfest}{Z318}, \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}, or \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Compulsory Education}{Allgemeine Schulpflicht}{ø19}{(Req 1 occ.)}
{Whenever you have family growth, you can pay 1 food to immediately play an occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you can also play a minor improvement, you must first play the occupation.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}, \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291}, or \cardref{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Emergency Housing}{Notunterkunft}{ø20}{(Cost 1W 1R. Req 1 stable.)}
{Select 1 of your built stables. It is now a room for one of your family members. The stable loses its original function, but it is still worth 1 additional point if fenced.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2980594]{You can still keep animals in the pasture, as if the stable did not exist.}
\item \ecp{You may not build a second stable on that farmyard space.}
\item \ecp{Playing the Emergency Housing does not count as building a room and, for example, does not activate the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}.}
\item \ecp{The stable only counts as a room when you have family growth (including when you use the Wet Nurse or \cardref{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325}) or when you play the \cardref{Guest Worker}{Gastarbeiter}{ø17}. It does not count as a room when renovating, scoring, or for other improvements and occupations.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1S.)}
{Whenever you use the ``Sow'' action, you can plant up to 3 food on this card. Up to 3 \changed{stacks of} food may be planted on it in total. These food are \changed{treated in the same way as sowed grain} and are harvested during the harvest.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You place up to 3 food from your personal supply next to each other on this card, and pile additional food from the general supply on your own 1--3 food markers.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/485481]{You may choose to only sow 1 or 2 food on this card. You may then in a later sowing action sow more food here.}
\item \ecp{In each harvest, you take one food from each of the stacks.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3183411]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow food on the Vineyard.}
\item \cardtext{This card does not count as a field when scoring.}
\item \ecp{If you may place 4 grain on a field when sowing, e.g. with an occupation, you also receive 4 food on each stack on the Vineyard; if you would receive 5 grain, you receive 5 food. If you have the \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}, you get a total of 5 food on the card if you only plant 1 food on this card (and nothing elsewhere); if you plant 2 food (and nothing else), you receive 4 food on each stack.}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} may not be used to plant extra food.}
\item \ecp{At the end of the game, the food is not counted as grain.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=453]{The Vineyard is not considered to be adjacent to any farmyard space or other card, regardless of its location, and does not benefit from the \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Unusual Architecture}{Seltsame Architektur}{ø22}{(1VP. Cost 2C.)}
{Whenever you extend your home with 1 or more rooms, you receive 2 food for each new room.}

\card{Lederhosen}{Lederhose}{ø23}{(Req 3 occ.)}
{For each sheep that you convert to food, place 1 food from the general supply on this card. If, at the end of the game, you have at least as many food on the Lederhosen as you have family members, you receive 2 bonus points; if you have twice as many, you receive 3 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The food on the Lederhosen is not part of your supply. You cannot use it in any way.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Styrian Oak}{Steirische Eiche}{ø24}{(Req 1 occ.)}
{Place 5 food from the general supply on the Styrian Oak. At the start of each round, you can return 1 food to the general supply. Once during the game, at any time, you can pay the number of food (0 to 5) remaining on the Styrian Oak to receive 6 wood from the supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The food on the Styrian Oak is not part of your supply. You cannot use it in any way.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Golden Hands}{Goldene Hðnde}{\v{C}13}{(Cost 1F.)}
{Whenever you play a minor or major improvement, you can replace exactly 1 building resource with another.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reeds, and stone.} \ecp{You cannot replace anything else (food, grain, vegetables, animals, etc.).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{School}{Schule}{\v{C}14}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1C.)}
{Whenever you can play 1 minor or major improvement, you can play 1 occupation instead. The price of the occupation is 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You can also use the School for actions in which you can play only a minor improvement, such as the one on the \actionref{Family Growth and Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement} action space.}
\item \ecp{In combination with one of \cardref{Traveling Salesman}{Handelsreisender}{K281}, \cardref{Businessman}{Geschðftsmann}{I228}, or \cardref{Merchant}{Kaufmann}{E179}, you can use the School to play either two occupations, or one improvement and one occupation, in any order.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Beer Festival}{Bierfest}{\v{C}15}{(Cost 1F. Req 3 persons.)}
{You can bake bread immediately when you play this card. At the end of the game, you get 1 bonus point for every 3 food you have left, with a maximum of 3 points.}

\card{Wagenburg}{Wagenburg}{\v{C}16}{}
{You may place 1 fence on each of any number of your unused farmyard spaces. This costs 1 wood per fence. You may at any time return a fence from a farmyard space to your personal supply. Spaces with fences count as used at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you take fences back from your farm, you don't get your wood back.}
\item \ecp{Farmyard spaces with fences also count as used during the game, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Rancher}{Landmann}{I340}.}
\item \ecp{Placing the fences is not a fencing action, and does not activate the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}, or another player's \cardref{Fencer}{Zaunbauer}{I264}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Chapel}{Kapelle}{\v{C}17}{(1VP. Cost 2C.)}
{The Chapel is an additional action space. Whenever a player uses it, they can discard up to 2 begging cards. Every begging card is paid with 1 stone, which is placed on the Chapel. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each stone on this card.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The stone on this card is not part of your personal supply.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461716]{The Chapel counts as played improvement, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Village Elder}{Dorfðltester}{I221} or as prerequisite for the \cardref{Carp Pond}{Karpfenteich}{E31}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hop Field}{Hopfenfeld}{\v{C}18}{(Req 1 empty field.)}
{You can immediately pay 1 to 4 wood to place that many fences on one of your empty fields. This field is no longer suitable for sowing, but will be scored as a field at the end of the game. For each fence on the field you receive 1 food immediately and 1 bonus point at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You cannot return fences from the field to your supply.}
\item \ecp{Placing the fences is not a fencing action, and does not activate the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}, or another player's \cardref{Fencer}{Zaunbauer}{I264}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wine Cellar}{Weinkeller}{\v{C}19}{(1VP. Cost 2S. Req 1 unfenced stable.)}
{Immediately convert one of your unfenced stables to a wine cellar by turning it on its side. You can no longer keep animals in it. You receive 2 food from the general supply in the field phase of each harvest. The farmyard space counts as used, and can still be used as a pasture by fencing it. The wine cellar does not count as a stable.}

\card{Golem}{Golem}{\v{C}20}{(1VP. Cost 2C. Req oven or cooking hearth.)}
{Place the 2 clay that you paid on this card. At the start of each of the next 2 rounds, return 1 of the clay to the general supply. In these 2 rounds, you use the action space where you place your first person, twice in succession. For accumulating action spaces, this means that for the second action you receive the number of resources or food that is added at the start of each round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The clay on this card is not part of your personal supply.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/462794]{You use only one person to take the double action.}
\item \ecp{The person counts only once for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}.}
\item \ecp{Taking a double action is not optional. You may only use an action space that you are able to use twice. For example, you can only use the action space \actionref{Family Growth and Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement} with your first person in the next round if you have 2 empty rooms.}
\item \ecp{If you only pay 1 clay for the Golem because of another improvement or occupation, you can only take the double action once, and only in the next round. If you pay no clay, you cannot take any double action. If you pay another type of resource, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Golden Hands}{Goldene Hðnde}{\v{C}13}, you cannot use those resources to take a double action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Venus Figure}{Venus von Vestonice}{\v{C}21}{(Cost 2C.)}
{Whenever you use the action space \actionref{Family Growth and Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement}, you may carry out the family growth action twice in the same turn, using only 1 person.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This action space is revealed in round 5, 6, or 7.}
\item \cardtext{You may only play 1 minor improvement.}
\item \ecp{Taking the family growth action twice activates the \cardref{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127} only once, but \cardref{Midwife}{Hebamme}{I232}, \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267}, \cardref{Child Prodigy}{Wunderknabe}{ø12}, and \cardref{Compulsory Education}{Allgemeine Schulpflicht}{ø19} twice.}
\item \ecp{You can only use the \cardref{Farm Steward}{Hofverwalter}{I233} for the first family growth action.}
\item \ecp{You cannot use the Venus Figure on the action space \actionref{Family Growth without Room}{FamilyXGrowthXwithoutXRoom}, or \actionref{1 Occupation or Family Growth}{1XOccupationXorXFamilyXGrowth} in the 5-player game, or when you carry out family growth because of a card.}
\item \ecp{The person that takes the family growth action counts only once for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bible}{Bibel}{\v{C}22}{(1VP. Cost 1W. Req 1 occ.)}
{In the feeding phase of each harvest, each family member that has used one of the following action spaces in the preceding round consumes 1 fewer food: \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField}, \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow}, \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain}, \actionref{Take 1 Vegetable}{TakeX1XVegetable}, and \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer},
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Cook}{Koch}{E181}, it is possible that some of your family members do not consume food at all.}
\item \ecp{You can use this card to pay less food for the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} or the \cardref{Guest Worker}{Gastarbeiter}{ø17}, but you do not receive food if you take any of the actions with another guest.}
\item \ecp{You can only receive the discount once for each family member, even if they took one of the actions twice because of e.g.\ \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Golem}{Golem}{\v{C}20}.}
\item \ecp{If you use the Acrobat to move a person at the end of the round, you receive the discount for that person.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hunger Wall}{Hungermauer}{\v{C}23}{(Cost 3C.)}
{In the feeding phase of each harvest, each player can pay 1 clay instead of 2 food to feed exactly 1 family member. Each paid clay is placed on this card. You receive 1 bonus point for every 2 clay on this card at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The clay on this card is not part of your personal supply.}
\item \ecp{If a player has the \cardref{Bible}{Bibel}{\v{C}22}, and all their family members need only 1 food, they can still use the Hunger Wall, but only to replace just 1 food with 1 clay.}
\item \ecp{In the solo game, you can replace 3 food with 1 clay.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Five-year Plan}{F■nfjahresplan}{\v{C}24}{(Req 2 occ, 1 empty field.)}
{Place a claim marker on an empty field. You cannot sow again on this field. It no longer counts as a field, but only as a used farmyard space. You may immediately sow on all of your other empty fields. Put 2 extra grain or vegetables on each stack that you plant.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/filepage/48632]{You put extra grain on grain fields, and extra vegetables on vegetable fields.}
\item \ecp{The field with the claim marker does not count as a field during scoring.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Almanac}{-}{G061}{(Cost 1W 1S.)}
{When you play this card, immediately take the field and breeding phases of a harvest on your farmyard. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Activates all your cards that can be used during the field and breeding phases of a harvest.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103} (only for you), also if owned by another player.}
\item \ecp{Does not activate the \cardref{Layabout}{Lehnerich}{I244}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Farm}{-}{G062}{(Cost 1W. Req 2 animal types.)}
{Once per round, you may return 1 of your animals to the supply for a guest token, which you place this round as you would a family member. (The guest represents the animal.)
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You can use the Animal Farm at the latest when it's your next turn after the one in which you placed your last family member (including the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} and other guests except for the one from the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}).}
\item \ecp{If another player has the Robber, Animal Farm does not count as a person left to place, unless you already took the guest token.}
\item \ecp{You can exchange an animal that comes directly from an action space or from an improvement or occupation, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2185]{If you discard the Animal Farm with the \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38} before you've used the guest marker, you have to discard that guest marker without using it. If you've already placed the guest marker, it is discarded in the return home phase as usual.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Baking Field}{-}{G063}{(Req 2 occ \& 1 baking imp)}
{When you sow, you can plant grain on this card as you would on a field. When harvesting, you must immediately bake this field's harvested grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You receive a baking action that you can and must use for this grain only.}
\item \ecp{The grain still counts as harvested, e.g.\ for \cardref{Bountiful Harvest}{-}{G067} and \cardref{Grain Market}{-}{G078}.}
\item \ecp{Every grain that is moved from this field to your personal supply has to be baked, including when \cardref{Manure}{Mist}{I92}, \cardref{Almanac}{-}{G061}, \cardref{Harvest Feast}{-}{G080}, or \cardref{Fish Farm}{-}{G115} are used.}
\item \ecp{Grain moved elsewhere (e.g. to another player's supply by \cardref{Harvest Helper}{Erntehelfer}{I223}) cannot be baked immediately.}
\item \ecp{When you harvest more than 1 grain at the same time, e.g.\ with the Harvest Feast, you must bake all grain in 1 baking action.}
\item \ecp{If you cannot bake a grain, e.g.\ because you discarded your baking implement for the \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}, you must convert it to 1 food.}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Baker}{Bðcker}{E150}, you get two separate baking actions during the harvest; you may use the same baking implement for both.}
\item \cardtext{This card does not count as a field when scoring.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3100898]{It counts as a field towards prerequisites of minor improvements.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3183411]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow on the Baking Field.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=453]{The Baking Field is not considered to be adjacent to any farmyard space or other card, regardless of its location, and does not benefit from the \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bartering Hut}{-}{G064}{}
{When you play this card, immediately buy up to 2 animals from the general supply. Pay any 2 building resources for each sheep, any 3 for each wild boar, and any 4 for each cattle. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The animals can be the same or different.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals to food with an appropriate improvement without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Beehive Oven}{-}{G065}{(1VP. Cost 2S.)}
{Whenever you use \changed{a bread baking} action, you can use the Beehive Oven to convert up to 1 grain into 4 food. Whenever you bake 1 or more grain into bread without using the Beehive Oven, you receive 1 additional food. When you play this card, you can also \changed{bake bread immediately}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is both an oven and a baking improvement.}
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you may bake bread with all of your ovens and other suitable improvements.}
\item \apx[Brotverkðufer]{Bread is not baked if schnaps is distilled or beer is brewed, or when a \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17} or \cardref{Hand Mill}{Handm■hle}{I75} is used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Birthstone}{-}{G066}{}
{Whenever you grow your family, you may pay 1 stone for 1 bonus point. When you play Birthstone, you may immediately do this for any new family member that you already received this round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you receive 2 new family members at once with \cardref{Mother of Twins}{Zwillingsmutter}{Z336}, you may pay 2 stone for 2 bonus points.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bountiful Harvest}{-}{G067}{(Req 2 occ.)}
{If you harvest at least 2 resources and breed at least 1 animal during a harvest, place 1 food from the \changed{general} supply on this card. You may use this food at any time. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each food on this card.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Food on this card is part of your personal supply, and counts for e.g.\ \cardref{Pilgrim}{?}{G045}.}
\item \ecp{Is activated by \cardref{Almanac}{-}{G061}.}
\item \ecp{If you also have \cardref{Harvest Helper}{Erntehelfer}{I223}, grain harvested from another player's field counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Chronicle}{-}{G068}{(Cost 2W or 2C. Req 1 occ.)}
{Place 1 food on each remaining major improvement on the major improvements board. When these improvements are acquired, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{(\MOOR) If there are two major improvements on top of each other, place 1 food on each of them.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clear Cutting}{-}{G069}{(Cost 1W. Req 1 occ.)}
{Whenever you plough 1 or more fields, you receive 1 wood from the \changed{general} supply for each field you just ploughed.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{(\MOOR) Is not activated when you place a field without ploughing, e.g.\ using the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} special action, \cardref{Cattle Collar}{-}{M017}, or \cardref{Peat Burn-off}{-}{M016}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Corral}{-}{G070}{(Cost 3W. Req 1 occ.)}

{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The fields do not count as pastures.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cow Bell}{-}{G071}{(Cost 1C.)}

{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The spaces still count as unused.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Dunghill}{-}{G072}{(Cost 1W. Req 2 occ.)}

{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Animal cards like \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120} do not count, but animals kept on cards do.}

\card{Farmers Market}{-}{G075}{(Cost 2F.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 1 vegetable. \passing}

\card{Gardening Tools}{-}{G076}{(Cost 2W.)}
{Whenever another player sows, you may pay 1 food to the supply to immediately take a \changed[``Sow'']{sowing} action.}

\card{Gimlet}{-}{G077}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1C.)}
{Pay 1 less wood/clay/stone for each wood/clay/stone room. Each round you build stables, pay 1 less wood for up to 2 stables.}

{Whenever you harvest at least 1 grain, you may immediately afterward exchange 1 grain from your personal supply for 1 vegetable.}

\card{Hayloft}{-}{G081}{(Cost 1W.)}
{At the end of the game, you receive \changed[1/2 bonus points for 3/4 stables]{1 bonus point if you have 3 stables, or 2 bonus points if you have 4 stables}.

\card{Hired Helpers}{-}{G082}{(Cost 1F.)}
{Each round, you may place 1 guest token as you would a family member. If you do this, you must place 1 fewer person next round. You can not use this ability in consecutive rounds nor in round 14.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2170]{You can decide to use the Hired Helpers at the start of any of your turns, and at the latest when it's your next turn after the one in which you placed your last family member (including the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} and other guests except for the one from the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}).}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2170]{You have to place the guest token in the same turn that you receive it, unless you skip that turn (e.g. because of the \cardref{Robber}{Rðuber}{\v{C}11} or (\MOOR) because of a special action). If another player has the Robber, Hired Helpers does not count as a person left to place, unless you skipped a turn.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2170]{If you have a card that is activated by placing your last person or taking your last action, e.g.\ Magician or Opportunist, and you use that card when you place your last family member, you can no longer use the Hired Helpers that turn. You may choose not to use that card when you place your last family member, but then you have to use the Hired Helpers next turn (and it counts as a person left to place until then).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Holiday Present}{-}{G083}{(Cost 1W or 1C.)}
{When you play this card, immediately either discard 1 begging card or take 1 animal (of your choice) from the supply. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you take an animal, you may immediately convert it to food with an appropriate improvement without having to make room for it in your farmyard.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Horse Barn}{-}{G084}{(Req 1 occ.)}
{Whenever you sow, each field you sow that is orthogonally adjacent to exactly 1 stable gets an additional 1 grain or 1 vegetable. Each field that is orthogonally adjacent to 2 or more stables, gets an additional 2 grain or 2 vegetables.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{It does not matter if \changed[the]{a} stable is fenced.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368508]{You can only put extra grain on grain fields, and extra vegetables on vegetable fields.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=453]{Cards such as \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} and \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18} do not benefit from the Horse Barn.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=919]{If you also have the \cardref{Winter Garden}{-}{G118}, grain or vegetable fields inside your home do not benefit from the Horse Barn.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Irrigation Canal}{-}{G085}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1S.)}
{Whenever you plow a field that is orthogonally adjacent to a planted field, you may take 1 grain or vegetable from that field and sow it immediately on the newly plowed field. Place 1 fewer grain or vegetable from the supply on the newly planted field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2172]{If you use the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action space, you may sow before you plough.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2172]{If you plow more than 1 field at the same time (e.g.\ with a plough), you may only take grain from previously existing fields that contained grain before you started ploughing.}
\item \ecp{You get a single sowing action that you can only use for one grain or vegetable per ploughed field. This activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} and the \cardref{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}, but not the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324}.}
\item \ecp{Removing the grain or vegetable from the planted field does not count as a harvest.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Itinerant Laborers}{-}{G086}{(Cost 1F.)}
{When you play this card, immediately take a \changed[``Sow'']{sowing} action. \passing

\card{Magic Beans}{-}{G087}{(Cost 1 cattle.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 2 vegetables. \passing

\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Meat Pie}{-}{G088}{(1VP. Cost 2F or 1 animal.)}
{Whenever you bake 1 or more grain into bread, you may pay 1 additional
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item grain and 1 animal for 3 Bonus points. When you play this card, you may
\item also take \changed[the ``Bake bread'']{a bread baking} action.
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use a baking improvement (with the ``baking'' symbol) to convert grain to food.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=573]{You may only use this card once per baking action, regardless of how many grain you bake.}
\item \apx[Brotverkðufer]{Bread is not baked if schnaps is distilled or beer is brewed, or when a \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17} or \cardref{Hand Mill}{Handm■hle}{I75} is used.}

\card{Paddocks}{-}{G090}{(Req 1 pasture \& 1 occ.)}
{\ecp{You may not use the Paddocks to fence unfenced farmyard spaces.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{This is a fence building action, and activates \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, and \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pelt Roof}{-}{G091}{(Req 2 occ.)}
{For each wild boar, cattle, or 2 sheep you convert into food, you may place 1 reed from the general supply on this card. You may use this reed to extend or renovate your home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=432]{If you convert a single sheep into food, you don't receive any reed, not even if you already converted a single sheep earlier.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=432]{Reed on this card is not part of your personal supply. It does not count for \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9} or \cardref{Storehouse Clerk}{Lagerhalter}{K287}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2173]{You may not use the reed on this card to pay for the \cardref{Wooden Hut Extension}{Holzh■ttenanbau}{I81}, \cardref{Clay Hut Extension}{Lehmh■ttenanbau}{K132}, or \cardref{Stone House Extension}{Steinhausanbau}{E55}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=432]{If you also have the \cardref{Pelts}{Tierfelle}{K339}, \cardref{Tanner}{Gerber}{K280}, \cardref{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273}, \ecp{\cardref{Taxidermist}{Prðparator}{Z330}, and/or \cardref{Brush Maker}{B■rstenbinder}{E156},} you may use those cards as well as the Pelt Roof for each converted animal.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pine Forest}{-}{G092}{}
{At the start of each round, you may place 1 wood on this card if you have zero wood in your supply. When this card has 5 wood, move the wood from this card to your \changed{personal} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You may not give wood to the general supply for nothing,} \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/584170]{unless you also have the \cardref{Pilgrim}{?}{G045}.}
\item \ecp{If you receive wood at the start of the round, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Rancher}{Landmann}{I340} or \cardref{Private Forest}{Privatforst}{E45}, you may use the Pine Forest before you receive that wood.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=699]{You must take the wood as soon as there are 5 wood on the card; you may not wait until there is 6 or more wood on the card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Plentiful Fields}{-}{G093}{}
{When you play this card, you receive 1 food for each planted plowed field in your farmyard. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1960]{You do not receive any food for improvements with planted resources, such as \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18} and \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=728]{You receive only 1 food for a field with 2 stacks of grain because of the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Potter's Wheel}{-}{G094}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you convert 1 clay into food using the \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8} or \cardref{Potter}{T—pfer}{E214}, you receive 1 additional food. The Pottery is now a minor improvement for you.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/497755]{The Pottery still counts as major improvement as well, e.g.\ for \cardref{Nosebag}{-}{M022} or \cardref{Administration}{-}{M070}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Private Market}{-}{G095}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1C.)}
{Once per round, you may exchange 2 food for a building resource of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Private School}{-}{G096}{(1VP. Cost 3W or 3C. Req 1 occ.)}
{This card is an additional action space for all players. Any player who uses the Private School must pay you 1 food to play an occupation.  All players must still pay any additional costs for their occupation (for \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172}, \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291}, etc).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=740.0]{If you use the Private School yourself, you do not need to have or to pay any food.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pulley}{-}{G097}{(1VP. Cost 2W.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space you may immediately afterward build one room.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Pay costs for the room normally.} \ecp{You can use discounts from e.g.\ \cardref{Axe}{Axt}{E13} and \cardref{Thatcher}{Dachdecker}{E157}.}
\item \ecp{If you receive building resources for the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Quarry}{Steinbruch}{E54} or \cardref{Clay Pit}{Lehmgrube}{K131}, you can use these to pay for the room.}
\item \ecp{Activates \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}, \cardref{Building Tycoon}{Baul—we}{ø07}, and \cardref{Unusual Architecture}{Seltsame Architektur}{ø22}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2174]{If you also have the \cardref{Oldest Occupation}{?}{G042}, you may first use the Pulley to build a new room and then the Oldest Occupation to grow a family member there.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pumpkin Pie}{-}{G098}{(1VP. Cost 2 grain or 1 veg.)}
{Whenever you bake 1 or more grain into bread, you may pay 1 additional grain and 1 vegetable for 3 bonus points. When you play this card, you can also take \changed[the ``Bake bread'']{a bread baking} action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use a baking improvement (with the ``baking'' symbol) to convert grain to food.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=573]{You may only use this card once per baking action, regardless of how many grain you bake.}
\item \apx[Brotverkðufer]{Bread is not baked if schnaps is distilled or beer is brewed, or when a \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17} or \cardref{Hand Mill}{Handm■hle}{I75} is used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reed Beds}{-}{G099}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 1 occ.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} action space, you receive 1 reed.}

\card{Reed Sale}{-}{G100}{(Cost 1R.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 3 food. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Remodeling}{-}{G101}{(Cost 1W 1R. Req 1 stable)}
{When you play this card, immediately return a stable from your farmyard to your supply and extend your wooden hut by 1 room. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The room does not cost anything, but you must pay the cost shown on this card.}
\item \ecp{You can not use discounts on room building costs, e.g.\ from \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91} and \cardref{Thatcher}{Dachdecker}{E157}, when paying for this card.}
\item \ecp{You cannot remove a stable that is used for \cardref{Emergency Housing}{Notunterkunft}{ø20}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sausage Grinder}{-}{G102}{(1VP. Cost 2S.)}
{Whenever you convert animals into food, you receive 1 additional food for each animal.}

\card{Scythe}{-}{G103}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1S. Req 1 occ.)}
{You may sow fields even if they already contain resources.  Place the new resources on top of the existing ones. You cannot sow different resources on a single field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you receive extra resources when sowing, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} or \cardref{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}, you also receive them when you use the Scythe.}
\item \ecp{Is activated by any sowing action, including those from \cardref{Hobby Farmer}{Kleingðrtner}{E180} and \cardref{Five-year Plan}{F■nfjahresplan}{\v{C}24}, except sowing actions on empty fields only (e.g.\ \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}.}
\item \ecp{You may also use the Scythe on improvements like the \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105}, \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, and \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, and on the indoors field of \cardref{Winter Garden}{-}{G118}, and on the farmyard spaces used by \cardref{No-Till Farming}{-}{M078}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2176]{If you sow an empty field, you cannot use the Scythe on that same field in the same sowing action.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2176]{You cannot use the Scythe twice on the same field in the same sowing action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Seasonal Plants}{-}{G104.}{(Req 1 occ.)}
{Whenever you sow during an even-numbered round, add 1 additional resource of the appropriate type to 1 field you just sowed.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1499]{You may choose to sow an extra resource on cards like \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278} and \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Seed Spreader}{-}{G105}{(Cost 1W 1C.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} action space, you may immediately afterward sow 1 grain or 1 vegetable.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You get a single sowing action that you can only use for one grain or vegetable from your personal supply. This activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} and the \cardref{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}, but not the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Shared Wall}{-}{G106}{(Cost 1S. Req 2 occ.)}
{\ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=909]{Areas of one or more unused farmyard spaces that are completely surrounded by fences or rooms are now automatically pastures. You may not use them any longer for any other purpose.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you want, you can add fences of another colour where these pastures border your home, for clarity.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space is entirely surrounded by your home, it becomes a pasture as well, even though it is not connected to your other pastures. You may not create an unconnected pasture in any other way with this card.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2177]{The sides of your home do not count as fences (even when they help surround one of your pastures). If you create a pasture by placing a new room, this does not count as building fences, e.g.\ for \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}. It does count as fencing a new pasture for \cardref{Shepherd's Crook}{Hirtenstab}{I77} and \cardref{Animal Breeder}{Tierz■chter}{K307}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2177]{If Shared Wall is discarded with the \cardref{Madonna Statue}{Marienfigur}{E38}, incompletely fenced spaces are no longer pastures. Leave the fences on your farmyard; they have no effect.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sheep Market}{-}{G107}{(Cost 1W. Req 1 occ.)}
{At the beginning of each harvest, you may exchange 1 grain or vegetable for 1 sheep. Alternatively, you may exchange 1 sheep for 1 grain or vegetable.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated before the field phase of the harvest.}
\item \ecp{If you take a sheep, you may immediately convert it to food with an appropriate improvement without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sheepdog}{-}{G108}{(-)}
{You may keep up to 2 sheep on each unused space in your farmyard. You may not keep any animal other than sheep in your home. The Sheepdog must be fed 1 food each harvest.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The farmyard spaces where you keep the sheep still count as unused.}
\item \cardtext{If you don't have enough food to feed the Sheepdog, you have to take a begging card.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2178]{The food for the dog must be paid during the feeding phase of the harvest.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=470]{If you already have played the \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120}, you cannot play the Sheepdog, and vice versa.}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=728.0]{The Sheepdog does not count as an animal, e.g.\ for prerequisites of minor improvements.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sheepskin Rug}{-}{G109}{(Cost 1 sheep.)}
{At the end of the game, if you own a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, you receive 2 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{A \cardref{Simple Fireplace}{Einfache Feuerstelle}{E20} counts as a fireplace; a \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4} doesn't.}
\item \ecp{You only receive the bonus once, even if you have 2 fireplaces.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Shovel}{-}{G110}{(Cost 1W 1C.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, you may immediately afterward take \changed[the ``Sow'']{a sowing} action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1973]{If you receive resources on the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Seasonal Worker}{Saisonarbeiter}{E202} or \cardref{Undergardener}{Gartenarbeiter}{E166}, you may use these in the sowing action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sickle}{-}{G111}{(Cost 1W.)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 3 bonus points if you have at least 5 plowed fields, 8 grain and 4 vegetables.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Planted grain and vegetables count.}
\item \ecp{Improvements such as \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} and \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18} do not count as fields for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Crane}{-}{G112}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1S. Req 2 occ.)}
{Whenever another player builds a room or renovates, you may immediately perform this action yourself (without placing a family member). Pay the costs using 1 less building resource of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You cannot build a room when another player renovates, or vice versa.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2179]{If the other player builds multiple rooms, you may build up to that same number. The Stone Crane gives a discount on all of those rooms.}
\item \ecp{You can use cards like \cardref{Axe}{Axt}{E13} or \cardref{Renovator}{Renovator}{E199} to reduce the costs of the new room(s) or the renovation.}
\item \ecp{Is also activated when another player builds a room or renovates because of an improvement or occupation, such as \cardref{Wooden Hut Extension}{Holzh■ttenanbau}{I81}, \cardref{Master Builder}{Baumeister}{E151}, or \cardref{Builder's Trowel}{Spachtel}{E50}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2117]{If the other player does an additional action, e.g.\ builds a stable as well as a room, or plays an improvement as well as renovates, you cannot do that action as well.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Kitchen}{-}{G113}{(2VP. Cost 3S.)}
{At any time, you may convert goods to food as follows: vegetables $\rightarrow$ 4 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 2 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 3 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 4 food. Whenever you use \changed[the ``Bake bread'']{a bread baking} action, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{With this card, you can convert several animals and vegetables to food at the same time. When you bake bread you can convert as many grain as you want. You may bake bread and convert other goods to food at the same time, in order to activate the \cardref{Gypsy's Crock}{Dreibeinkessel}{E19}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stonecutter's Hall}{-}{G114}{(2VP. Cost 2S 3W or 2S 3C or 2S 3R.)}
{In each harvest, you can use the Stonecutter's Hall to convert \changed[at most]{exactly} 1 stone to 3 food. At the end of the game, you receive 1/2/3 bonus points for 2/4/5 stone.}

{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This also applies to field cards} \ruling{such as \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} and \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}.}
\item \ecp{You cannot take other resources, such as wood from \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} or \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}.}

\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Winter Garden}{-}{G118}{}
{You may sow 1 of your rooms as if it were 1 field. Whenever you have an animal in your home (including \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120}), move all resources planted in this room to the general supply. Harvest resources from your room as normal and additionally at the end of rounds 6, 8, 10 and 12.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The \cardref{Sheepdog}{-}{G108} does not count as an animal for this card.}
\item \ecp{You are allowed to sow in a room when you have an animal in your home, e.g.\ to use the \cardref{Serf}{Ackerfrohne}{K266}, but you lose the grain or vegetables immediately.}
\item \ecp{You cannot use the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324} when you sow in a room.}
\item \ecp{The field in your home does not count as a field for prerequisites of minor improvements or in scoring at the end of the game.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Cookhouse}{Kochnische}{M013/014}{(2VP. Cost 6C or return FP/CH.)}
{You can exchange goods for food at any time, as follows: vegetables $\rightarrow$ 3 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 2 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 3 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 4 food; horses $\rightarrow$ 2 food. Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 3 food.

\item Cannot be bought as long as it is covered by the \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}.

If the minor improvement \cardref{Simple Fireplace}{Einfache Feuerstelle}{E20} or \cardref{Cooking{ }Hearth}{Kochstelle}{K128} is upgraded, it is removed from the game.}
\item It is allowed to take the Cookhouse from a space on the major improvement board, and then return a Cooking Hearth to that same space.% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/472782
\item \ecp{You can own more than one Cookhouse.}
\item \ecp{When you bake bread you can convert as many grain with the Cookhouse as you want.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fallow Fields}{-}{M015}{}
{Place 2 food \changed{from the general supply} on each of up to 3 empty fields. You cannot harvest the food. You receive it when you sow in the fields.}

\card{Peat Burn-off}{-}{M016}{}
{You immediately receive 1 fuel. In addition you can (optionally) immediately exchange 1 moor tile for a field tile. \passing

\item \cardtext{If there is another tile under the moor tile, it is discarded with the moor.}
\item \ecp{Does not count as a ploughing action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/543284]{If you already have fields, you can only exchange a moor tile that borders an existing field.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
