\card{Cattle Collar}{-}{M017}{(1VP. Cost 1W. Not before round 8.)}
{Whenever you use the ''Plough Field'' action or the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} special action, you can immediately place 1 additional field tile on an empty farmyard space. To do this, you must have at least 1 cattle in your farm.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated on both the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} and the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action spaces, and when you plough a field using a card.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated by \cardref{Peat Burn-off}{-}{M016} or \cardref{Surveyor's Map}{-}{M018}.}
\item \ecp{You can only use this card once per turn to place 1 extra field, even if you plough several fields at once.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/477071]{You may use the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} action to create a field that does not border your other fields, as long as the extra field from the Cattle Collar connects all of your fields.}
\item \ecp{Placing the additional field does not count as ploughing.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Surveyor's Map}{-}{M018}{(Cost 3F. Not after round 2.)}
{Place a field tile on the space for round 11, a moor tile on round 12, and a forest tile on round 13. At the start of the rounds, you must either place the tile on an empty space in your farm or return it to the supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Placing the field tile does not count as a ploughing action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/543284]{If you already have fields, you must place the field tile adjacent to an existing field.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sowing Machine}{-}{M019}{(1VP. Cost 3W. Req 1 horse.)}
{Whenever you use a special action, you may immediately take a ``Sow'' action as long as you have at least 2 horses.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/519251]{The sowing action follows the special action. If you use the special action to play an improvement that gives you benefits when sowing (e.g. \cardref{Fallow Fields}{-}{M015}), you receive those benefits when you sow after that special action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Peat Fertilizer}{-}{M020}{(Req 2 fields.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, you can immediately take a ``Sow'' action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/576164]{You do not place a family member to perform the sowing action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Peat Ash Fertilizer}{-}{M021}{(Cost 1F.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, you can place 1 additional grain on all fields and farmyard spaces where grain is growing. In addition, you can place 1 additional vegetable on all fields and farmyard spaces where vegetables are planted.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You receive nothing for empty fields.}
\item \ecp{Does not count as a sowing action.}
\item \ecp{Is optional, but if you choose to add grain, you have to add them to all your grain fields, and if you choose to add vegetables, you have to add them to all your vegetable fields.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Nosebag}{-}{M022}{(Cost 1F. Req 1 major imp.)}
{Whenever you use the ``Take 1 Grain'' action, you also receive 1 horse.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is only activated by taking the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} action space.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ploughhorse Market}{-}{M023}{(1VP. Cost 1C. Req 1 major imp.)}
{Whenever you use a person to take a ``Plough fields'' action, you can buy 1 horse for 1 food immediately afterwards.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This does not include the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} special action,} \ecp{but only the two action spaces \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} and \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Large Livestock Market}{-}{M024}{(Cost 1F.)}
{You can immediately exchange 2 sheep for 1 cattle and 1 horse. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You cannot exchange only 1 sheep for 1 other animal.}
\item \ecp{You cannot return 1 cattle and 1 horse to the supply to receive 2 sheep.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Special Pasture}{-}{M025}{(Cost 2W. Req 1 pasture.)}
{Immediately fence 1 empty farmyard space (or a farmyard space with a stable) with 4 fences. You need not pay wood for these. The fenced space may not border your existing pastures.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You may connect your pastures later.}
\item \cardtext{All future pastures must border at least one existing pasture.}
\item \ecp{If you build extra fences this turn, e.g. with the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, you may not use these to connect the special pasture to the existing pastures: they should remain unconnected until the end of the turn.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Home Wood}{-}{M026}{(Req 3 imp.)}
{With this improvement, you can keep 1 animal (except a sheep) on each of your forest tiles.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\item \ecp{The forest tiles do not count as pastures.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Horse Trough}{-}{M027}{(Cost 1S.)}
{You can keep up to 2 horses in an unused farmyard space adjacent to your home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The space does not count as used.}
\item \cardtext{You may change which space you keep the horses in.}
\item \ecp{The farmyard space does not count as a pasture.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Open Grill}{Grillplatz}{M028}{(2VP. Return fireplace.)}
{At any time, you may convert goods to food as follows: vegetable $\rightarrow$ 2 food; sheep $\rightarrow$ 2 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 3 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 3 food; horse $\rightarrow$ 2 food. Whenever you \changed{use a bread baking action}, you may convert: grain $\rightarrow$ 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When you bake bread you can convert as many grain with the Open Grill as you want.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/331835]{Is a cooking improvement and a baking improvement, but not an oven.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\item After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pot Roast Recipe}{-}{M029}{(Req 2 horses.)}
{You can use the \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2} or \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4} major improvements to convert horses to food. You receive 2 food for each horse.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{You can also use this card with the \cardref{Cooking{ }Hearth}{Kochstelle}{K128} minor improvement (because it counts as a major improvement), but not with the \cardref{Simple Fireplace}{Einfache Feuerstelle}{E20}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Grain Distillery}{-}{M030}{(1VP. Cost 2S 1 grain.)}
{In the feeding phase of each harvest, you can convert exactly 1 fuel and 1 grain to 5 food. In the final harvest, you can convert any number of pairs of 1 fuel and 1 grain from your supply to 1 bonus point per pair.}

\card{Forest Kindergarten}{Waldkindergarten}{M031}{(1VP. Cost 1W 2S. Req max 3 forests.)}
{Whenever you take any ``family growth'' action, you receive 1 food for each of your farmyard spaces that contains a forest tile.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This includes improvements \ecp{and occupations} that allow family growth.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pheromones}{Viehzuchtunterst■tzung}{M032}{(Req max 2 imp.)}
{You immediately receive 1 food. In addition, each player who has at least one stable or pasture receives 2 food.}

\card{Malthouse}{-}{M033}{(1VP. Cost 2C.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, you can also convert 1 grain to 4 food.}

\card{Chimney Hood}{-}{M034}{(Cost 1C.)}
{You immediately receive as much food as you would receive from one of your baking improvements if you baked 1 grain into bread. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You do not lose the grain.}
\item \ecp{Using the Chimney Hood does not count as baking bread.}
\item \ecp{If you have no baking improvements, you do not receive any food when you play this card. Baking improvements are improvements with a ``baking'' symbol.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Village Hall}{-}{M035}{(1VP. Cost 2W 2C.)}
{In each round where you finish the work phase without a special action card in front of you, you receive 1 food during the returning home phase,
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You also receive the food if you took a special action card which another player then took from you.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479848]{In the solo game, you receive the food if you have not used a special action card during a round.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Healing Clay}{-}{M036}{(1VP. Cost 1C.)}
{You immediately receive 1 food. Whenever you take the \actionref{Infirmary}{Infirmary} action with a person who is marked with a bed token, you receive 1 additional food.}

\card{Arid Field}{-}{M037}{(Req 3 imp.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, place 1 fuel and 1 food from the \changed{general} supply on the emptied farmyard space. You receive the token once the space is no longer empty.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{A space with fuel and food counts as unused.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Birthing House}{-}{M038}{(2VP. Cost 2C 1S.)}
{Whenever you use any ``family growth'' action, you receive 1 bonus point as well as 1 fuel and 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This includes improvements \ecp{and occupations} that allow family growth.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Barge}{-}{M039}{(1VP. Cost 3W. Req 2 imp.)}
{Place, alternately, 1 fuel or 1 food on each remaining round space, beginning with 1 fuel. At the start of each round, you receive the token.}

\card{Peat Barge}{Torfkahn}{M040}{(1VP. Cost 2W.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action, you also receive 2 fuel.}

\card{Peat Sled}{Torfkreite}{M041}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Add your choice of 2, 4, 7, or 10 to the current round number. On the corresponding round space, place 3, 4, 5, or 6 fuel (depending on which number you added). At the start of that round, you receive the fuel.}

\card{Peat Iron}{Torf Spaten}{M042}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you have at least 2 moor tiles in your farmyard at the start of a harvest, you receive 1 fuel.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Spinning Mill}{-}{M043}{(2VP. Cost 2W 2C. Req 1 sheep.)}
{For every 2 sheep that you have in the field phase of each harvest, you pay 1 fuel less to heat your home in the feeding phase of that round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You can never pay fewer than 0 fuel.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Built-in Oven}{Ofenanlage}{M044}{(Return Furnace. -1VP.)}
{You no longer need to pay any heating costs.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The \cardref{Furnace}{-}{M007} is found under the \cardref{Clay Oven}{Lehmofen}{A5}.}
\item \ecp{Is not an oven.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/514728]{The point from this card counts as negative for the \cardref{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276}, but can be compensated with \cardref{Yeoman Farmer}{Freibauer}{E165}.}
\item After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Coal Seam}{-}{M045}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1C.)}
{You immediately receive 1 fuel. Whenever you use the \actionref{Hiring Fair}{HiringXFair} special action or the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action \changed{space}, you also receive 1 fuel.}

\card{Oven Damper}{-}{M046}{(Cost 2S.)}
{You immediately receive 3 fuel. The \cardref{Clay Oven}{Lehmofen}{A5}, \cardref{Stone Oven}{Steinofen}{A6}, \cardref{Furnace}{-}{M007} and \cardref{Heating Stove}{Heizofen}{M008} major improvements and the \cardref{Built-in Oven}{Ofenanlage}{M044} minor improvement are each worth 1 additional bonus point to you.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is not an oven.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Draughthorses}{-}{M047}{}
{Whenever you take exactly 3 wood from an action space, you can pay 1 food to receive 1 additional wood. Whenever you take 4 or more wood from an action space, you can pay 1 food to receive 2 additional wood. To do either of these, you must have at least 1 horse.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Only wood that is taken directly from an action space is counted. Wood received from other cards is not.}
\item \ecp{Wood placed on an action space by the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} is also counted.}
\item \ecp{Wood from the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games is also counted, and may activate the Draughthorses if there is additional wood on the space.}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, the wood that you leave on the action space also counts for the Draughthorses.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Forest Path}{Waldweg}{M048}{(Cost 1C. Req 1 forest.)}
{You immediately receive 3 wood. Once this card has been passed, the player who has it at the end of the game receives -1 point. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Use a green arrow to show who currently has the card.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Moor Birch Tree}{-}{M049}{(1VP. Cost 2F. Req 3 rooms.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, you also receive 2 wood.}

\card{River Clay}{-}{M050}{(Req 1 major imp.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action \changed{space}, you also receive 2 clay.}

\card{Willow Bank}{-}{M051}{(Req 1 major imp.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fell Trees}{FellXTrees} special action, you also receive 1 reed.}

\card{Stone Quarry}{-}{M052}{(1VP. Cost 3F.)}
{Place 5 stone on this card. Whenever you use the \actionref{Hiring Fair}{HiringXFair} special action, you also receive 1 stone from this card.}

\card{Hardware Store}{-}{M053}{(Cost 2C 1R. Req 2 imp.)}
{Place 3 usage counters on this card. At any time, you can return one usage counter to the supply and take 1 of each building resource that you have none of.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reeds, and stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Basic Supplies}{Grundausstattung}{M054}{(Cost 1 veg.)}
{Immediately take goods and tokens from the \changed{general} supply until you have at least 1 fuel, 1 food, 1 wood, 1 clay, 1 reed, 1 stone, and 1 grain in your \changed{personal} supply. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Wood does not count as fuel and grain does not count as food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Advance Payment}{Darlehen}{M055}{(-4VP.)}
{You immediately receive 1 fuel, 1 food, 1 wood, 1 clay, 1 reed, 1 stone, 1 sheep, and 1 grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/514728]{The points from this card count as negative for the \cardref{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276}, but can be compensated with \cardref{Yeoman Farmer}{Freibauer}{E165}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Peat Moss}{-}{M056}{(Req exactly 1 moor.)}
{You require 2 less wood and 1 less reed to build wooden hut rooms.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Farmhands' Quarters}{-}{M057}{(Cost 1W 1R.)}
{Whenever you acquire a major improvement, you can save 1 building resource of your choice by paying 1 fuel instead. Whenever you receive an improvement card in your hand from the player to your right, you also receive 1 food from the \changed{general} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Minor improvements that can be upgrades of major improvements count as major improvements for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Living History Museum}{-}{M058}{(4VP. Return Museum o/t Moors. Req clay hut.)}
{The following major improvements are cheaper for you: \cardref{Village Church}{-}{M009}, by 1 stone; \cardref{Furniture Stall}{M—belhandel}{M010}, by 1 wood; \cardref{Ceramics Stall}{Keramikhandel}{M011}, by 1 clay; \cardref{Basket Stall}{Korbhandel}{M012}, by 1 reed; \cardref{Furnace}{-}{M007}, by 1 clay; \cardref{Heating Stove}{Heizofen}{M008}, by 1 stone; \changed{\cardref{Riding Stables}{Reiterhof}{M003}}, by 1 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The \cardref{Museum of the Moors}{-}{M006} is under the \cardref{Peat-charcoal Kiln}{Torfk—hlerei}{M001}.}
\item After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Register of Craftsmen}{-}{M059}{(Req 2 major imp.)}
{Immediately acquire the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8}, or \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9}, without placing a person. You pay 1 stone less for it. \passing

\card{Tinker}{-}{M060}{(Cost 1F. Req 3 major imp.)}
{If you have at least one of the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8}, or \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9} major improvements, you immediately receive 1 wood, 1 clay, 1 reed, and 1 stone. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Workbench}{-}{M061}{(Cost 2W. Req max 4 imp.)}
{You receive 3 wood, 2 clay, and 1 reed in the field phase of each of the last 2 harvests.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can use these, for example, to earn bonus points from the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8}, or \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Taps}{-}{M062}{(Req 2 imp.)}
{You can take an available special action card even after you have already placed all your person markers, when it would be your turn again. Then the work phase is over for you.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You cannot use this card twice in one round.}
\item \ecp{You can even use this card to take a special action when no other player has a family member left (or in the solo game).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Tool Shed}{-}{M063}{(1VP. Cost 1W 1C. Req 2 imp.)}
{Whenever you take the special action card with \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} and \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat}, and take one of these special actions, you can take both of these special actions (in whichever order you choose).}

\card{Farm Extension}{-}{M064}{(1VP. Cost 1C.)}
{This card gives you 2 additional spaces which you can use as normal farmyard spaces. Place it beside your farmyard. Each of the new spaces must border an existing farmyard space. This expands your famyard by 2 spaces.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If the new farmyard spaces are not used at the end of the game, they each score -1 point.}
\item \ecp{This card still counts as a minor improvement.}
\item \ecp{You may place this card anywhere around your farmyard. You may not move it later. The farmyard spaces are considered to be adjacent to the existing farmyard spaces, so you can e.g. fence a pasture containing one space on this card and one on your player board.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Thicket}{Dickicht}{M065}{(Req 4 forests.)}
{Choose up to 2 forest tiles, and place 1 additional forest tile on top of each of them. You can remove 1 tile with the \actionref{Fell Trees}{FellXTrees} special action---you cannot use the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} action on spaces with 2 forest tiles.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When counting forests, e.g.\ for requirements, only the top tile on a space is counted.}
\item \ecp{You may add a tile to a farmyard space already containing 2 or more tiles, as long as the top one is a forest.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Swamp}{-}{M066}{(Not after round 4.)}
{Place 1 moor tile on the space for round 12. At the start of this round, you can take the tile and place it on an empty space in your farmyard.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you don't place the tile in your farmyard, it is returned to the general supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clear Felling}{Kahlschlag}{M067}{(Req max 3 forests.)}
{You immediately receive 2 wood. You can immediately turn over up to 2 forest tiles to show the moor side, as long as there is nothing except the forest tile on those spaces. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reforestation}{-}{M068}{(Req 3 major imp.)}
{Immediately place 1 forest tile on an empty space in your farmyard. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Forest tiles need not be adjacent to one another.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bog Body}{-}{M069}{(Req 1 moor.)}
{The owner of the \cardref{Museum of the Moors}{-}{M006} and the owner of the \cardref{Living History Museum}{-}{M058} each receive 1 bonus point at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The Museum of the Moors is a major improvement and is under the \cardref{Peat-charcoal Kiln}{Torfk—hlerei}{M001}. The Living History Museum is a hand card and is an upgrade of the Museum of the Moors.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Administration}{-}{M070}{(Cost 1W 2C. Req max 4 cards in hand.)}
{You immediately receive 2 food. In the last harvest, for each major improvement that you have, you can exchange 1 food for 1 bonus point.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This card itself counts as a card in hand for its own requirement.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/497755]{Minor improvements that are upgrades of major improvements count as major improvements for this card. Major improvements that are minor improvements to you, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Manufacturer}{Fabrikant}{K277} or \cardref{Well Builder}{Brunnenbauer}{I220}, also count as major improvements.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Leather Saddle}{-}{M071}{(1VP. Cost 1F. Req 2 horses.)}
{Whenever you have at least 3 horses, you receive 1 bonus point for each cattle that you convert to food.}

\card{Wedding Coach}{-}{M072}{(Cost 1W 1 veg. Req 4 horses.)}
{You can immediately carry out a ``family growth even without space in your home'' action, but you do not place a person to take this action. Place the offspring on this card until the returning home phase.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You cannot use the newborn to take an action in this round,} \ecp{unless you use the \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Forest Hut}{-}{M073}{(1VP. Cost 2W.)}
{Immediately place 1 guest marker on one of your forest tiles. You will receive the guest marker when you use a special action to clear that forest tile. Then, in that same round, you can place the guest marker as you would a person. At the end of that round, return the guest marker to the supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains more than 1 tile, you receive the guest marker when the top tile is removed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Farm Cart}{-}{M074}{(Cost 3W. Req 2 horses.)}
{Whenever you take at least 5 wood, 4 clay, 3 reeds, or 2 stone from an action space, you also receive 1 grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Only building resources that are taken directly from an action space are counted. Building resources received from other cards are not.}
\item \ecp{Wood placed on an action space by the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} is also counted.}
\item \ecp{Resources from the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games are also counted, and may activate the Farm Cart if there are additional resources on the space (e.g.\ due to the Wood Distributor).}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, the wood that you leave on the action space also counts for the Farm Cart.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Moor Fire}{-}{M075}{(Req 2 moors.)}
{Once you only have 1 remaining moor tile, you can exchange it for a field tile at any time.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If there is another tile underneath it, you must also return it.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/543284]{If you already have fields, you can only exchange the moor tile if it borders an existing field.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Deep Plough}{-}{M076}{(2VP. Cost 3W. Req 2 imp.)}
{Immediately place 1 moor tile on an empty space in your farmyard. Whenever you use a person to take the ``Plough fields'' action, you can also exchange one moor tile for 1 field tile.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This does not include the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} special action,} \ecp{but only the two action spaces \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} and \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow}.}
\item \cardtext{If another tile is underneath the moor tile, it must also be returned to the supply.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/543284]{If you already have fields, you can only exchange a moor tile that borders an existing field.}
\item \ecp{This is a plough.} \apx[Riding Plough]{Each time you use a ploughing action space, you may only use one card out of the ploughs and the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wild Fields}{-}{M077}{(2F. Req 2 fields.)}
{You can immediately place up to 2 field tiles on empty spaces in your farmyard---on the condition that neither tile borders any other field at the time when it is placed.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The two new fields may not border each other either.}
\item \cardtext{Later, they may be connected.}
\item \cardtext{All later fields should be adjacent to at least one existing field.}
\item \ecp{Does not count as a ploughing action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{No-Till Farming}{-}{M078}{(Req 2 fields.)}
{You can plant grain or vegetables on up to 2 empty farmyard spaces. These spaces do not count as fields when scoring, but as empty spaces.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You determine the 2 farmyard spaces immediately when you play this card (and cannot change this choice later), but you have to take a sowing action to actually plant the grain or vegetables.}
\item \ecp{After you've harvested all grain or vegetables from a farmyard space, you may not plant there again.}
\item \cardtext{You can destroy the plants at any time, by returning the resources to the supply.}
\item \cardtext{The grain and vegetables count towards those totals when scoring.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Nature's Fertilizer}{-}{M079}{(Cost 2F. Req 1 major imp.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} special action, you immediately receive a ``Sow'' action for that field only. This also applies if you turn 1 moor tile into a field using the \cardref{Moor Fire}{-}{M075} or \changed{\cardref{Peat Burn-off}{-}{M016}} minor improvement.}

\card{Peat Hut}{Torfplankenh■tte}{M080}{(1VP. Cost 5 fuel 2R.)}
{This card serves as a room for one of your people. It must be heated with 1 fuel during the feeding phase of each harvest. You can use \changed{a} renovate action to discard this card and add 1 room to your wooden hut.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You can no longer exchange this card for a room after renovating to a clay hut or stone house.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479979]{You cannot exchange this card for a room and renovate to a clay hut with the same renovate action.}
\item \ecp{You can use the \cardref{Hay Wagon}{Leiterwagen}{M094}, but not the \cardref{Builder's Trowel}{Spachtel}{E50} to exchange the Peat Hut for a room.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Flatboat}{-}{M081}{(Cost 4W.)}
{Place, alternately, 1 fuel or 1 horse on each of the next 7 remaining round spaces, beginning with 1 fuel. At the start of each round, you receive the fuel or the horse.}

\card{Livestock Market}{-}{M082}{(Req 5 animals.)}
{You can immediately exchange up to 3 animals for the next most valuable animal. You must swap them al at the same time, and you can only take the new animals if you have room for all of them on your farm. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The order (from least to most valuable) is: sheep, wild boar, cattle, horse.}
\item \ecp{The 3 animals need not be the same type.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cattle Stall}{Viehhandlung}{M083}{(1VP. Cost 2W 2C.)}
{Add 2, 4, 6, 8 to the current round. Place 1 animal on each corresponding round space. You choose which animal goes on which space, but all the animals must be different. At the start of these rounds, you can buy the animal for 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you don't buy the animal, it is returned to the supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Night Pasture}{Hutanger}{M084}{(Cost 2C.)}
{You can keep 3 animals of your choice on this card, and other players can keep 1. All the animals on this card count as yours when animals breed. You are always the last to play during the breeding phase.}

\card{Nature Reserve}{-}{M085}{(Cost 1F. Req 1 pasture.)}
{Immediately fence 1 farmyard space which contains a forest or moor tile. You do not pay any wood for these fences. Once there are no tiles left on the space, it becomes a pasture.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can also fence a space which contains 2 tiles.}
\item \cardtext{The fenced space must be adjacent to your pastures} \ecp{when you play this card.}
\item \ecp{The space does not count as a pasture while there is still a tile in it. When you fence a new pasture, it may not border only this fenced space, but it has to border at least one real pasture.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Building Plan}{-}{M086}{(Cost 1F.)}
{Whenever you build 2 rooms at once with the ``Build rooms'' action, you can immediately build 2 stables from your personal supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Instead of 2 stables, you can choose to only build 1.}
\item \ecp{You don't pay wood for these stables.}
\item \ecp{You also receive the free stables if you build more than 2 rooms. You cannot receive more than 2 stables from the Building Plan in one turn.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Horse Butcher}{-}{M087}{(3VP. Return Horse Slaughterhouse.)}
{At any time, you may convert animals to food as follows: sheep $\rightarrow$ 1 food; wild boar $\rightarrow$ 2 food; cattle $\rightarrow$ 3 food; horse $\rightarrow$ 2 food; 2 horses $\rightarrow$ 5 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{There is a \cardref{Horse Slaughterhouse}{Rossschlachterei}{M004/005} under each \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}.}
\item \ecp{The Horse Slaughterhouse is returned to the major improvements board, on the space from which it originally came, and on top of any card lying there.}
\item \ecp{Is a cooking improvement.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=673]{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/328175]{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\item After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Butcher's Block}{Schlachtbank}{M088}{(1VP. Cost 1W.)}
{This card cannot be played in a round that is followed by a harvest. All other players must and you may immediately convert one animal of their (your) choice to food. Sheep provide 1 food, wild boar 2 food, cattle 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Players may not convert more than 1 animal and do not need to have a cooking improvement.}
\item \ecp{Is not a cooking improvement. Does not activate the \cardref{Schnitzel Mallet}{Schnitzelklopfer}{ø18}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fire Brigade}{-}{M089}{(Cost 1C 1S. Req 4F 4 fuel.)}
{You immediately receive 2 food. If you still have forest tiles on at least \changed{2 farm yard spaces, you get bonus points: 1 fewer point than you have forests, with a maximum of 4 points.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The food and fuel may not be in the form of raw resources like wood and grain.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/466456]{You receive the bonus points immediately when you play this card; write them done on the scoring pad.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wild Harvest}{-}{M090}{}
{You immediately receive 1 food. At the start of each harvest, shuffle all the start cards and draw 1. The start cards are numbered from 1 to 9. If the number on the card is equal to or less than the number of forest tiles in your farmyard, you receive 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fish Smokehouse}{-}{M091}{(2VP. Cost 1W 2C.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action \changed{space}, you can pay 1 fuel to receive an additional 3 food.}

\card{Loan}{-}{M092}{(1VP. Cost 2F.)}
{At the start of each harvest, shuffle all the start cards and draw 1. The start cards are numbered from 1 to 9. If the number on the card is equal to or less than the amount of clay you have in your supply, the 2 food that you paid are returned to you with interest: you receive 6 food but must pass this improvement to the player on your left, who adds it to their hand.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after the loan has been repaid.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fallow Land}{-}{M093}{(Req 2 imp.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fell Trees}{FellXTrees} or \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special actions to clear a space in your farmyard, place 1 Food on the space. You receive the food when the space is no longer empty.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{A farmyard space with food counts as unused.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hay Wagon}{Leiterwagen}{M094}{(1VP. Cost 2W. Req 2 horses.)}
{Immediately after you take 3 wood, 3 clay, 2 reed, or 2 stone from an action space, you can take a ``Build room(s)'' or ``Renovate'' action without placing a person.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/476708]{Is also activated if you take more resources. Is only activated once per action space.}
\item \ecp{Only building resources that are taken directly from an action space are counted. Building resources received from other cards are not.}
\item \ecp{Wood placed on an action space by the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} is also counted.}
\item \ecp{Resources from the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games are also counted, and may activate the Hay Wagon if there are additional resources on the space (e.g.\ due to the Wood Distributor).}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, the wood that you leave on the action space also counts for the Hay Wagon.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Peat Bath}{-}{M095}{(1 VP. Cost 1W 1C.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Infirmary}{Infirmary} action \changed{space} with a person, count how many moor tiles are in your farmyard. Place 1 food on the next remaining round space(s) up to that number. At the beginning of those rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{It is irrelevant whether the person has a bed marker or not.}
\item \ecp{If the number of the current round is equal or higher to the number of moor tiles, the Peat Bath has no effect.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Edge of the Forest}{-}{M096}{(Req 3 imp.)}
{For each border between a forest tile and a field in your farmyard, you receive 1 food. For each border between a forest tile and a moor tile in your farmyard, you receive 1 fuel. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Borders are the spaces where you could place a fence.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ecological Niche}{-}{M097}{}
{\changed{If there is at least one type of animal that only you own, you receive 2 food.} If you are the only player who has planted grain, you receive 1 food. If you are the only player who has planted vegetables, you receive 1 food. You receive 1 fuel is you have more forest tiles than any other player and 1 fuel if you have more moor tiles than any other player. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When checking for grain and vegetables, you only take into account grain and vegetables that are currently on your (and other players') fields; not resources that were harvested earlier.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Winter Storehouse}{Lagerstðtte}{M098}{(Cost 1W 2C.)}
{Place 3 usage counters on this card. At any time (even while you are taking an action) you can return 1 usage counter and take fuel and food from the supply until you have at least 2 fuel and 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Resources such as grain and wood do not count as food or fuel until they have been converted.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Lawn Turf}{-}{M099}{(Req 4 imp.)}
{\changed{If you have at least 3 unused spaces on your farmyard, you immediately receive 1 fuel for each unused space except the first 2, up to a maximum of 5 fuel.} \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Spaces with forest or moor tiles do not count as unused spaces.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Firewood}{-}{M100}{(Cost 1W. Req 1 major imp.)}
{You immediately receive 1 fuel. Whenever you convert at least 1 wood to fuel during a harvest to heat your home, you need a total of 1 fuel fewer.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Can only be used once per harvest.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Peat Pellets}{Torfpellets}{M101}{(Req 1 major imp.)}
{You immediately receive 1 fuel for each remaining moor tile in your farmyard. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fuel Storage}{Brennstofflager}{M102}{(1VP. Cost 1C 1R.)}
{Add 1, 5, and 9 to the current round. Place 1 wood on each corresponding round space. Add 3, 7, and 11 to the current round. Place 1 fuel on each corresponding round space. At the start of each round, you receive the wood or fuel.}

\card{Bog Pony}{Grubenpferde}{M103}{(Req 1 major imp.)}
{At any time, you can lie one of your horses that is standing up on its side and take 2 fuel. This horse does not count during the breeding phase of the harvest. At the end of the game, it is worth only half a point, but it can (like other horses) be converted into food with an appropriate improvement.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Outside of the breeding phase, a pony counts as a horse. You get the full amount of food when you cook a pony.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{You can have as many ponies as you want.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Drying Field}{-}{M104}{(1VP. Cost 2F.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, add 3 to the current round. Place 2 fuel on the corresponding round space. At the start of the round, you receive the fuel.}

\card{Peat-cutting Expedition}{-}{M105}{(Cost 4F.)}
{Immediately take as many moor tiles from your farmyard as you wish. For each moor tile that you remove, you receive 1 bonus point and 2 fuel. If you have at least 2 horses, you receive 1 additional fuel for each horse except the first one, up to a maximum of 4 additional fuel. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You cannot remove covered moor tiles.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Riverside Woods}{-}{M106}{(Req 3 major imp.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, you receive 1 additional wood for each of your farmyard spaces with a forest tile, up to a maximum of 3 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If a farmyard space contains 2 tiles, only the topmost tile counts for this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Timber Mill}{-}{M107}{(3VP. Cost 3C 2S.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fell Trees}{FellXTrees} special action or take at least 4 wood from an action space, you receive 1 additional wood. If you pay 1 fuel, you receive 1 \changed{more} additional wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Only wood that is taken directly from an action space is counted. Wood received from other cards is not.}
\item \ecp{Wood placed on an action space by the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} is also counted.}
\item \ecp{Wood from the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games is also counted, and may activate the Timber Mill if there is additional wood on the space.}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, the wood that you leave on the action space also counts for the Timber Mill.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Oak Bark}{-}{M108}{(Cost 1F. Req 2 major imp.)}
{You immediately receive 2 wood. Whenever you convert cattle, wild boar, or horses to food, you receive 1 additional wood for each of these animals that you convert.}

\card{Loam}{-}{M109}{(Req 1 imp.)}
{Whenever you have placed all except one of your people during the work phase and you use the \actionref{Hiring Fair}{HiringXFair} special action, you receive 1 additional clay.}

\card{Alder Swamp}{-}{M110}{(1VP. Cost 2F. Req 2 imp.)}
{Whenever you use a \actionref{Fell Trees}{FellXTrees} special action, you also receive your choice of 1 reed or 1 wood.}

\card{Stone Wagon}{-}{M111}{(Cost 2W.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action, you also receive 1 stone.}

\card{Wheelbarrow}{-}{M112}{(Cost 2W. Req 1 major imp.)}
{Whenever you take at least 4 of the same building resources from an action space, you also receive 1 fuel. Whenever you \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat}, you also receive 1 building resource of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reeds, and stone.}
\item \ecp{Only building resources that are taken directly from an action space are counted. Building resources received from other cards are not.}
\item \ecp{Wood placed on an action space by the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} is also counted.}
\item \ecp{Resources from the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games are also counted, and may activate the Wheelbarrow if there are additional resources on the space (e.g.\ due to the Wood Distributor).}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, the wood that you leave on the action space also counts for the Wheelbarrow.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Peat Boat}{-}{M113}{(3VP. Cost 3W 2R.)}
{At any time, you can exchange fuel for goods as follows: 3 fuel $\rightarrow$ 2 wood or 2 clay; 4 fuel $\rightarrow$ 2 reed or 2 stone; 2 fuel $\rightarrow$ 1 grain; 3 fuel $\rightarrow$ 1 vegetable.}

\card{Household Inventory}{-}{M114}{(Cost 1F. Req 1 field, pasture, or stable.)}
{If you have 5/6/7/8/9/10 empty farmyard spaces, you receive the first 1/2/3/4/5/6 goods from the following list (in order): 1 reed, 1 grain, 1 cattle, 1 stone, 1 vegetable, 1 horse. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Moor and forest tiles do not count as empty spaces.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Village Shop}{Dorfladen}{M115}{(Cost 1W 1R. Not after round 4.)}
{Place 3 usage counters on this card. At any time, you can remove them to receive 1 other good or marker. The offer changes each round: 2: food, 3: grain, 4: fuel, 5: wood, 6: clay, 7: sheep, 8: reed, 9: wild boar, 10: stone, 11: cattle, 12: horse, 13: vegetable, 14: guest marker.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The guest marker allows you to take one additional action.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2368]{A harvest counts as part of the preceding round.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals that you receive into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/485528]{You may use this card more than once per round, to take multiple identical items.}% see also http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1025.0
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hearth Brush}{-}{M116}{(Cost 1R.)}
{If the \cardref{Stone Oven}{Steinofen}{A6} has not yet been built, you can immediately place it underneath the \cardref{Heating Stove}{Heizofen}{M008}. From next round, whenever you use a person to take an action, you can build the Heating Stove immediately afterwards by paying the required resources. The Heating Stove is worth 1 additional bonus point for you.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The Stone Oven and the Heating Stove swap places.} \ecp{The Stone Oven cannot be acquired while it is covered by the Heating Stove.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pastoral Letter}{-}{M117}{(Req 2 major imp.)}
{If the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10} has not yet been built, you can immediately place it under the \cardref{Village Church}{-}{M009}. From next round, whenever you use a person to take an action, you can build the Village Church immediately afterwards by paying the required resources. The Village Church and the \cardref{Church}{Kirche}{M132} are each worth 1 additional bonus point for you.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The Well and the Village Church swap places.} \ecp{The Well cannot be acquired while it is covered by the Village Church.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Co-operative Store}{-}{M118}{(1VP. Cost 2W 1C.)}
{Place 4 usage counters on this card. At any time, you can remove 1 of them to exchange any 1 building resource for any other building resource except stone.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reeds, and stone.}
\item \ecp{You are allowed to pay stone for any other building resource.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Out on the Wallaby}{-}{M119}{}
{You receive goods if you own craftman's buildings. \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}: 3 wood; \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8}: 3 clay; \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9}: 2 reeds. \passing
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2564841]{In a solo game, this card is removed from the game after you play it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Chamber of Commerce}{-}{M120}{(1VP. Cost 2C 1S.)}
{You immediately receive 1 wood and 1 reed. At the end of the game, each of these major improvements: \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8} and \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9} is worth 1 additional bonus point to you.}

\card{Routine Work}{-}{M121}{(Cost 1F. Req no imp.)}
{Whenever you choose not to use a craftman's building to convert building resources to food during the harvest, you receive your choice of 1 food or 1 fuel instead.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can use this card on up to 3 buildings: the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, the \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8}, and the \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9}.}
\item \ecp{You can only get food or fuel for buildings that you own.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Peat-Cutting Rights}{Torfstechvorrecht}{M122}{(Req 1 horse.)}
{Add 4 and 7 to the current round. Place 1 moor tile on each of the corresponding rounds. These tiles show that you can use the special action \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} at the start of the round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Take the appropriate special action card whenever you use the Peat-Cutting Rights.} \ecp{After you've used the special action, return the moor tile to the general supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Agricultural Implement}{-}{M123}{(Cost 1W.)}
{Whenever you use a person to take the ``Plough fields'' action, you can take a special action card immediately afterwards, as long as it has not already been used twice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The special action card costs 0 or 2 food, as usual.}
\item \ecp{Is only activated on both the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} and the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action spaces, but not by the \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} special action or cards that allow you to plough.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/530572]{You are allowed to take the special action even if you have no family members left at home.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Moor Enclosures}{-}{M124}{(1VP. Cost 1S. Req clay hut.)}
{Place 2 Moor tiles on this card. The card represents 2 additional, normal farmyard spaces. Place it beside your farmyard. Each of the new spaces must border an existing farmyard space. This expands your farm by 2 spaces.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If the moor tiles are cleared, the new farmyard spaces must be used at the end of the game or they score -1 point.}
\item \ecp{You may place this card anywhere around your farmyard. You may not move it later. The farmyard spaces are considered to be adjacent to the existing farmyard spaces, so you can e.g. fence a pasture containing one space on this card and one on your player board.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bog Forest}{Moorwald}{M125}{(Cost 1F. Req 3 imp.)}
{Immediately place 1 forest tile on as many of your own moor tiles as you wish. You can only use the covered moor tiles once you have removed the forest tiles with the \actionref{Fell Trees}{FellXTrees} special action. You cannot use \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn} on forest tiles that are on top of moor tiles.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{When counting moors, e.g.\ for requirements, only the top tile on a space is counted.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Forest Swamp}{-}{M126}{(Req 2 major imp.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, turn over the moor tile that you remove. Add 4 to the current round and place the tile on the corresponding round space. At the start of the round, you can place the forest tile on an empty space in your farmyard.}

\card{Tree Nursery}{-}{M127}{(Cost 1W. Req no imp.)}
{Place 1 forest tile on the spaces for rounds 12 and 13. At the start of these rounds, you can take the tile and place it on an empty space in your farmyard.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you choose not to place the tile in your farmyard, the tile is returned to the general supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Land Parcel}{-}{M128}{(Req max 2 imp.)}
{When you play this card, you receive 1 forest tile that you must immediately place on an empty space in your farmyard. At the end of the game, \changed{you receive 2 bonus point if you have 1 unused farmyard space, you receive -1 bonus point if you have 2 unused spaces, and you receive -3 bonus point if you have 3 or more unused spaces.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may not play this card if you have no unused farmyard spaces.}
\item \ecp{Negative points from this card count as negative for the \cardref{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276} and \cardref{Yeoman Farmer}{Freibauer}{E165}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stock-breeding Prize}{Tierzuchtprðmie}{M129}{(Cost 1 grain. Req no unused spaces.)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each other player in the game, as long as you have at least 1 animal of each of the 4 types. These points are doubled or tripled if you have 2 or 3 of each type of animal.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{For the requirement, farmyard spaces on improvement cards such as \cardref{Moor Enclosures}{-}{M124} are also counted.}
\item \cardtext{For example, in a 5-player game, you receive 4 bonus points if you have 1 of each animal.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Family Burial Plot}{-}{M130}{(1VP. Cost 1S. Req stone house.)}
{Immediately place the tombstone on an \changed{unused} space in your farmyard. That space cannot be used to hold anything now, but is counted as used, and is worth 1 additional bonus point at the end of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The bonus point is in addition to the 1 regular point of this card.}
\item \ecp{You may not play this card if you have no unused farmyard spaces.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Moor Archaeology}{-}{M131}{(1VP. Req clay hut.)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat} special action, you can place 1 fence from your supply on the emptied farmyard space. You cannot use this farmyard space to hold anything, but it is counted as used, and is worth 1 additional bonus point at the end of the game.}

\card{Church}{Kirche}{M132}{(5VP. Discard Village Church.)}
{For upgrading the \cardref{Village Church}{-}{M009} to the Church, you receive 2 food. At the end of each round, you can tithe up to 1 fuel to earn 1 bonus point.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The Village Church is under the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10}.}
\item After this card has been played, it counts both as a minor and as a major improvement, e.g.\ for the requirements of other cards. (Of course, it still counts as a single improvement.)
\item The discarded Village Church is removed from the game, not returned to the major improvements board.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\section{Occupations}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\card{Land Agent}{Ackerhðndler}{E147}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Take 1 Vegetable}{TakeX1XVegetable} action space, you also receive 1 grain. When you play this card, you receive 1 vegetable from the \changed{general} supply.}

\card{Academic}{Akademiker}{E148}{(3--5 players)}
{This card counts as 2 occupations for minor improvements and when scoring the \cardref{Reeve}{Vogt}{E217} \changed{or \cardref{Tutor}{Hauslehrer}{E174}} occupation card.\comment{changed in pimp-box}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3910803]{Playing the Academic counts as 1 occupation for the \cardref{Bread Paddle}{Brotschieber}{K111} and \cardref{Bookshelf}{B■cherregal}{K112}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Master Baker}{Backðltester}{E149}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player bakes bread, you can bake bread if you have a baking improvement with the ``baking'' symbol. If you take a bake action yourself, you receive 1 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when another player uses a baking improvement (with the ``baking'' symbol) to convert grain to food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/382609]{Is not activated if another player uses the \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} action space, but does not bake.}
\item \apx[Brotverkðufer]{Bread is not baked if schnaps is distilled or beer is brewed, or when a \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17} or \cardref{Hand Mill}{Handm■hle}{I75} is used.}
\item \ecp{You do not receive the additional food if you bake bread because of the Master Baker itself.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Baker}{Bðcker}{E150}{(1--5 players)}
{During each harvest, you may bake bread at the start of the feeding phase if you have an appropriate improvement. When you play this card, you may bake bread as an additional action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may only use the Baker to bake bread just once each harvest, but} \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/248488]{you may use all of your ovens and other improvements to bake as much bread as you can.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Master Builder}{Baumeister}{E151}{(1--5 players)}
{Once during the game, at any time after your home reaches at least 5 rooms, you may extend it by 1 room at no cost.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx[Mason]{You may place a room tile on this card to show that you have not yet taken the extension action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3496604]{You do not have to use an action space to build a room with the Master Builder.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Berry Picker}{Beerensammler}{E152}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use a \changed{person}'s action to take wood, \changed{you receive} an additional 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which wood is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no wood (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}).}
\item \ecp{Is activated even if you leave all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space that contains wood because of the Wood Distributor.}
\item \ecp{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games, and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take wood.}
\item \apx{Is activated when you play \cardref{Building Material}{Baumaterial}{E16}.} \ecp{Is not activated when you receive wood because of any other minor improvement or an occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mendicant}{Bettelm—nch}{E153}{(1--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you can discard up to 2 begging cards without losing points for them.}

\card{Master Brewer}{Braumeister}{E154}{(1--5 players)}
{In the feeding phase of each harvest, the Master Brewer can convert up to 1 grain to 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Brewing beer does not count as baking.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3651107]{The grain that you want to convert into 3 food may not be on fields; it must be taken from your personal supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bread Seller}{Brotverkðufer}{E155}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive 1 food from the \changed{general} supply for each grain that is baked whenever any player (including yourself) bakes bread.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Bread is not baked if schnaps is distilled or beer is brewed, or when a \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17} or \cardref{Hand Mill}{Handm■hle}{I75} is used.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when any player uses a baking improvement (with the ``baking'' symbol) to convert grain to food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/382609]{Is not activated if anybody uses the \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} action space, but does not bake.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Brush Maker}{B■rstenbinder}{E156}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you convert wild boar to food, you \changed{place} the boar on this card. At the end of the game, you receive bonus points if you have wild boar markers on this card: {4 or more markers, 3 points; 3 markers, 2 points; 2 markers, 1 point}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item A converted wild boar may either be placed on the \cardref{Tanner}{Gerber}{K280}, \ecp{\cardref{Taxidermist}{Prðparator}{Z330}}, or Brush Maker; you cannot use two of these cards for the same animal.
\item If you also have the \cardref{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273} \ecp{and/or the \cardref{Pelts}{Tierfelle}{K339},} you may use those cards as well as the Brush Maker for each converted wild boar.
\item \ecp{Wild boar markers on this card do not count in the scoring at the end of the game.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Thatcher}{Dachdecker}{E157}{(3--5 players)}
{Pay 1 reed less to build each room, for each renovation, and for each of the \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103}, \cardref{Half-timbered House}{Fachwerkhaus}{E21}, \cardref{Chicken Coop}{H■hnerstall}{I84}, \cardref{Holiday House}{Ferienh■tte}{I71}, \cardref{Mansion}{Villa}{K144} and \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room.}
\item \ecp{If you also have other cards that reduce costs for building rooms, e.g.\ the \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91}, you may use all of these cards for the same action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3456758]{The Thatcher has no effect if the number of reeds required is already lowered to 0, e.g.\ by using both \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36} and \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272} when building a new room.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Turner}{Drechsler}{E158}{(3--5 players)}
{At any time, you can use the Turner to convert any number of wood to 1 food each.}

\card{Head of the Family}{Familienoberhaupt}{E159}{(4--5 players)}
{You can use any \changed{room building} or family growth action space, even if another player has already placed a person on it.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may not use the same action space in the same round with 2 of your own people.}
\item \ecp{If the action space provides a choice of actions, you may choose either. For example,} \apx[2nd ed]{you may take the ``Traveling Players'' action on the \actionref{Build 1 Room or Traveling Players}{BuildX1XRoomXorXTravelingXPlayers} action space in the 5-player game,} \ecp{or play an occupation on the \actionref{1 Occupation or Family Growth}{1XOccupationXorXFamilyXGrowth} action space.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/359723]{It is not allowed to use an empty accumulating action such as ``Traveling Players'', not even if it activates other improvements or occupations.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}{(4--5 players)}
{The next time you build fences, \changed{you receive} 1 wild boar. Each time you build at least 1 fence after that, \changed{you receive} 1 cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You only receive 1 new animal \ecp{per turn}, even if several pastures are created with the same action.}
\item Is activated when you use the \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}, or when you play the \cardref{Mini Pasture}{Miniweide}{E40}.
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fisherman}{Fischer}{E161}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, you can choose to take twice as many food as is on the space. If you do this, you must give 1 food each to \changed{the owners of} the \cardref{Fishing Rod}{Angel}{E12}, \cardref{Raft}{FloÔ}{E22}, \cardref{Canoe}{Kanu}{E30}, \cardref{Fish Trap}{Reuse}{I95}, and \cardref{Landing Net}{Kescher}{K126}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/332535]{Only the food that is lying on the action space is doubled. Take the food from the action space, and the same amount from the general supply.}
\item \ecp{You only give food to another player if he has the improvement in front of him on the table.}
\item \ecp{If a player has played more than one of these improvements, you give him more than one food.}
\item \ecp{You do not have to pay anything for an item if you own it yourself.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{It is possible that you have to pay more food than you receive.} \ecp{If you won't have enough food to pay the owners of the improvements after using the Fisherman, you are not allowed to use it.}
\item \ecp{The effect of the Fisherman is optional. If you do not take the double amount of food, you do not have to pay anything to the other players.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{Is not activated by using the \cardref{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}{(1--5 players)}
{If you have an oven, you can \changed{convert} your animals into food at any time. Take 2 food for each sheep, 3 for each wild boar and 4 for each cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The Meat Seller may not be used after upgrading an oven to a \cardref{Baker's Kitchen}{Backstube}{I65} or \cardref{Bakehouse}{Backhaus}{K106},} \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/282344]{unless you have another oven.}
\item \ecp{You can cook animals that come directly from an action space, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ecp{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\item \ecp{Ovens are not a cooking improvement, even if you have the Meat Seller. Using the Meat Seller does not activate the \cardref{Schnitzel Mallet}{Schnitzelklopfer}{ø18}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Field Warden}{Flursch■tze}{E163}{(4--5 players)}
{You can use the \actionref{Take 1 Vegetable}{TakeX1XVegetable}, \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} and \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} \changed{action spaces} even if another player has already placed a person on the space.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may not use the same action space in the same round with 2 of your own people.}% see Familienoberhaupt in appendix
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/410794]{You can use the Field Warden when you move a family member to the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} space because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Master Forester}{Forstwirt}{E164}{(4--5 players)}
{Include the \actionref{2 Wood}{2XWood} action card from the 3-player game as an additional forest. At the start of each round, place 2 wood on the card. Any player who uses this \changed{action space} must pay you 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you use the Master Forester yourself, you do not need to have or to pay any food.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335955]{The food must be paid before the wood is collected. If the player who wants the wood gets food for this action, for example because of the \cardref{Berry Picker}{Beerensammler}{E152}, he may not use this food to pay for the Master Forester.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Yeoman Farmer}{Freibauer}{E165}{(3--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you only lose points for unused \changed{farmyard} spaces and begging cards.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Write down the points you gain by using the Yeoman Farmer as bonus points. The number of bonus points you get is equal to the number of scoring categories for which you would otherwise have scored negative points.}
\item \ecp{Negative points that are compensated by the Yeoman Farmer are not counted as negative for the \cardref{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276}.}
\item \ecp{If you use the \cardref{Horse}{Pferd}{K135} to compensate for a missing type of animals, you still receive a bonus point for that animal from the Yeoman Farmer (and 2 bonus points from the Horse).}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{The Yeoman Farmer also compensates negative (bonus) points for \cardref{Forest Path}{Waldweg}{M048}, \cardref{Built-in Oven}{Ofenanlage}{M044}, etc.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Undergardener}{Gartenarbeiter}{E166}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, you also receive 1 vegetable.}

\card{Conjurer}{Gaukler}{E167}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the ``Traveling Players'' action on an action space, you receive \changed{1 additional grain}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext[Jongleur]{If another player uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} with a ``Traveling Players'' action, he pays you 1 food.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Greengrocer}{Gem■sehðndler}{E168}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} action space, you also receive 1 vegetable.}

\card{Storyteller}{Geschichtenerzðhler}{E169}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the ``Traveling Players'' action on an action space, you can leave 1 food on the space and \changed{receive} 1 vegetable instead.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext[Jongleur]{If another player uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} with a ``Traveling Players'' action, he pays you 1 food.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/307781]{If you have the \cardref{Dancer}{Tðnzer}{E212} as well, you receive at least 4 food and 1 vegetable when you leave one food on the action space.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Estate Manager}{Gutsverwalter}{E170}{(3--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive bonus points, \changed{if for none of the three animal species, any other player has more animals than you: in a 3 player game, 2 points; in a 4 player game, 3 points; in a 5 player game, 4 points.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2647802]{If a player has the \cardref{Horse}{Pferd}{K135}, it does not count as 1 animal of a missing type of his choice when counting animals for the Estate Manager. The \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120} does not count as an animal.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Dock Worker}{Hafenarbeiter}{E171}{(1--5 players)}
{At any time, you can use the Dock Worker to convert 3 wood to either 1 clay, 1 reed or 1 stone, or to convert 2 clay, 2 reed or 2 stone to 1 other building resource.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172}{(1--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each room in your stone house. Playing this card costs an additional 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you have the \cardref{Half-timbered House}{Fachwerkhaus}{E21} as well, you use both to get 4 points per room; if you have the \cardref{Mansion}{Villa}{K144} as well, or all three of Chief, Mansion and Half-timbered House, you use them all to get 5 points per room.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Chief's Daughter}{Hðuptlingstochter}{E173}{(1--5 players)}
{If another player plays the \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172} card, you can play this card immediately at no cost. At the end of the game, you receive 3 bonus points if you have a stone house, 1 if you have a clay hut.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can also play this card using an action space in the usual way.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/308267]{If you play the \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172} yourself, you may not play the Chief's Daughter at the same time.}
\item \ecp{In a solo game, you can only play this card using an action space.}
\item If you have the \cardref{Clogs}{Holzpantoffel}{E28} as well, you get points for both cards.
\item \ecp{If you play the Chief's Daughter because the Chief is played, this activates the \cardref{Bread Paddle}{Brotschieber}{K111}, \cardref{Bookshelf}{B■cherregal}{K112}, \cardref{Patron}{Mðzen}{E192}, and \cardref{Educator}{Ausbilder}{K271}, but not the \cardref{Writing Desk}{Schreibpult}{E49}, \cardref{Perpetual Student}{Bummelstudent}{K275}, or \cardref{Therapist}{Therapeut}{ø03}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Tutor}{Hauslehrer}{E174}{(1--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each occupation that you play after this one.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may note the bonus points on the scoring pad immediately, or you can simply lay out your occupations in the order that you play them.
\item \cardtext[Academic]{The \cardref{Academic}{Akademiker}{E148} counts as two occupations.}
\item \ecp{If you keep this card after playing a round in a series of solo games, you also receive bonus points for permanent occupation cards kept in play after subsequent games.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you build at least 1 fence, you can build 3 additional fences without paying any additional wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}, \cardref{Fence Builder}{Zaunaufsteller}{I263} or \cardref{Fence Deliveryman}{Zaunlieferant}{I265},} \ecp{or when you play the \cardref{Mini Pasture}{Miniweide}{E40}.}
\item \apx{If you also have the \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}, \cardref{Wood Carver}{Schnitzer}{K301} or \cardref{Sawhorse}{Holzbock}{K121}, you may use all of those cards during the same fence building action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/459498]{The free fences from the Hedge Keeper are built in the same fence building action as all other fences, but in an order of your choosing. However, you may not use the Hedge Keeper for the first fence you build in a turn.}
\item \ecp[http://www.trictrac.net/jeux/forum/viewtopic.php?t=54699]{Can only be used once per turn.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{Only after building the extra fences, you need to follow the conditions for building fences (i.e.\ no open pastures).}% http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=702.0
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335574]{You may choose to build fewer than 3 fences, for example, if you do not have 3 unbuilt fences left.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335574]{If you build no free fences, or fewer than 3, you cannot save the other free fences for later rounds.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Woodcutter}{Holzfðller}{E176}{(1--5 players)}
{You receive 1 additional wood whenever you use a \changed{person}'s action to take wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which wood is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no wood (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}).}
\item \ecp{Is activated even if you leave all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space that contains wood because of the Wood Distributor.}
\item \apx{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games,} \ecp{and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take wood.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1099]{Is not activated when you receive wood because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wooden Hut Builder}{Holzh■ttenbauer}{E177}{(3--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each room in your wooden hut.}

\card{Hut Builder}{H■ttenbauer}{E178}{(4--5 players)}
{Play this card during \changed{round 1--4}. At the start of round 11, you can extend your hut by 1 room at no cost, as long as you have not yet renovated to a stone house.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{When the card is played, put a room tile on the round 11 action space as a reminder.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2409]{It is allowed to play this card after round 4, in which case it has no effect. It still counts as a played occupation, e.g.\ for the prerequisite of an improvement.}
