\item \ecp{If you choose not to build a free room at the start of round 11, you cannot build it later in the game.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Merchant}{Kaufmann}{E179}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use a ``minor improvement'' or ``minor or major improvement'' action, you can pay 1 food to use the action a second time.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you use a ``major or minor improvement'' action, you can either play 2 major or 2 minor improvements, or 1 major and 1 minor improvement.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/366476]{Is activated by every improvement you play, even if you play several in a single turn.}
\item \apx{Using both Merchant and \cardref{Traveling Salesman}{Handelsreisender}{K281}, you can play up to 4 minor improvements for 1 food on a ``major or minor improvement'' action space, or you can acquire 2 major improvements for 1 food on a ``minor improvement'' action space.}
\item \apx{Using both Merchant and \cardref{Businessman}{Geschðftsmann}{I228}, you can first play 1 minor improvement and 1 major or minor improvement, and then additionally for 1 food, either 2 minor improvements or 1 major and 1 minor improvement when you use the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space.}\comment{Old appendix: Using both Merchant and \cardref{Businessman}{Geschðftsmann}{I228}, you can first 1 minor improvement and then additionally, for 1 food, 2 major or 2 minor improvements may be played using the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space.}
\item \ecp[http://boardgamegeek.com/thread/346984]{If you receive goods or food from the first improvement, you may use them to pay for the use of the merchant, or for buying the second improvement.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Scholar}{Gelehrter}{K279} to play an improvement.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hobby Farmer}{Kleingðrtner}{E180}{(4--5 players)}
{When you play this card, \changed{you receive} 1 vegetable that you may sow immediately if you have an empty plowed field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You perform a sowing action, which you can only use for this vegetable.
\item \ecp{Sowing the vegetable activates the \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}, \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}, \cardref{Potato Dibber}{Kartoffelstecher}{E32}, \cardref{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}, \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90} and another player's \cardref{Field Worker}{Feldarbeiter}{I224}.}
\item \ecp{Sowing the vegetable is optional. You may not sow anything else, including wood on \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278} and \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, or food on \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2035]{You may sow the vegetable on the \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}, or \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cook}{Koch}{E181}{(4--5 players)}
{In the feeding phase of each harvest, only 2 of your people eat 2 food each; all others are satisfied with only 1 food \changed{each}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/501986]{You still need to feed newborns with 1 food.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Charcoal Burner}{K—hler}{E182}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive 1 food and 1 wood whenever any player (including you) builds a baking improvement with a ``baking'' symbol.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You can place 1 food and 1 wood on the affected unbuilt major improvements to remind you to take the tokens.}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=683]{You also receive the food and wood when an improvement is upgraded to a baking improvement.}% also http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3003938
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Basketmaker}{Korbflechter}{E183}{(4--5 players)}
{In each harvest, the Basketmaker can convert up to 1 reed to 3 food.}

\card{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184}{(1--5 players)}
{Pile (from bottom to top) 1 vegetable, reed, clay, wood, vegetable, stone, grain, reed on this card. At any time, you may buy the top item for 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/504943]{The resources come from the general supply, and are not part of your personal supply until you buy them.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Firer}{Lehmbrenner}{E185}{(4--5 players)}
{You can use the Clay Firer at any time to convert \changed{2 clay to 1 stone or 3 clay to 2 stone}.}

\card{Clay Seller}{Lehmhðndler}{E186}{(4--5 players)}
{You can use the Clay Seller at any time to convert 2 clay to 1 sheep or 1 reed, 3 clay to 1 wild boar or 1 stone, and/or 4 clay to 1 cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you receive animals from the Clay Seller, you may convert them to food with an appropriate improvement without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Deliveryman}{Lehmlieferant}{E187}{(1--5 players)}
{Place 1 clay on \changed[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1621]{each remaining space} for rounds 6 to 14. At the start of these rounds, you receive the clay.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You do not receive clay for the current round, or any of the earlier rounds.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Mixer}{Lehmmischer}{E188}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever \changed{you take only clay with} one of your people's actions, you receive 2 additional clay.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which clay is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no clay (e.g.\ when you have the \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}).}
\item \ecp{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take clay.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you receive clay because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you take clay from an action space, and at the same time receive other goods because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Lord of the Manor}{Lehnsherr}{E189}{(1--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each scoring category where you have scored the maximum 4 points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The bonus point is also awarded for 4 fenced stables.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368121]{Bonus points from other cards, such as the \cardref{Brewery}{Brauerei}{K110} or the \cardref{Schnaps Distillery}{Schnapsbrennerei}{I98}, are not taken into account when scoring the \cardref{Lord of the Manor}{Lehnsherr}{E189}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Maid}{Magd}{E190}{(1--5 players)}
{Once you have built a clay hut, place 1 food on each remaining round space. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you already have a clay hut or a stone house when you play this card, place the food immediately.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mason}{Maurer}{E191}{(1--5 players)}
{Once during the game, at any time after your stone house reaches at least 4 rooms, you may extend it by 1 room at no cost.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may place a room tile on this card to show that you have not yet taken the extension action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3496604]{You do not have to use an action space to build a room with the Mason.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Patron}{Mðzen}{E192}{(4--5 players)}
{In future, whenever you play an occupation, you receive 2 food before you pay the costs of the occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/231808]{If you use the \cardref{Writing Desk}{Schreibpult}{E49}, you receive food for both occupations you play.}
\item \apx[B■cherregal]{If you also have the \cardref{Bookshelf}{B■cherregal}{K112}, you can use both to receive 5 food for each occupation you play.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pastor}{Pfarrer}{E193}{(4--5 players)}
{If, when you play this card or later in the game, you are the last player to have only 2 rooms in your home, you receive 3 wood, 2 clay, 1 reed and 1 stone.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You choose the moment at which you're paid, but it has to be after the last player (other than you) build his third room and before you build your third room yourself.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Plough Driver}{Pflughalter}{E194}{(1--5 players)}
{Once you have a stone house, you can pay 1 food at the start of each round to plough (at most) 1 field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item When you use the Plough Driver, you may not use a plough or the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68} to plough multiple fields.
\item \ecp{Food that you receive at the start of a round (e.g. because of the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10}) can be used to pay for the field immediately.}% Compare Scholar
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Plough Maker}{Pflugmacher}{E195}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use either of the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} or \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action spaces, you can pay 1 food to plough 1 additional field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may use one of the ploughs or the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68} at the same time as the Plough Maker (unlike the \cardref{Plough Driver}{Pflughalter}{E194}); in that case, you pay 1 food to plough 1 field more than the plough or Harrow allows.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use a person's action to take wood \changed{that is lying on an action space}, you can leave 1 of \changed{that} wood on the space and \changed{receive} 2 food in exchange.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, you can use both cards to leave 3 wood to receive 5 food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/451697]{You can use an action space with only 1 wood on it, and only take 2 food (and no wood). This still counts as taking wood, and activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Berry Picker}{Beerensammler}{E152}, \cardref{Wood Cart}{Holzfuhre}{I79}, and \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}.}
\item \ecp{If there is no wood on the action space, for example because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}, you may not use the Mushroom Collector.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space that contains wood because of the Wood Distributor.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/507803]{Is not activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Braggart}{Prahler}{E197}{(3--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive bonus points for the number of improvements in front of you: \changed{for 9 or more improvements, 9 points; for 8 improvements, 7 points; for 7 improvements, 5 points; for 6 improvements, 3 points; for 5 improvements, 1 point.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Both major and minor improvements count. Discarded improvements do not.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ratcatcher}{Rattenfðnger}{E198}{(3--5 players)}
{In rounds 10 and 12, all other players may not place 1 of their family's offspring (if they have any). This card may only be played until the end of Round 9.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The idle family members do count towards the question whether there is space in the hut or house for family growth.}
\item \cardtext{You yourself may place all your family members.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=680.0]{All family members except for the first two are offspring; not only newborns.}
\item \ecp{Guests and the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} are not offspring and may always be played.}
\item \ecp{You are allowed to play this card after round 9, but it has no effect. Remove it from the game immediately after you've played it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Renovator}{Renovator}{E199}{(1--5 players)}
{Pay 2 less clay to renovate to a clay hut, and pay 2 less stone to renovate to a stone house.}

\card{Conservator}{Restaurator}{E200}{(1--5 players)}
{You can renovate your wooden hut to a stone house without first needing to renovate it to a clay hut.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may not use both the Conservator and the \cardref{Stone Breaker}{Steinklopfer}{K303} \ecp{or the Conservator and the \cardref{Builder's Trowel}{Spachtel}{E50}} to renovate your wooden hut to a stone house out of turn.}
\item \apx{The renovation is paid, as usual, with 1 stone per room plus 1 reed,} \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3078423]{and you still have to take a ``Renovate'' action to use the Conservator.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Clay Hut Builder}{Lehmh■ttenbauer}{I242} when used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cattle Whisperer}{Rinderfl■sterer}{E201}{(4--5 players)}
{Add 5 and 9 to \changed{the number of} the current round. Place 1 cattle on each corresponding round space. At the start of these rounds, you receive the cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=711.0]{If this card is already in play at the start of a solo game, the current round number is 0. You receive the cattle on rounds 5 and 9.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Seasonal Worker}{Saisonarbeiter}{E202}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, you receive 1 additional grain. From round 6 \changed{onwards}, you can choose to receive 1 vegetable instead.}

\card{Shepherd}{Schðfer}{E203}{(4--5 players)}
{During each harvest, if you have at least 4 sheep during the breeding phase, you receive 2 lambs instead of 1 as long as you have room for them.}

\card{Master Shepherd}{Schafmeister}{E204}{(4--5 players)}
{Place 1 sheep on each of the next 3 round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the sheep.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animal into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reed Collector}{Schilfsammler}{E205}{(3--5 players)}
{Place 1 reed on the next 4 round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the reed.}

\card{Swineherd}{Schweinehirt}{E206}{(4--5 players)}
{\changed{Whenever you use the \actionref{1 Wild Boar}{1XWildXBoar} action space, you receive 1 additional wild boar from the general supply.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The \actionref{1 Wild Boar}{1XWildXBoar} action space is added in round 8 or 9.
\item \ecp{In the 5-player game, there is an action space that gives players 1 animal of their choice. The Swineherd is not activated by using this space.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you build at least 1 fence, you also receive 1 stable which you must build immediately.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The stable may be built inside or outside the fenced area.}
\item You do not need to pay any wood for the stable.
\item \apx[Miniweide]{Is activated when you play the \cardref{Mini Pasture}{Miniweide}{E40}.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=895.0]{Only 1 free stable is awarded in each turn.}% Contradicts the Appendix, under Zaunaufseher ("once per ROUND")
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}: when you build a stable, you may fence it, after which you have to build another stable. You may not then fence that second stable.}
\item Activates the Fence Overseer when used: when you build a fence, you must build 1 free stable, which can be fenced for free. You may not use the Stablehand again to receive a second free stable.
\item \ecp{If you have no unbuilt stables left, or if there is no place in your farmyard where it can be placed, the Stablehand has no effect.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/339668]{If you use the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, the additional 3 fences do not activate the Stablehand a second time.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stablemaster}{Stallmeister}{E208}{(1--5 players)}
{One (and only one) of your unfenced stables may hold up to 3 animals of the same type.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you also have the \cardref{Shepherd's Pipe}{Hornfl—te}{E29}, that card has no effect on the unfenced stable for which the Stablemaster is used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Quarryman}{Steinhauer}{E209}{(3--5 players)}
{You can use the Quarryman at any time to convert stone to food. For each stone you convert, \changed{you receive} 2 food.}

\card{Stone Carrier}{Steinschlepper}{E210}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you take stone with an action \changed{of a person}, you can also take 1 additional stone. If you also receive other building resources, this costs you 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which stone is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no stone (e.g.\ when you have the \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}.)}
\item \ecp{Is activated by the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take stone.}
\item \ecp{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games and the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood} in 4-player games, if you pay 1 food.}
\item \ecp{You also pay 1 food to use this card if you receive other building resources at the same time from occupations and minor improvements.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you receive stone because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Other building resources are wood, clay, and reed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stonecutter}{Steinschneider}{E211}{(3--5 players)}
{All improvements, rooms and renovations cost \changed{you} 1 stone less.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item For example, you do not have to pay any stone if you play \cardref{Lumber}{Bauholz}{K107}.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2803227]{If you buy more than one room, you receive the discount for all rooms. If you renovate, you only get a discount of 1 stone, no matter how many rooms your house has.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of an improvement, room or renovation together with the Stonecutter for the same action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Dancer}{Tðnzer}{E212}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the ``Traveling Players'' action on an action space, you receive at least 4 food, \changed{even if only 1 to 3 food are on the space}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext[Jongleur]{If another player uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} with a ``Traveling Players'' action, he pays you 1 food.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{If you have the \cardref{Storyteller}{Geschichtenerzðhler}{E169} as well, you receive at least 4 food and 1 vegetable when you leave one food on the action space.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/307781
\item \apx[2nd ed]{You cannot use both the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} and the Dancer for the same action.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/307781
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stockman}{Tierpfleger}{E213}{(4--5 players)}
{You receive 1 cattle when you build your second stable, 1 wild boar when you build your third and 1 sheep when you build your fourth.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you build several stables at once, you may receive more than one animal.
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/304474]{You do not get animals for stables that have already been built when you play the Stockman.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animal into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Potter}{T—pfer}{E214}{(3--5 players)}
{In each harvest, the Potter can convert up to 1 clay to 2 food.}

\card{Tenant Farmer}{Viehpðchter}{E215}{(4--5 players)}
{You immediately receive a loan of one of each type of animal. Before scoring, return the 3 animals. For each animal that you cannot or do not want to return, you lose 1 point.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals to food with an appropriate improvement without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/297050]{If you also have the \cardref{Yeoman Farmer}{Freibauer}{E165}, you do not deduct points if you do not return an animal.}
\item \ecp{If you deduct points for not returning an animal, you do not get the bonus points from the \cardref{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276}.}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Animal Feed}{Tierfutter}{I101}, you may use the animals from the Animal Feed to repay your loan, even if you have no space in your farm to keep them.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1191]{You may repay the loan at any time before the scoring, including during the game. If you repay part of the loan during the game, you may no longer repay the rest of the loan later in the game or before scoring.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Keeper}{Viehwðrter}{E216}{(4--5 players)}
{You can keep sheep, wild boar and cattle in the same pasture.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item This applies to all your pastures except the \cardref{Forest Pasture}{Waldweide}{K145}.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reeve}{Vogt}{E217}{(3--5 players)}
{\changed{You receive wood immediately when you play this card: if played in round 12 or 13, take 1 wood; if played in round 9, 10, or 11, take 2 wood; if played in round 6, 7, or 8, take 3 wood; if played before round 6, take 4 wood.} At the end of the game, all players with the most occupation cards \changed{in front of them} receive 3 bonus points each.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The \cardref{Academic}{Akademiker}{E148} counts as two occupations.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Carpenter}{Zimmermann}{E218}{(1--5 players)}
{To extend your home, you need only 3 of the appropriate resource and 2 reed for each new room.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{For example, if you live in a wooden hut, you need 3 wood and 2 reed.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room.}
\item \apx{This card sets a new base cost for a room. If you also have another card that sets a new base cost (e.g.\ \cardref{Clay Supports}{Lehmstake}{E37}, \cardref{Axe}{Axt}{E13}, or \cardref{Clay Plasterer}{Lehmdecker}{I241}), you may only use one such card at the same time.} \ecp{If you build more than one room, you can choose the same or a different card for each room.}
\item \ecp{After you've used the Carpenter, you may then also use any card that changes the cost of a room (e.g.\ \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36}, \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91}, \cardref{Stonecutter}{Steinschneider}{E211}, and \cardref{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243}).}
\item \ruling[http://boardgamegeek.com/thread/346260]{For example, if you also have the \cardref{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243}, you may use both cards to build rooms for 1 clay and 2 reed.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{You may not use this card to change the costs of the \cardref{Wooden Hut Extension}{Holzh■ttenanbau}{I81} and \cardref{Clay Hut Extension}{Lehmh■ttenanbau}{K132}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you sow 1 field, place 2 additional goods \changed{of the same type} from the \changed{general} supply on the stack. Whenever you sow 2 fields, place 1 extra good on each.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you sow three or more fields, you do not get any additional goods.}
\item \apx{You also get the extra goods if planting on the \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}, \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137}, \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105},} \ecp{and \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}.}
\item \apx{The Acreage counts as two fields if both fields of the Acreage are planted.} \apx[F—rster]{The Forester counts as up to three fields.} \ecp{If you use the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324} to sow a field twice, it counts as two fields.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Hobby Farmer}{Kleingðrtner}{E180} or the \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Well Builder}{Brunnenbauer}{I220}{(1--5 players)}
{For you, the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10} is \changed[not a major but]{now} a minor improvement and costs only 1 stone and 1 wood to build.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{After the upgrade to the \cardref{Village Well}{Dorfbrunnen}{I66}, the Well may be built a second time. The benefits of the Well Builder apply both times.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/497755]{The Well still counts as major improvement as well, e.g.\ for \cardref{Nosebag}{-}{M022} or \cardref{Administration}{-}{M070}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Village Elder}{Dorfðltester}{I221}{(3--5 players)}
{\changed{You receive wood immediately when you play this card: if played in round 12 or 13, take 1 wood; if played in round 9, 10, or 11, take 2 wood; if played in round 6, 7, or 8, take 3 wood; if played before round 6, take 4 wood.} At the end of the game, all players with the most improvements \changed{in front of them} receive 3 bonus points each.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Both major and minor improvements count. Discarded improvements do not.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Social Climber}{Empork—mmling}{I222}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you are the first player to renovate to a clay hut or a stone house, you receive 3 stone. If you are the second, you receive 2 stone; the third, you receive 1 stone.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Rewards are not given for renovations performed before you played this card.}
\item \apx{You receive the stone immediately after renovating, so you can use them immediately for the following small improvement.} \ecp{You cannot use the stone for the renovation itself.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1675]{If you use the \cardref{Conservator}{Restaurator}{E200} to renovate directly to stone, you do not receive stone for the renovation to a clay hut. If you renovate to a clay hut after another player has used the Conservator, he does not count as having renovated to clay before you.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Harvest Helper}{Erntehelfer}{I223}{(3--5 players)}
{At the start of the feeding phase in each harvest, you can take 1 grain from 1 field belonging to another player. That player \changed{receives} 2 food from the \changed{general} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You may not take an additional grain from one of your own fields.}
\item \apx{You may take the grain from another player's \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105} minor improvement.}
\item \apx{The Harvest Helper is used after the \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}.}
\item \ecp{You decide which of the opponents' fields to take the grain from, including \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105}, the opponent's home (if he has \cardref{Winter Garden}{-}{G118}, and his farmyard (if he has \cardref{No-Till Farming}{-}{M078}).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Field Worker}{Feldarbeiter}{I224}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player sows one or more fields, you receive 1 grain in a 3-player game or 1 food in a 4 or 5 player game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you sow, you do not get anything from the Field Worker.
\item \apx{Is activated when another player uses the \cardref{Hobby Farmer}{Kleingðrtner}{E180} or the \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Field Watchman}{Feldh■ter}{I225}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the action space \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain}, you can also plough up to 1 field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You cannot use ploughs or the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68} when this card is used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Gardener}{Gðrtner}{I226}{(1--5 players)}
{Take vegetables from the \changed{general} supply and not from your vegetable field whenever you harvest them --- you keep the vegetables on the fields.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{All your vegetable fields remain untouched until the end of the game. This also applies to the \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} and \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47}.}
\item \ecp{The effect of the Gardener is not optional.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}{(1--5 players)}
{\changed{You receive wood immediately when you play this card: if played in round 12 or 13, take 1 wood; if played in round 9, 10, or 11, take 2 wood; if played in round 6, 7, or 8, take 3 wood; if played before round 6, take 4 wood.} At the end of the game, any player who performed actions with at least 5 people in round 14 receives 3 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{An action by a guest is counted.} \ecp{An additional action because of moving an already placed person, e.g. because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}, is not.}
\item \apx{A player who only gets a 5th family member in round 14 does not receive the bonus points,} \ecp{unless the new family member takes an action that round because of the \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267}.}
\item \ecp{A player who has built the \cardref{Holiday House}{Ferienh■tte}{I71} does not receive bonus points for the Church Warden.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Businessman}{Geschðftsmann}{I228}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space, you can play an additional minor or major improvement after you play the minor improvement.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Optional; can only be used once per turn.}
\item \apx{Using both Businessman and \cardref{Traveling Salesman}{Handelsreisender}{K281}, you can play up to 3 minor improvements one after another when you use the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space.}
\item \apx{Using both Businessman and \cardref{Merchant}{Kaufmann}{E179}, you can first play 1 minor improvement and 1 major or minor improvement, and then additionally for 1 food, either 2 minor improvements or 1 major and 1 minor improvement when you use the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space.}\comment{Old appendix: Using both Merchant and \cardref{Businessman}{Geschðftsmann}{I228}, you can first 1 minor improvement and then additionally, for 1 food, 2 major or 2 minor improvements may be played using the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space.}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=719]{You may not play a major improvement without playing a minor improvement.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sycophant}{Getreideschmuser}{I229}{(4--5 players)}
{Any other player that uses the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} action space must first pay you 1 food. In addition, you receive 1 food from the \changed{general} supply. \changed{You receive that food even when you take the grain yourself.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Note that there are enough cards in the interactive deck that the other players can use to avoid the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} action space.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/337589]{The food has to be paid before using the action space; if a player has no food to pay before taking the grain, he cannot use the action space. He cannot take a begging card to get 1 food.}% also http://www.trictrac.net/jeux/forum/viewtopic.php?t=63009
\item \ecp{You do not have to pay anything if you use the action space yourself.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Digger}{Gruber}{I230}{(4--5 players)}
{Include the \actionref{1 Clay}{1XClay} action card from the 3-player game as an additional clay pit. Immediately place 3 clay on the card and add 1 clay at the start of each round. Any player who uses this action must pay you 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you use the Clay Digger yourself, you do not need to have or to pay any food.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Manservant}{Hausknecht}{I231}{(1--5 players)}
{When you build a stone house, place 3 food on each remaining round space. At the start of these rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you already have a stone house when you play this card, place the food immediately.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Midwife}{Hebamme}{I232}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player \changed{has offspring and then} has a larger family than you, you receive 1 food. If they have at least 2 more family members than you, you receive 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The food is taken from the general supply, not from the other player.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when another player uses the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}, \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291}, or \cardref{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325}.}
\item \ecp{This card is not activated when another player gets a guest or plays the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138}.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{Guests \ecp{and the occupant of the Reed Hut} are not counted in the size of the families.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Farm Steward}{Hofverwalter}{I233}{(1--5 players)}
{Once you live in a clay hut or stone house, play your next family growth action as a ``family growth even without room''.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The next family growth is performed as if the round card from stage 5 was used. All future family growth is carried out as normal.}
\item \apx{Allows at most 1 family growth without space in the hut.}
\item \apx{If a room is built later, the offspring occupies it immediately.}
\item \ecp{If you already live in a clay hut or stone house, you use the Farm Steward for the first family growth action after you've played it.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=743.0]{If your next family growth is the \actionref{Family Growth and Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement} action space, you can play a minor improvement as usual.}
\item \ecp{If your next family growth action is \actionref{Family Growth without Room}{FamilyXGrowthXwithoutXRoom}, or when playing the \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291}, this card has no effect.}
\item \ecp{Using the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270} or \cardref{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325} counts as a family growth action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wood Buyer}{Holzaufkðufer}{I234}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player receives wood from an action, you can buy 1 wood from them for 1 food (even without their agreement).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368102]{You may buy only 1 wood each turn, but you can use this card multiple times per round.}
\item \ecp{The other player cannot refuse this exchange.}
\item \ecp{If the other player leaves all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, you cannot buy wood from him.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when a player uses an action space that contains wood because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}.}
\item \apx{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games,} \ecp{and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if the other player takes wood.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{Is not activated when another player receives wood because of a special action (\MOOR),} \ecp{minor improvement or occupation.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1160]{The wood still counts as ``taken'' for the other player; they can still use their \cardref{Berry Picker}{Beerensammler}{E152}, \cardref{Woodcutter}{Holzfðller}{E176}, \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}, etc., even if you buy the only wood that they take this turn. However, they cannot use their \cardref{Resource Seller}{Werkstoffhðndler}{K310}, because they do not ``receive'' the wood.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wood Collector}{Holzsammler}{I235}{(1--5 players)}
{Place 1 wood on each of the next 5 round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the wood.}

\card{Hide Farmer}{Hufenbauer}{I236}{(3--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you can pay 1 food each for any number of unused \changed{farmyard spaces}. These do not lose you points in the scoring.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Negative points that are compensated by the Hide Farmer are not counted as negative for the \cardref{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the ``Traveling Players'' action on an action space, you can choose to \changed{receive} twice as much food as is on the card. If you do this, you must give one food each to \changed{the owners of} the \cardref{Magician}{Zauberk■nstler}{K311}, \cardref{Conjurer}{Gaukler}{E167}, \cardref{Street Musician}{StraÔenmusikant}{I257}, \cardref{Puppeteer}{Puppenspieler}{I249}, \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}, \cardref{Dancer}{Tðnzer}{E212}, \changed{\cardref{Animal Trainer}{Dompteur}{K342}} and \cardref{Storyteller}{Geschichtenerzðhler}{E169}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/307781]{You cannot use both the Juggler and the \cardref{Dancer}{Tðnzer}{E212} for the same action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/332535]{Only the food that is lying on the action space is doubled. Take the food from the action space, and the same amount from the general supply.}
\item \ecp{You only give food to another player if he has the occupation in front of him on the table.}
\item \ecp{If a player has played more than one of these occupations, you give him more than one food.}
\item \ecp{You do not have to pay anything for an occupation if you own it yourself.}
\item \ecp{It is possible that you have to pay more food than you receive.}\comment{appendix, Fisherman}
\item \ecp{The effect of the Juggler is optional. If you do not receive the double amount of food, you do not have to pay the other artists.}
\item \ecp{If you would not have enough food to pay the other artists, you are not allowed to use the Juggler.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Chamberlain}{Kðmmerer}{I238}{(1--5 players)}
{At the start of round 11 (or immediately, if you play this card after the start of Round 11), turn over the round cards for the remaining rounds. You (and only you) can use these actions immediately; the other players must wait until the appropriate round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The order in which the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} and \actionref{Family Growth without Room}{FamilyXGrowthXwithoutXRoom} action spaces enter the game is determined by the Chamberlain immediately when they are turned over.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Corn Profiteer}{Kornschinder}{I239}{(4--5 players)}
{You can convert 1 grain to 3 food at any time. Any other player can \changed{prevent} this by buying the grain from you for 2 food. If more than one player wants to buy, you choose one of them.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Using the Corn Profiteer does not count as baking bread.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cowherd}{Kuhhirt}{I240}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{1 Cattle}{1XCattle} action space, you receive 1 additional cattle from the \changed{general} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The \actionref{1 Cattle}{1XCattle} action space is added in round 10 or 11.}
\item \apx{In the 5-player game, there is an action space that gives players 1 animal of their choice. The Cowherd is not activated by using this space.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Plasterer}{Lehmdecker}{I241}{(1--5 players)}
{Renovating your wooden hut to a clay hut costs you only 1 clay and 1 reeds. Each room of your clay hut costs you 3 clay and 2 reeds.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx[Lehmstake]{This card sets a new base cost for a room. If you also have another card that sets a new base cost (e.g.\ \cardref{Clay Supports}{Lehmstake}{E37}, and/or \cardref{Carpenter}{Zimmermann}{E218}), you may only use one such card at the same time.} \ecp{If you build more than one room, you can choose the same or a different card for each room.}
\item \ecp{After you've used the Clay Plasterer, you may then also use any card that changes the cost of a room (e.g.\ \cardref{Clay Roof}{Lehmdach}{E36}, \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91}, and \cardref{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243}).}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{You may not use this card to change the costs of the \cardref{Clay Hut Extension}{Lehmh■ttenanbau}{K132}.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=696.0]{For example, if you have the \cardref{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243} as well, you can use both to renovate to a clay hut for 1 reed and to build new clay rooms for 1 clay and 2 reeds.}% Contradicted by 2nd ed. appendix!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Hut Builder}{Lehmh■ttenbauer}{I242}{(1--5 players)}
{Once you live in a clay hut, place 2 clay on each of the next 5 round spaces. At the start of these rounds, you receive the clay.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you already live in a clay hut or a stone house when you play this card, place the clay on the round spaces immediately.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Conservator}{Restaurator}{E200} to renovate to a stone house.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243}{(1--5 players)}
{Pay 1 less clay for each improvement and renovation. Pay 2 less clay for each room.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/281875]{With e.g. \cardref{Helpful Neighbours}{Nachbarschaftshilfe}{E42} the player receives 1 stone or 1 reed for free.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=696.0]{If you also have the \cardref{Clay Plasterer}{Lehmdecker}{I241}, you can use both to renovate to a clay hut for 1 reed and to build new clay rooms for 1 clay and 2 reed;} \ruling[http://boardgamegeek.com/thread/346260]{you can use both the \cardref{Carpenter}{Zimmermann}{E218} and the Bricklayer to build rooms for 1 clay and 2 reed;} \ecp{or you can use both the \cardref{Clay Supports}{Lehmstake}{E37} and the Bricklayer to build rooms for 1 wood and 1 reed.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of an improvement, room or renovation together with the Bricklayer for the same action.}
\item \ecp{If a new room costs only 1 clay, e.g.\ after using the Clay Plasterer and the \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272}, the Bricklayer reduces the cost to 0.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1097]{The cost of the \cardref{Clay Hut Extension}{Lehmh■ttenanbau}{K132} is lowered by only 1 clay.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Layabout}{Lehnerich}{I244}{(1--5 players)}
{Once you have played this card, you may not take part in the next harvest.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You do not perform the actions of either the field phase or the breeding phase of the next harvest. Neither may you use cards that have effects at harvest time.
\item On the other hand, you do not need to feed your family during that harvest.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/501886]{Although you do not take part in the harvest, other players may still use your cards or interact with your farm, if you or they have a card that allows this, such as \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103} and \cardref{Harvest Helper}{Erntehelfer}{I223}. However, you may not use the Harvest Helper or another player's Water Mill yourself.}
\item \ecp{You can still receive food from the \cardref{Slaughterman}{Schlachter}{K299} or \cardref{Slaughterhouse}{Schlachthof}{I97}.}
\item \ecp{Using the \cardref{Manure}{Mist}{I92} or the \cardref{Almanac}{-}{G061} does not count as a harvest.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Market Crier}{Marktschreier}{I245}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} action space, you can take an additional 1 grain and 1 vegetable. If you do this, the other players each receive 1 grain from the \changed{general} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/497920]{Is not activated by \cardref{Corn Sheaf}{Korngarbe}{K129} or any other improvement or occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Milking Hand}{Melker}{I246}{(4--5 players)}
{In the field phase of the harvest, you receive food if you have cattle, without having to give up the cattle: \changed{for 5 or more cattle, 3 food; for 3 or 4 cattle, 2 food; for 1 cattle, 1 food}. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for every 2 cattle.}

\card{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}{(1--5 players)}
{You can \changed{convert} your animals into food at any time. \changed{You receive} 1 food for each sheep, 2 for each wild boar and 3 for each cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You do not need a cooking improvement to use the Butcher.}
\item \ecp{Using the Butcher does not activate the \cardref{Schnitzel Mallet}{Schnitzelklopfer}{ø18}.}
\item \ecp{You cannot convert animals into food during the breeding phase of the harvest. After the breeding phase of the last harvest, the game ends immediately; you can not convert the animals received in the last harvest to food at all.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248}{(1--5 players)}
{If one of your people uses an action space that \changed{directly} provides reeds, you can take all food from the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space in the returning home phase (phase 4).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{When you play a person on an action space with reeds, you stake your claim by placing a claim marker on the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1196]{If someone takes the food from \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} before the end of the round, you receive nothing.}% also http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=824
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=684.0]{Is not activated when you play the \cardref{Reed Exchange}{Schilftausch}{I96}} \ecp{or \cardref{Helpful Neighbours}{Nachbarschaftshilfe}{E42}, or use any other improvement to receive reeds, or when you use an occupation to get reeds.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{Collecting the food does not count as taking the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action, and does not activate the \cardref{Fisherman}{Fischer}{E161}, \cardref{Fishing Rod}{Angel}{E12}, \cardref{Fish Trap}{Reuse}{I95}, \cardref{Raft}{FloÔ}{E22}, or \cardref{Canoe}{Kanu}{E30}.}% http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=659.0
\item \ecp{You can not take other resources that may be on the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, e.g. because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/346270]{In the round in which you play this card, you may only claim the food on \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} if you take reed \emph{after} you play the Net Fisherman.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Puppeteer}{Puppenspieler}{I249}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player chooses the ``Traveling players'' action on an action space, you can pay 1 food to play an occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You pay the 1 food to the general supply.}
\item \apx{You may only play an occupation if you have food --- even if it would provide immediate food.}
\item \cardtext[Jongleur]{If the player who takes the ``Traveling players'' action uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237}, he pays you 1 food.} \ecp{You receive this food before you use the Puppeteer.}
\item \apx[Brotschieber]{Activates the \cardref{Bread Paddle}{Brotschieber}{K111} when used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sheep Whisperer}{Schaffl■sterer}{I250}{(4--5 players)}
{Add 4, 7, 9 and 11 to \changed{the number of} the current round and place 1 sheep on each corresponding round space. At the start of these rounds, you receive the sheep.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=711.0]{If this card is already in play at the start of a solo game, the current round number is 0. You receive the sheep in rounds 4, 7, 9, and 11.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animal into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Reed Buyer}{Schilfaufkðufer}{I251}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever reed is taken for the first time in a round, you may give the player who takes it 1 food in exchange for 1 of the reed. The other player receives an additional 1 food from the \changed{general} supply as compensation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The other player cannot refuse this exchange.}
\item \apx{If you are the first person to take reed in a round, you do not get any advantage from the Reed Buyer.}
\item \apx{The Reed Buyer cannot interfere when reed is taken for the second time in a round,} \ecp{not even when you took the first reed yourself.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when a player uses an action space on which reed is placed each round, the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood} in 4-player games.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when another player receives reed because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1160]{The reed still counts as ``taken'' for the other player; they can still use their \cardref{Landing Net}{Kescher}{K126}, \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}, \cardref{Fish Trap}{Reuse}{I95}, etc., even if you buy the only reed that they take this turn. However, they cannot use their \cardref{Resource Seller}{Werkstoffhðndler}{K310}, because they do not ``receive'' the reed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pig Breeder}{Schweinez■chter}{I252}{(4--5 players)}
{Your wild boar breed at the end of round 12, if there is room for the piglet. When you play this card, you receive 1 wild boar.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The wild boar you receive when you play this card may immediately be converted into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use a person to take wood that is on an action space, you can leave 2 of \changed{that} wood on the space and \changed{receive} a wild boar instead.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/239038]{If there is less than 2 wood on the action space, you may not use the Pig Catcher; not even when you receive additional wood from e.g. the \cardref{Wood Cart}{Holzfuhre}{I79}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/451697]{You can use an action space with only 2 wood on it, and only take the wild boar (and no wood). This still counts as taking wood, and activates e.g.\ the \cardref{Berry Picker}{Beerensammler}{E152}, Wood Cart, and \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space that contains wood because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the wild boar into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Groom}{Stallknecht}{I254}{(4--5 players)}
{Once you have a stone house, you can build 1 stable at the beginning of each round at a cost of 1 wood. You do not need to place a family member on an action space to do this.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Wood that you receive at the same time through a \cardref{Private Forest}{Privatforst}{E45}, \cardref{Wood Collector}{Holzsammler}{I235} or \cardref{Wood Deliveryman}{Holzlieferant}{K283} may be used immediately to build 1 stable.}
\item \apx[Zaunaufseher]{Activates the \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312} when used.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Buyer}{Steinaufkðufer}{I255}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever stone is taken for the first time in a round, you may give the player who takes it 1 food in exchange for 1 of the stone. The other player receives an additional 1 food from the \changed{general} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The other player cannot refuse this exchange.}
\item \apx{If you are the first player to take stone in a round, you do not get any advantage from the Stone Buyer.}
\item \apx{The Stone Buyer cannot interfere when stone is taken for the second or third time in a round,} \ecp{not even when you took the first reeds yourself.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when a player uses an action space on which stone is placed each round, the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood} in 4-player games, the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when another player receives stone because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1160]{The stone still counts as ``taken'' for the other player; they can still use their \cardref{Stone Carrier}{Steinschlepper}{E210}, \cardref{Storehouse Keeper}{Lagerverwalter}{K288}, \cardref{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}, etc., even if you buy the only stone that they take this turn. However, they cannot use their \cardref{Resource Seller}{Werkstoffhðndler}{K310}, because they do not ``receive'' the stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Carver}{Steinmetz}{I256}{(1--5 players)}
{In each harvest, the Stone Carver can convert up to 1 stone to 3 food.}

\card{Street Musician}{StraÔenmusikant}{I257}{(4--5 players)}
{You receive 1 grain whenever another player takes the ``Traveling Players'' action on an action space.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext[Jongleur]{If the player who takes the ``Traveling players'' action uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237}, he pays you 1 food.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cabinetmaker}{Tischler}{I258}{(3--5 players)}
{In each harvest, the Cabinetmaker can convert up to 1 wood to 2 food.}

\card{Animal Dealer}{Viehtreiber}{I259}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use one of the \changed{\actionref{1 Sheep}{1XSheep}, \actionref{1 Wild Boar}{1XWildXBoar} or \actionref{1 Cattle}{1XCattle}} action spaces, you can pay 1 food to take 1 additional animal of that type.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The \actionref{1 Sheep}{1XSheep}, \actionref{1 Wild Boar}{1XWildXBoar} and \actionref{1 Cattle}{1XCattle} cards are added in Rounds 1--4, 8--9 and 10--11.
\item \apx{In the 5-player game, there is an action space that gives players 1 animal of their choice. The Animal Dealer is not activated by using this space.}
\item \apx[Tierhalter]{After you've paid the 1 food, you may immediately convert the animal into food with an appropriate improvement. However, you must pay the 1 food beforehand; you may not subtract it from the proceeds.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Taster}{Vorkoster}{I260}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player is the starting player, you can pay them 1 food at the start of the round and be the first to place a family member. After that, play starts with the starting player as usual.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{For example, if your right-hand neighbour is the starting player, you may pay him 1 food and place the first person. The starting player then places the second person, and the third person is then played by you due to the normal flow of the game.}
\item \cardtext{If you are the starting player yourself, yo do not get any advantage.}
\item \apx{The \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}, \cardref{Foreman}{Vorarbeiter}{K308} and Taster may react to each other. A player who decides to use his occupation cannot take back their decision. A player who does not wish to use the occupation has until the start of the work phase (phase 3) to reconsider.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Outrider}{Vorreiter}{I261}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the most recent round card with one of your people, you receive 1 additional grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/337444]{You receive the grain before you've taken the action. For example, if you use a sowing action, you can immediately sow the grain from the Outrider.}
\item \ecp{The most recent round card is always the one corresponding to the current round, even if the \cardref{Chamberlain}{Kðmmerer}{I238} has been played.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Water Carrier}{Wassertrðger}{I262}{(1--5 players)}
{Once any player has built the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10}, place 1 food on the remaining round spaces. At the start of these Rounds, you receive the food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If the well has already been built, place the food immediately.}
\item \apx{Food is not distributed a second time when the Well is upgraded to the \cardref{Village Well}{Dorfbrunnen}{I66}. It is distributed again if the Well is built for a second time.} \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=705.0]{If the Well has already been upgraded to the Village Well and returned to the major improvements board, the food is nevertheless distributed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fence Builder}{Zaunaufsteller}{I263}{(1--5 players)}
{When you play this card, place one of your fences on an action space of your choice. If you use an action on this action space, you can also build fences as an additional action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{From now on, you have only 14 fences available for building.}
\item \ecp{You have to perform a regular action on the action space; fence building is optional,} \apx{and follows all other actions on the action space.}
\item \ecp{You may place the fence on any action space, including minor improvements that are action spaces (such as \cardref{Clay Deposit}{Lehmh■gel}{I337}), action spaces that have been introduced to the game by other cards (such as \cardref{Master Forester}{Forstwirt}{E164}), and \actionref{Infirmary}{Infirmary}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2036]{If you use an occupation action space to play the Fence Builder, and you place the fence on that occupation action space, you cannot use Fence Builder this turn to immediately build fences.}% Also http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/5520887#5520887
\item \ecp{You may not place the fence on a round space of a future round, unless the action card has already been revealed by the \cardref{Chamberlain}{Kðmmerer}{I238}.}
\item \apx{Pastures may only be built if they are completed --- you may not leave a pasture open.}
\item If you use the action space containing your fence, and you build fences, this activates the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207} and \cardref{Animal Breeder}{Tierz■chter}{K307}.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2830389]{If the action space with your fence is a space on which goods are placed at the start of each round, and it is empty (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}), you may not use the action space just to build fences.}
\item \ecp{If you put the fence on an action space that already allows the buiding of fences, you can take 2 fence building actions in 1 turn. This activates the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160}, \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}, or another player's \cardref{Fencer}{Zaunbauer}{I264} twice, as if the 2 fencing actions were taken in separate turns. The conditions for fence buildings (e.g.\ no open pastures) should be observed after each fencing action.}
\item \ecp{If you already have built all your fences when you play this card, it has no effect.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fencer}{Zaunbauer}{I264}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player builds 1 to 4 fences, you receive 1 wood from the \changed{general} supply. Whenever another player builds 5 or more fences, you receive 2 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you build fences yourself, you receive no benefit.}
\item \ecp{If another player builds fences twice with the same action, e.g. because of the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}, you get wood only once, based on the total number of fences built.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fence Deliveryman}{Zaunlieferant}{I265}{(1--5 players)}
{Add 6 and 10 to \changed{the number of} the current round. Place 4 of your fences on each corresponding round space. At the start of these rounds, you can pay 2 food to build all 4 fences immediately.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you have fewer than 8 unbuilt fences when you play this card, you place fewer than 4 fences on the latest of the two affected round spaces. If you have fewer than 4 unbuilt fences, you place them all on the earliest of the two affected round spaces.}
\item \apx{Fences may not be removed from the round space to build them in the usual way.}
\item \apx{You may build fewer than 4 fences, but you still pay 2 food if you build at least 1 fence. If you choose to build fewer than 4 fences, you return the leftover fences to your personal supply of unbuilt fences.}
\item \cardtext{You do not need to pay wood to build the fences.}
\item \apx{You may not leave a pasture open.}
\item \apx[Heckenwart]{Building the fences activates the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}.}
\item \ecp{Food that you receive at the start of a round can be used to pay for the fences immediately.}% Compare Scholar
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=711.0]{If this card is already in play at the start of a solo game, the current round number is 0. You can build the fences in round 6 and 10.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Serf}{Ackerfrohne}{K266}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} \changed{action space}, you receive 1 grain before taking the action(s). Alternatively, you can exchange 1 grain for 1 vegetable.}

\card{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267}{(1--5 players)}
{When you take a family growth action, you can pay 1 food to immediately place the offspring in your \changed{home}. This allows you to take an action with it this round. If you do this, the offspring does not count as ``newborn''.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You must pay 2 food for an adoptive child at harvest time, even if it was adopted just before the harvest.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}, \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291}, or \cardref{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325}.}
\item \ecp{If you use the \cardref{Mother of Twins}{Zwillingsmutter}{Z336} for the same family growth action, you may use the Adoptive Parents for one or both of the new family members. This costs 1 food per family member.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/442204]{When checking the size of the family for a normal family growth action, requiring room in the house, you must also count newborns you gained with a ``family growth without room'', even though the newborn for which you use the Adoptive Parents is put in a room before these previous newborns return home.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pieceworker}{Akkordarbeiter}{K268}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you receive wood, clay, reed, stone or grain on an action space, you can buy one more of the same good for 1 food. Whenever you receive vegetable(s) on an action space, you can buy one more for 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You can only buy goods in the work phase (phase 3) --- not at the start of a round.}
\item \apx{Only affects goods that are earned directly through an action space, not through improvements and occupations.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/239038]{If you get more than one type of goods, you can buy 1 of each type for 1 food each. All extra goods must be payed at the same time.}
\item \ecp{You may first convert the goods received directly from the action space to food to pay for the Pieceworker. The Pieceworker is used before other cards, so you cannot convert goods that you receive from an occupation or improvement.}
\item \ecp{You must pay for the Pieceworker before you receive the extra good(s). You may not convert the goods that you receive from the Pieceworker to food to pay for this card.}
\item \ecp{Is also activated when you use an action space that contains wood because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}.}
\item \ecp{If you use an action space that contains wood, and you leave all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, you still can buy 1 wood with the Pieceworker. You cannot use the food received from those cards to pay the cost of the Pieceworker.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3922484]{When you sow by taking grain or vegetables from the general supply and putting them on your fields, this does not count as receiving resources, and does not activate the Pieceworker.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the ``Traveling players'' action on an action space, after \changed{all of the players} have finished their turns you may move that person to \changed{one of the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain}, \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} and \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} action spaces, if it's free,} and take the action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you use the ``Traveling Players'' action, you should place claim markers on the three action spaces \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain}, \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} and \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow}, as a reminder that these may be claimed later.}
\item \cardtext[Jongleur]{If another player uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} with a ``Traveling Players'' action, he pays you 1 food.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{If the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Pond Watchman}{?}{G046} also have been played, the family members are moved in player order, starting with the player left of the one who placed the last regular person. If you can move more than one person, you move them consecutively in an order of your choice. You cannot move the same person twice (e.g.\ by moving it to \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} with Acrobat, and then using Countryman). You cannot move to an action space that was occupied after the last regular person placement.}% Also http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/323471
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/346270]{In the round in which you play this card, you may only move the family member from the ``Traveling Players'' action space if it was placed \emph{after} you played the Acrobat.}
\item \ecp{Moving a person with the Acrobat counts as taking an action, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Opportunist}{?}{G043}, but not as placing your last person, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Magician}{Zauberk■nstler}{K311}, because this person has already been placed previously.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you build room(s), you may grow your family by up to the number of rooms that you build, \changed{if you have the room to house the new family members}. This costs 1 food per person.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may build several rooms at once with a building action. For 2 food, the Wet Nurse allows an immediate family growth of 2 people; for 3 food, 3 people.
\item The new family members are placed on top of the person that was placed on the building action space. They are only available as people in the next round.
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=685.0]{You may use the Wet Nurse more than once in the game.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Hut Builder}{H■ttenbauer}{E178} or \cardref{Mason}{Maurer}{E191}, or when you play the \cardref{Wooden Hut Extension}{Holzh■ttenanbau}{I81}, \cardref{Clay Hut Extension}{Lehmh■ttenanbau}{K132}, or \cardref{Stone House Extension}{Steinhausanbau}{E55}.}
\item \ecp{Using the Wet Nurse counts as a family growth action. If you use the \cardref{Farm Steward}{Hofverwalter}{I233} for this family growth action, you do not need an empty room for one of the new family members.}
\item \ecp{Does not activate the \cardref{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Educator}{Ausbilder}{K271}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player plays an occupation card, you can pay 3 food to play one yourself. From your 4th occupation, this only costs 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you play an occupation yourself, you cannot use the Educator to play a second one.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/555986]{Is also activated when another player uses an improvement or occupation, e.g.\ \cardref{Puppeteer}{Puppenspieler}{I249}, to play an occupation.}
\item \apx[Brotschieber]{Activates the \cardref{Bread Paddle}{Brotschieber}{K111} when used.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{If more than one occupation is played in one action (e.g. because of \cardref{Writing Desk}{Schreibpult}{E49} or \cardref{Chief's Daughter}{Hðuptlingstochter}{E173}), you can use the Educator more than once too.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272}{(1--5 players)}
{In each renovation, you may replace exactly 1 clay or 1 stone with 1 wood. In each extension, you may replace exactly 2 clay or 2 stone with 1 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Frame Builder for the same action.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3456758]{If a room costs only 1 clay and/or 1 stone, e.g.\ after using the \cardref{Clay Plasterer}{Lehmdecker}{I241} and \cardref{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243}, you cannot use the Frame Builder.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273}{(4--5 players)}
{For each wild boar that you convert into food, you can place up to 2 wood from your personal supply on this card. At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each wood on this card except the 1st, 4th, 7th and 10th.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Converted wild boar may either be placed on the \cardref{Tanner}{Gerber}{K280}, \ecp{\cardref{Taxidermist}{Prðparator}{Z330},} or used for the Basin Maker; you cannot use two of these cards for the same animal.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/300894]{If you also have the \cardref{Pelts}{Tierfelle}{K339} \ecp{and/or the \cardref{Brush Maker}{B■rstenbinder}{E156},} you may use those cards as well as the Basin Maker cards for the same wild boar.}
\item \ecp{You may not remove wood from this card, or use it again in any way. Wood on this card is not part of your personal supply,} \apx[2nd ed]{and does not count for the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7},} \ecp{\cardref{Storehouse Clerk}{Lagerhalter}{K287}, or \cardref{Sawmill}{Holzmanufaktur}{K122}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Organic Farmer}{Biobauer}{K274}{(1--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=747]{of your pastures} that contains at least 1 animal, but could contain at least 3 more animals than it does.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You also get a bonus point for the \cardref{Forest Pasture}{Waldweide}{K145} if you have at least one animal on it.}
\item \ecp{You may also receive a bonus point for the \cardref{Animal Yard}{Tierhof}{E58}, for example if you also have the \cardref{Drinking Trough}{Trðnke}{E59}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Perpetual Student}{Bummelstudent}{K275}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you can play an occupation card, you can ask another player to randomly draw one of your \changed{occupation} cards instead of choosing one yourself. If you do this, you receive 3 food before you pay the costs of the card, but you must play the card that the other player draws.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{If an occupation card is drawn that you cannot afford, for example \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291} or \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172}, you have to take begging cards to make up the difference.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/242605
\item \ecp{Can also be used if you have only 1 occupation card left.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Constable}{Dorfschulze}{K276}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive wood immediately when you play this card: \changed{if played in round 12 or 13, take 1 wood; if played in round 9, 10, or 11, take 2 wood; if played in round 6, 7, or 8, take 3 wood; if played before round 6, take 4 wood}. At the end of the game, any player who has no negative points receives 5 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/514728]{You lose the bonus points from this card if you score negative points in any scoring category, if you have begging cards or unused farmyard tiles, or if you have any card in front of you that has a negative value or gives negative bonus points.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{Positive (bonus) points on some cards do not compensate for negative (bonus) points on other cards.}
\item \ecp{Negative points that are compensated by \cardref{Yeoman Farmer}{Freibauer}{E165} or \cardref{Hide Farmer}{Hufenbauer}{I236} are not counted as negative for the Constable.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Manufacturer}{Fabrikant}{K277}{(3--5 players)}
{Once you have a clay hut or a stone house, the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8} and \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9} are minor improvements for you and their cost is reduced by 2 building resources of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/497755]{The Joinery, Pottery and Basketmaker's Workshop still count as major improvements as well, e.g.\ for \cardref{Nosebag}{-}{M022} or \cardref{Administration}{-}{M070}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use a sowing action, you can plant wood on this card. \changed{There can be up to 3 stacks of wood on this card, as shown.} The wood is treated the same as sown grain and is harvested during the Field phase.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{You place up to 3 wood from your personal supply next to each other on this card, and pile additional wood from the general supply on your own 1--3 wood markers.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/485481]{You may choose to only sow 1 or 2 wood on this card. You may then in a later sowing action sow more wood here.}
\item \ecp{In each harvest, you take one wood from each of the stacks.}
\item \apx{If you may place 4 grain on a field when sowing, e.g. with an occupation, you also receive 4 wood on each stack on the Forester; if you would receive 5 grain, you receive 5 wood. If you have the \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219}, you get a total of 5 wood on the card if you only plant 1 wood on this card (and nothing elsewhere); if you plant 2 wood (and nothing else), you receive 4 wood on each stack.}
\item \apx[Kleinbauer]{The \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286} may not be used to plant extra wood.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/530122]{It is allowed to choose an action space with a sowing action, only to sow wood on the Forester.}
\item \ecp{Wood on this card is not in your personal supply, and does not count for the \cardref{Storehouse Clerk}{Lagerhalter}{K287} or \cardref{Pilgrim}{?}{G045}. At the end of the game, it does count for the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7} or the \cardref{Sawmill}{Holzmanufaktur}{K122}.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{At the end of the game, the wood is not counted as grain, of course.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Scholar}{Gelehrter}{K279}{(1--5 players)}
{Once you have a stone house, at the start of a round you can always either pay 1 food to play an occupation card or play an improvement card by paying its costs.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Activates the \cardref{Bookshelf}{B■cherregal}{K112}, \cardref{Perpetual Student}{Bummelstudent}{K275}, and \cardref{Patron}{Mðzen}{E192} when used to play an occupation card.
\item Each round, the Scholar allows you to play up to 1 additional card.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2760626]{You may play major improvements with the Scholar.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Merchant}{Kaufmann}{E179} when used to play an improvement.}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{Food that you receive at the start of a round can be used to pay for an occupation,} \ecp{and food or goods received at the start of a round may be used to pay for an improvement.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=693]{If the occupation or improvement that you play with the Scholar has an effect at the start of a round, you may choose to use it immediately in the round it is played.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1621]{If you play an occupation or improvement to place goods or food on remaining round spaces (e.g.\ \cardref{Swan Lake}{Schwanensee}{K140}, \cardref{Sack Cart}{Sackkarre}{E46} or \cardref{Wood Deliveryman}{Holzlieferant}{K283}), you do not place any on the current round space, as the round has already started. The current round also does not count for \cardref{Ranch}{Ranch}{Z321} etc.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Tanner}{Gerber}{K280}{(3--5 players)}
{When you convert wild boar or cattle to food, \changed{place them on this card}. At the end of the game, you receive bonus points if you have animal markers on this card. \changed{For the wild boar on this card, you receive: 6 or more wild boar, 3 points; 4 or 5 wild boar, 2 points; 2 or 3 wild boar, 1 point. For the cattle on this card, you receive: 4 or more cattle, 3 points; 3 cattle, 2 points; 2 cattle, 1 point}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you place a converted wild boar on the Tanner, you may not use the \cardref{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273}, \ecp{\cardref{Taxidermist}{Prðparator}{Z330} }, or \cardref{Brush Maker}{B■rstenbinder}{E156} for the same animal.
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/300894]{If you also have the \cardref{Pelts}{Tierfelle}{K339}, you may use that card as well as the Tanner for each converted animal.}
\item \ecp{Animals on this card do not count in the scoring at the end of the game.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Traveling Salesman}{Handelsreisender}{K281}{(1--5 players)}
