{Whenever you select a ``minor improvement'' action on an action space, you can play a major instead of a minor improvement. If you select a ``major or minor improvement'' action \changed{on an action space}, you can play 2 minor improvements.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Optional; can only be used once per turn.}
\item \apx{Using both Traveling Salesman and \cardref{Merchant}{Kaufmann}{E179}, you can play up to 4 minor improvements for 1 food on a ``major or minor improvement'' action space, or you can acquire 2 major improvements for 1 food on a ``minor improvement'' action space.}
\item \apx{Using both Traveling Salesman and \cardref{Businessman}{Geschðftsmann}{I228}, you can play up to 3 minor improvements one after another when you use the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you use the \cardref{Scholar}{Gelehrter}{K279}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{House Steward}{Hausmeier}{K282}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive wood immediately when you play this card: \changed{if played in round 12 or 13, take 1 wood; if played in round 9, 10, or 11, take 2 wood; if played in round 6, 7, or 8, take 3 wood; if played before round 6, take 4 wood}. At the end of the game, the player(s) with the most rooms in their home receive 3 bonus points each.}

\card{Wood Deliveryman}{Holzlieferant}{K283}{(1--5 players)}
{Place 1 wood on each remaining space for rounds 8 to 14. At the start of these rounds, you receive the wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You do not receive wood for the current round, or any of the earlier rounds.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}{(1--5 players)}
{At the start of the work phase \changed{of each round}, you can distribute the wood from the \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood} action space as evenly as possible onto the neighbouring \actionref{1 Clay}{1XClay}, \actionref{1 Reed}{1XReed} and \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} spaces. When you play this card, you receive 2 wood.\comment{Added in pimp-box}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Because of occupations like the \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253} and the \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, \ecp{or in the solo game,} there may be wood on the wood space that cannot be distributed evenly --- in this case, 1 or 2 wood are left on the action space.}
\item \apx{The Wood Distributor, \cardref{Foreman}{Vorarbeiter}{K308} and \cardref{Taster}{Vorkoster}{I260} may react to each other. A player who decides to use his occupation cannot take back their decision. A player who does not wish to use the occupation has until the start of the work phase (phase 3) to reconsider.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/359723]{It is not allowed to use the \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood} action space if it is empty, not even if that would activate other improvements or occupations.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Tinsmith}{KannengieÔer}{K285}{(3--5 players)}
{You can convert clay into food at any time. You receive 1 food per clay. If any player has built a \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10}, you receive 3 food for each 2 clay \changed{instead}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item The bonus for the Well is also awarded if it has been upgraded to the \cardref{Village Well}{Dorfbrunnen}{I66}.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}{(1--5 players)}
{\changed{Your pastures that can hold 2 animals can hold 3 animals.} While you have at most 2 fields, add 1 extra grain or vegetable \changed{from the general supply to each field you sow}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you have the \cardref{Drinking Trough}{Trðnke}{E59} and/or the \cardref{Shepherd's Pipe}{Hornfl—te}{E29} as well, the bonuses from those cards are added to the one of the Smallholder. If you have all three cards, you can have up to 7 sheep on a 2 animal pasture.}
\item If you have the Shepherd's Pipe, the Smallholder cannot be used for unfenced stables.
\item \apx[Acreage, Bean Field, Turnip Field]{\cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105}, \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18}, \cardref{Lettuce Patch}{Salatfeld}{E47} and \cardref{Turnip Field}{R■benacker}{K137} count towards the indicated maximum of 2 fields, and you receive extra grain or vegetables on them because of the Smallholder.} \ecp{The Acreage counts as two fields.}% Contradicted by Smallholder entry in appendix. See http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/415890
\item \apx{\cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278} \ecp{and \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}} do not count towards the indicated maximum of 2 fields, and the Smallholder may not be used when you plant on those cards.}% The appendix contradicts itself on the interaction between Bean Field et al and Smallholder.
\item \ecp{Does not increase the capacity of the \cardref{Animal Yard}{Tierhof}{E58}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368508]{You can only put an extra grain on grain fields, and an extra vegetable on vegetable fields.}
\item \ecp{The effect of the Smallholder is optional, but if you use it in an action, you must use it for all fields you sow in that action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Storehouse Clerk}{Lagerhalter}{K287}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you have at least 5 stone at the start of a round, you receive 1 extra stone. If you have at least 6 reed, you receive 1 reed. If you have at least 7 clay, you receive 1 clay. If you have at least 8 wood, you receive 1 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Only resources in your personal supply count. Resources on cards in front of you, such as the \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} or the \cardref{Resource Seller}{Werkstoffhðndler}{K310}, do not count.}
\item \ecp{If you receive resources at the start of the round because of occupations or minor improvements, you may take them before you use the Storehouse Clerk.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Storehouse Keeper}{Lagerverwalter}{K288}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use a \changed{person}'s action to take reed and stone \changed{at the same time}, you also receive your choice of 1 clay or 1 grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is only activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games, and the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood} in 4-player games.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you receive reed and stone because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289}{(4--5 players)}
{After all players have placed their \changed{people}, you may move one of your \changed{people} from a \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} or \actionref{Take 1 Vegetable}{TakeX1XVegetable} action space to a free \changed{action space with a ``sow'' action}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you choose one of these action spaces, you place claim markers on the empty ``Sowing'' spaces to show that you have a claim.}
\item \apx{There are 2 ``Sowing'' action spaces. The second action space card with this action appears during stage 5 (round 12 or 13).}
\item \ecp{Both ``Sowing'' action spaces provide a choice of actions. You may also do the other action on this action space when you move your family member, even if you do not do the sowing action.}
\item \ecp{If you use both the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} and \actionref{Take 1 Vegetable}{TakeX1XVegetable} action spaces in the same round, you may move only one of the two family members.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/410794]{If you have the \cardref{Field Warden}{Flursch■tze}{E163}, you may also move a family member to the \actionref{Plough Field and Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow} space if it's occupied.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{If the \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269} or \cardref{Pond Watchman}{?}{G046} also have been played, the family members are moved in player order, starting with the player left of the one who placed the last regular person. If you can move more than one person, you move them consecutively in an order of your choice. You cannot move the same person twice (e.g.\ by moving it to \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} with Acrobat, and then using Countryman). You cannot move to an action space that was occupied after the last regular person placement.}% Also http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/323471
\item \ecp{If you have already used a family member on one of the two action spaces before you play this card, you may move this family member at the end of the round.}
\item \ecp{Moving a person with the Countryman counts as taking an action, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Opportunist}{?}{G043}, but not as placing your last person, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Magician}{Zauberk■nstler}{K311}, because this person has already been placed previously.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Worker}{Lehmarbeiter}{K290}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use an action \changed{of a person} to take wood or clay, you also receive 1 additional clay.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which wood or clay is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no wood or clay (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}).}
\item \ecp{Is activated even if you leave all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space that contains wood because of the Wood Distributor.}
\item \apx{Is also activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games,} \ecp{and the action space \actionref{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource} in 3-player games if you take wood or clay.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you receive wood because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\item \ecp{You get a maximum of 1 clay from the Clay Worker per action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291}{(3--5 players)}
{When you play this card, immediately carry out a ``Family growth even without room'' action (similar to the round card from stage 5). Playing this card costs you an additional 4 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{If you build a room after the Lover has had offspring, the offspring occupies the new room. It is better to build the room first, then take a normal family growth action, and only then play the Lover.}
\item \ecp{Does not activate the \cardref{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2356]{The newborn is a part of your family, and you must put it in your home in the return home phase of this round. Until then, you can put the newborn on this occupation card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Market Woman}{Marktfrau}{K292}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you receive vegetables through a \changed{person}'s action or through a minor improvement, you receive an additional 2 grain.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Is not activated when you use an occupation to get vegetables.}
\item \apx{Is activated when you play the \cardref{Market Stall}{Marktstand}{E39} or \cardref{Weekly Market}{Wochenmarkt}{I104}; however, you must first pay the grain for the improvement card in order to get grain back.}
\item \apx{Is also activated when you take a vegetable at the start of the round because of the \cardref{Greenhouse}{Gewðchshaus}{K117}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3922484]{When you sow by taking vegetables from the general supply and putting them on your fields, this does not count as receiving vegetables, and does not activate the Market Woman.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ploughman}{Pfl■ger}{K293}{(1--5 players)}
{Add 4, 7 and 10 to \changed{the number of} the current round and place 1 field on each corresponding round space. At the start of these rounds, you can plough that field by paying 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you choose not to lay down a field, the tile is returned to the general supply.
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=711.0]{If this card is already in play at the start of a solo game, the current round number is 0. You can plough the fields in rounds 4, 7, and 10.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/429382]{You may use food received at the start of the round, for example from the \cardref{Well}{Brunnen}{A10}, to pay for the field.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Brushwood Collector}{Reisigbinder}{K294}{(3--5 players)}
{You may replace the required reed with a total of 1 wood for any renovation or \changed{for each new room}. (You use brushwood to make the roof.)
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Brushwood Collector for the same action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cattle Breeder}{Rinderz■chter}{K295}{(4--5 players)}
{Your cattle breed at the end of round 12, if there is space for the calf. When you play this card, you receive 1 cattle.}

\card{Seed Seller}{Samenhðndler}{K296}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} action space, you receive 1 additional grain. When you play this card, \changed{you receive} 1 grain.}

\card{Sheep Farmer}{Schafbauer}{K297}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you take sheep with one of your people, you receive an additional sheep from the \changed{general} supply. You can exchange 3 sheep for 1 cattle and 1 wild boar at any time (except during the breeding phase).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Is activated by the \actionref{1 Sheep}{1XSheep} action space (round 1--4), \apx{and by the \actionref{Sheep, Wild Boar, or Cattle}{SheepXXWildXBoarXXorXCattle} action space in the 5-player game.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you receive sheep because of occupations and minor improvements.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/440124]{You may immediately use the Sheep Farmer to exchange animals you receive, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{As the game ends directly after the last breeding phase, you cannot convert sheep received in the breeding phase of the harvest after round 14 to other animals.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335596
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Shepherd Boy}{Schðferknecht}{K298}{(4--5 players)}
{Once you live in a stone house, place 1 sheep on each remaining round space. At the start of these rounds, you receive the sheep.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you already live in a stone house, place the sheep immediately.}
\item You do not receive a free sheep for the current round.
\item The free sheep may be immediately converted into food with an appropriate improvement.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Slaughterman}{Schlachter}{K299}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player converts \changed{1 or more} animals into food, you receive 1 food from the general supply. In the feeding phase \changed{of the harvest}, you are the last player to feed your family (so you can benefit if other players slaughter).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you convert an animal yourself, you receive no additional food.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/368106]{If both the Slaughterman and the \cardref{Slaughterhouse}{Schlachthof}{I97} are on the table, the owners of these two cards feed their families in current turn order (which is the turn order of the next round).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Schnaps Distiller}{Schnapsbrenner}{K300}{(1--5 players)}
{In the feeding phase of each harvest, you can convert up to 1 vegetable to 5 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You do not need a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4} or oven to convert the vegetable.
\item Distilling schnaps does not count as baking.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3651107]{The vegetable that you want to convert into 5 food may not be on a field; it must be taken from your personal supply.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wood Carver}{Schnitzer}{K301}{(1--5 players)}
{In each round, you pay 1 wood less for one of the following: an improvement, a room of a wooden hut, a stable or a fence.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item May only be used once in each round. You can place your personal wood supply on this card to remind you of the benefits of this occupation.
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2804686]{If you build several rooms in one action, you can only use the Wood Carver for one of them.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Wood Carver for the same action.}
\item \ecp{May not be used when you build a new room for a clay hut or a stone house, not even if you have the \cardref{Clay Supports}{Lehmstake}{E37}, \cardref{Brushwood Roof}{Reisigdach}{K136}, \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272}, or \cardref{Brushwood Collector}{Reisigbinder}{K294}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pig Whisperer}{Schweinefl■sterer}{K302}{(4--5 players)}
{Add 4, 7 and 10 to \changed{the number of} the current round and place 1 wild boar on each corresponding round space. At the start of these rounds, you receive the wild boar.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=711.0]{If this card is already in play at the start of a solo game, the current round number is 0. You receive the wild boars in rounds 4, 7, and 10.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Breaker}{Steinklopfer}{K303}{(4--5 players)}
{At any time, you can renovate your clay hut to a stone house without using a ``Renovation'' action space.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You must still pay the costs of the renovation.}
\item You may not use both the \cardref{Conservator}{Restaurator}{E200} and the Stone Breaker to renovate your wooden hut to a stone house out of turn.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Veterinarian}{Tierarzt}{K304}{(4--5 players)}
{When you play this card, place 4 sheep cubes, 3 wild boar cubes and 2 cattle cubes in a container. At the start of each round, draw two animals. If they are the same, keep one. Return the 1 or 2 animals to the container.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you draw 2 different animals, both are returned to the container.
\item If you draw identical animals, the one you keep may be immediately converted into food with an appropriate improvement.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Handler}{Tierhalter}{K305}{(4--5 players)}
{Place 1 sheep on the space for round 7, 1 wild boar on round 10 and 1 cattle on round 14. At the start of these rounds, you can buy the animal for 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{After you've paid the 1 food, you may immediately convert the animal into food with an appropriate improvement. However, you must pay the 1 food beforehand; you may not subtract it from the proceeds.}
\item \ecp{Food that you receive at the start of a round can be used to pay for the animal immediately.}% Compare Scholar
\item \cardtext{You do not receive animals for the current round, or any of the earlier rounds.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Tamer}{Tierzðhmer}{K306}{(1--5 players)}
{You can keep 1 animal in each room of your home. You may keep more than 1 type of animal in your home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Has no effect after you have bought a \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/3061226]{The animals that the Animal Tamer allows you to keep in the house replace the usually allowed 1 pet (so if you have 3 rooms, you can keep 3 animals in your home, not 4).}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Breeder}{Tierz■chter}{K307}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you fence unused spaces to create at least one new pasture, you can buy a pair of animals: 2 sheep for 1 food, 2 wild boar for 2 food, or 2 cattle for 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx[2nd ed]{At least one space must be newly used, and may not contain stables. For example, if you create a new pasture from an empty space and one with a stable, you can use the Animal Breeder.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{Is not activated when you use the \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}.}% Contradicts the appendix. See also http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1611
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/393480]{You can only buy at most 1 pair of animals per turn, even if you create more than 1 new pasture, or if you build fences again in the same turn, e.g.\ with the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175}.}
\item \ecp{After you've paid the food, you may immediately convert the animals into food with an appropriate improvement. However, you must pay the food beforehand; you may not subtract it from the proceeds.}
\item \ecp[http://banach.ucsd.edu/forums/index.php?topic=1571]{If you also receive other animals from the fence building, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160} or \cardref{Shepherd's Crook}{Hirtenstab}{I77}, you may convert those animals to food first to pay for the animals from the Farm Breeder.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Foreman}{Vorarbeiter}{K308}{(4--5 players)}
{At the start of the work phase \changed{of each round}, you can place 1 food from the general supply on an action space of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{The \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}, Foreman and \cardref{Taster}{Vorkoster}{I260} may react to each other. A player who decides to use his occupation cannot take back their decision. A player who does not wish to use the occupation has until the start of the work phase (phase 3) to reconsider.}
\item \ecp{You may place the food on any action space, including minor improvements that are action spaces (such as \cardref{Clay Deposit}{Lehmh■gel}{I337}), action spaces that have been introduced to the game by other cards (such as \cardref{Master Forester}{Forstwirt}{E164}), and \actionref{Infirmary}{Infirmary}.}
\item \ecp{You may not place the food on a round space of a future round, unless the action card has already been revealed by the \cardref{Chamberlain}{Kðmmerer}{I238}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Weaver}{Weber}{K309}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you have at least 2 sheep at the start of the work phase \changed{of a round}, you receive 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Sheep that are on the board because of the \cardref{Shepherd Boy}{Schðferknecht}{K298}, \cardref{Sheep Whisperer}{Schaffl■sterer}{I250}, \cardref{Master Shepherd}{Schafmeister}{E204}, or \cardref{Animal Handler}{Tierhalter}{K305}, \ecp{and sheep from the \cardref{Veterinarian}{Tierarzt}{K304},} are taken before the start of the work phase, and may count towards the 2 sheep requisite to use the Weaver.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Resource Seller}{Werkstoffhðndler}{K310}{(1--5 players)}
{Pile (from bottom to top) 1 stone, clay, stone, clay, reed, clay, wood on this card. You receive the top marker when you receive that type of building resource.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx{Resources may be obtained at the start of the round (phase 1) as well as in the work phase (phase 3).}
\item \ecp{Is also activated when you receive resources from improvements and occupations. But if you do not receive certain resources because of other cards (\cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Wood Buyer}{Holzaufkðufer}{I234}, etc.), you cannot use the Resource Seller for those resources.}
\item \apx{It is possible to receive more than 1 resource from the Resource Seller by using occupations such as \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}, \cardref{Storehouse Keeper}{Lagerverwalter}{K288} or \cardref{Clay Worker}{Lehmarbeiter}{K290}.}
\item \ecp{If you receive more than one resource at the same time, you can choose the order in which you receive them, except that if you use an action space, you first receive all resources from the action itself, and then all resources from card effects.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Magician}{Zauberk■nstler}{K311}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use your last person to choose the ``Traveling Players'' action on an action space, you receive an additional 1 grain and 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext[Jongleur]{If another player uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} with a ``Traveling Players'' action, he pays you 1 food.}
\item \ecp{If you play the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}, that guest counts as your last person placed in the round.}
\item \ecp{If you move a person at the end of a round, e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}, that does not count as your last person placed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}{(1--5 players)}
{\changed{Once} each round, for a cost of 1 food, you can immediately fence a pasture of 1 farmyard space around a stable that you have just built. You do not need to pay wood for the fences.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2113]{You must use fence the pasture in the same turn in which you built the stable.}
\item \apx{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Groom}{Stallknecht}{I254} to build a stable.}
\item \apx{Is activated when you use the \cardref{Stablehand}{Stalljunge}{E207}: when you build a fence, you must build 1 free stable, which can be fenced for free. You may not use the Stablehand again to receive a second free stable.} \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/339668]{The fences built in the original action (before using Stablehand and Fence Overseer) must follow the rules for fence building: complete pastures only.}
\item \apx[Zaunaufseher,Heckenwart]{Activates the \cardref{Hedge Keeper}{Heckenwart}{E175} and \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160} when used.}
\item \ecp{Activates the Stablehand when used: when you build a stable, you may fence it, after which you have to build another stable. You may not then fence that second stable.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=700.0]{You must follow the rules for fence building. If you already have pastures, only a stable that is adjacent to one of them may be fenced in.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Rancher}{Landmann}{I340}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever, at the start of a round, you \changed{are using more farmyard spaces} than every other player, you receive 1 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If there is a tie, you get nothing.}
\item \ecp{The number of used spaces is counted before using the \cardref{Ploughman}{Pfl■ger}{K293} or \cardref{Fence Deliveryman}{Zaunlieferant}{I265}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Guildmaster}{Zunftvorsteher}{E341}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive 4 wood when you acquire the \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7} or play the \cardref{Cabinetmaker}{Tischler}{I258}. When you acquire the \cardref{Pottery}{T—pferei}{A8} or play the \cardref{Potter}{T—pfer}{E214}, you receive 4 clay. When you acquire the \cardref{Basketmaker's Workshop}{Korbflechterei}{A9} or play the \cardref{Basketmaker}{Korbflechter}{E183}, you receive 3 reed. If you have already played any of these cards when you play the Guildmaster, you receive 2 building resources of the appropriate type for each existing card.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you have already upgraded the Joinery to the \cardref{Sawmill}{Holzmanufaktur}{K122} before you play the Guildmaster, you also get 2 wood.}
\item \ecp{You receive the building resources after acquiring or playing each card; you cannot use these resources to pay for the cards.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/520827]{If you e.g.\ obtain both the Joinery and the Cabinetmaker, you get 4 wood twice. If you play an improvement for a second time (e.g.\ the Joinery after upgrading it to a Sawmill), you receive the wood again.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Trainer}{Dompteur}{K342}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you take food from a ``Traveling players'' space, you may immediately use it to buy animals: Pay 2 food for each sheep or wild boar and 3 food for each cattle.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{Only the food that was lying on the action space can be used to buy animals. If you use e.g. the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} or \cardref{Dancer}{Tðnzer}{E212}, the additional food cannot be used.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/5403411]{Juggler and Dancer are used before you use the Animal Trainer to buy animals.}% See also http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2187
\item \ruling[http://lookout-games.de/2008/04/07/einer-geht-noch-einer-geht-noch-rein/]{If another player uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} with a ``Traveling Players'' action, he pays you 1 food.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard. However, you may not use that food to buy more animals with the Animal Trainer.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325}{(1--5 players)}
{At any time, you can pay 3 food to take a family growth action without placing one of your \changed{people}. You must have room in your home. You can use the newborn to take actions from the following round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Farm Steward}{Hofverwalter}{I233}, \cardref{Mother of Twins}{Zwillingsmutter}{Z336}, and \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267} when used.}
\item \ecp{Does not activate the \cardref{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/4083106]{If you use the Village Beauty during the harvest after feeding your family, the new family member remains a newborn for the entire following round.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Gentleman}{Gentleman}{Z326}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you manage to be the very last player to place a \changed{person} in any round, you receive 1 food after you take the final action. If you play this occupation with the last \changed{person} to be placed during the current round, you receive 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If a player plays the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}, that guest counts as the last person placed in the round.}
\item \ecp{If a player moves a person at the end of a round, e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}, that does not count as the last person placed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Herald}{Herold}{Z327}{(3--5 players)}
{At any time, you may look at all the remaining unplaced round cards and re-sort them. When you play this card, you receive 2 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{When re-sorting, the round cards must remain in the appropriate game stage.}
\item \ecp{If round cards are outside their appropriate game stage because of the \cardref{Fortune Teller}{Wahrsagerin}{\v{C}06}, you have to correct this when you use the Herald.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Cooper}{K■fer}{Z328}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you or another player receives \changed{3 food or more on} an action space, you receive 1 food from the general supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The amount of food is counted without taking any improvements or occupations into account. The Cooper can only be activated by an action space that has at least 3 food on it: only the action space \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing}, an action space with ``Traveling players'', or an action on which the \cardref{Foreman}{Vorarbeiter}{K308} has placed enough food.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated by using the \cardref{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mail Coach Driver (German)}{Postkutscher}{Z329}{(3--5 players)}
{From now until the end of the game, the other players do not receive goods and food during the work phase, but only when they return their people to their home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{``Goods'' includes wood, clay, reed, stone, vegetables, grain, and animals.}
\item \ecp{When another player places a family member that would give him goods, the action has no immediate effect. Improvements and occupations that are activated by choosing an action are activated at this time; improvements and occupations activated by the receipt of goods are activated when the family members return home.}
\item \ecp{If you perform an action that would give another player goods or food, e.g. because of the \cardref{Fencer}{Zaunbauer}{I264} or the \cardref{Spinney}{Holzgarten}{I80}, he only receives them in the returning home phase. If you give goods or food to another player, e.g. because of the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237} or the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}, you lose them immediately, but the other player receives them later.}
\item \ecp{In the returning home phase, each of the other players decides the order in which they receive their goods and food. Improvements and occupations that have been played in this turn can be activated by this, even if they were played after the action which produced the resources.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mail Coach Driver (English)}{-}{Z329*}{(3--5 players)}
{From now until the end of the game, the other players only receive goods from action spaces when they return their \changed{people} to their home.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{This card applies to goods that are on action spaces as well as goods that are taken from the supply, but not to goods that are received from cards.}
\item \ecp{``Goods'' includes wood, clay, reed, stone, vegetables, grain, and animals.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Taxidermist}{Prðparator}{Z330}{(4--5 players)}
{When you convert animals to food, you can place \changed{some or all of them} on this card instead of returning them to the \changed{general} supply. The card can hold a maximum of 1 sheep, 1 wild boar and 1 cattle. These animals are counted in scoring.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you place a converted animal on the Taxidermist, you may not use the \cardref{Basin Maker}{Beckenbauer}{K273}, \cardref{Tanner}{Gerber}{K280}, or \cardref{Brush Maker}{B■rstenbinder}{E156} for the same animal.}
\item \ecp{If you also have the \cardref{Pelts}{Tierfelle}{K339}, you may use that card as well as the Taxidermist for each converted animal.}
\item \ecp{Animals on this card count for the \cardref{Loom}{Webstuhl}{K146}, \cardref{Milking Stool}{Melkschemel}{K133}, \cardref{Estate Manager}{Gutsverwalter}{E170} and \cardref{Milking Hand}{Melker}{I246}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Sower (German)}{Sðmann}{Z331}{(1--5 players)}
{You may immediately sow each grain that you receive outside the \changed{field phase of a harvest} and would otherwise place in your supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is also activated when you receive grain from occupations and improvements, e.g.\ \cardref{Corn Sheaf}{Korngarbe}{K129}, \cardref{Conjurer}{Gaukler}{E167}, \cardref{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184}, and \cardref{Harvest Helper}{Erntehelfer}{I223}.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated in an extra field phase because of the \cardref{Manure}{Mist}{I92}.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219} when used. If you get several grain at once, and you want to sow more than 1, you have to sow them at the same time.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}, \cardref{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}, \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90} and another player's \cardref{Field Worker}{Feldarbeiter}{I224} when used to sow the vegetable.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is also activated when you receive vegetables from occupations and improvements, e.g.\ \cardref{Weekly Market}{Wochenmarkt}{I104}, \cardref{Undergardener}{Gartenarbeiter}{E166}, and \cardref{Seed Trader}{Saatguthðndler}{Z332}.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Fieldsman}{Ackermann}{I219} when used. If you get several vegetable at once, and you want to sow more than 1, you have to sow them at the same time.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}, \cardref{Liquid Manure}{G■lle}{K118}, \cardref{Planter Box}{Lehnbeet}{I90}, \cardref{Potato Dibber}{Kartoffelstecher}{E32}, and another player's \cardref{Field Worker}{Feldarbeiter}{I224} when used to sow the vegetable.}

\item \ecp{Pay the food before receiving the grain or vegetable.}

\card{Game Designer}{Spieleentwickler}{Z333}{(1--5 players)}
{You can exchange 1 wood, 1 clay, 1 reed and 1 stone for 2 food and 1 bonus point at any time and as often as you like.

\item \cardtext{Write down the bonus points on the scoring pad immediately.}
\item \ecp{You cannot use the \cardref{Wood Carver}{Schnitzer}{K301}, \cardref{Stonecutter}{Steinschneider}{E211}, or \cardref{Bricklayer}{Lehmkleber}{I243} to reduce the costs.}

\card{Dance Instructor}{Tanzlehrer}{Z334}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive 4 food before you pay the costs of playing this occupation. \changed{You may} immediately return this card to your hand after you have played it.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When you play this card, you have to decide immediately if you want to take it back. If you leave it on the table, you may not change your mind later.}
\item \ecp{If you return this card to your hand, it does not count as a played occupation, e.g.\ for minor improvements, when scoring the \cardref{Reeve}{Vogt}{E217} or \cardref{Tutor}{Hauslehrer}{E174}, or when determining the costs of playing a subsequent occupation.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/2783359]{If you return this card to your hand, you may play it again later. If you also have the \cardref{Writing Desk}{Schreibpult}{E49}, you may play the Dance Instructor two times in the same action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

{\begin{explanationlist}

\item \ecp{You can only use this card once per harvest.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\card{Mother of Twins}{Zwillingsmutter}{Z336}{(1--5 players)}
{When you have family growth, you can pay 3 food to bring 2 new family members instead of 1 into the game. \changed{You do not need to have space in your home for the second new family member.}
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Using the \cardref{Wet Nurse}{Amme}{K270}, \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291} or \cardref{Village Beauty}{Dorfsch—nheit}{Z325} activates the Mother of Twins.}
\item \ecp{Receiving 2 family members with one family growth action activates the \cardref{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127}, \cardref{Midwife}{Hebamme}{I232}, \cardref{Child Prodigy}{Wunderknabe}{ø12}, and \cardref{Compulsory Education}{Allgemeine Schulpflicht}{ø19} only once, but \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267} twice.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Big Backer}{GroÔsponsor}{ø01}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player receives 2 or more animals of one type, you can buy one from him. A sheep costs 2 food, a wild boar 3 food, a cattle 4 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/380013]{The other player cannot refuse to sell the animal.}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when another player uses the \cardref{Clay Seller}{Lehmhðndler}{E186} or \cardref{Sheep Farmer}{Schafbauer}{K297} (to get cattle and wild boar), not even if he uses the card multiple times in succession.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when another player receives multiple animals at one time because of the \cardref{Swineherd}{Schweinehirt}{E206}, \cardref{Stockman}{Tierpfleger}{E213}, \cardref{Animal Dealer}{Viehtreiber}{I259}, \cardref{Sheep Farmer}{Schafbauer}{K297} (only sheep), \cardref{Animal Trainer}{Dompteur}{K342}, \cardref{Animal Breeder}{Tierz■chter}{K307}, \cardref{Shepherd}{Schðfer}{E203}, \cardref{Cowherd}{Kuhhirt}{I240}, or \cardref{Shepherd's Crook}{Hirtenstab}{I77}.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when another player receives multiple animals at the start of a round, including those from the \cardref{Veterinarian}{Tierarzt}{K304}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Action Artist}{Aktionsk■nstler}{ø02}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the ``Traveling Players'' action on an action space, you can return 1 animal of your choice to the general supply and receive 4 food in exchange.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You do not need a cooking improvement.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Therapist}{Therapeut}{ø03}{(3--5 players)}
{When you play this card, you can pay 2 food to immediately play 1 further occupation. Whenever another player plays an occupation, you can pay him 1 food. He must then, if possible, play a different occupation card instead.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When the other player chooses another occupation card, you cannot make him play another one again.}
\item \ecp{If the other player has only one occupation, he can play it as usual, even if you pay him 1 food.}
\item \ecp{If the other player cannot afford to play his other occupation cards (for example \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291} or \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172}), he has to take begging cards to make up the difference.}% compare Perpetual Student, but see http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/369277
\item \ecp{If you force another player to play a different occupation card, that does not count as playing a second occupation, so e.g. it does not activate the \cardref{Educator}{Ausbilder}{K271} twice.}
\item \ecp{If the other player has the \cardref{Perpetual Student}{Bummelstudent}{K275}, he may use that card for his second occupation as well; the occupation that was initially played (or drawn from his hand) cannot be drawn again.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Ski Instructor}{Skilehrer}{ø04}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player has family growth, he must pay you 1 food (or beg the food, if necessary). You must immediately turn the Ski Instructor face-down when you grow your family. You no longer receive its benefits, but it still counts as a played occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/362203]{You can use the Ski Instructor even if you already had family growth before you play this card. You receive the benefits of the Ski Instructor until your next family growth.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Lovable Vagabond}{Liebenswerte Sandler}{ø05}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you have no more food during the feeding phase of a harvest and should take one or more begging cards, you receive one fewer begging card.}

\card{Opinion Leader}{Meinungsmacher}{ø06}{(3--5 players)}
{At the start of each round, you can mark one action space of your choice with an arrow (claim) marker. Each player can use this action space during this round. (This cannot be used on action spaces on which goods are placed). Remove the arrow marker at the end of each round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/4124105]{If the start player action is used more than once in a round, the last player to use it will be the start payer next round.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/359723]{It is not allowed to use an empty accumulating action space such as \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood}, not even if it activates other improvements or occupations. It is allowed to use an empty accumulating action space that produces other resources directly, such as \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Building Tycoon}{Baul—we}{ø07}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player builds at least one room, you can give him 1 food and immediately build exactly one room yourself.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You must pay the building costs for the room.}
\item \ecp{You may use your improvements and occupations to lower the cost of the new room.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Environmentalist}{Umweltsch■tzer}{ø08}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you play or buy an improvement, you can replace 1 building resource of your choice with 1 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You can replace either 1 clay, 1 reed, or 1 stone.}
\item \ecp{There is no discount for renovations and room building, but only for minor and major improvements.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of an improvement together with the Environmentalist for the same action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Family Singers}{Sðngerfamilie}{ø09}{(1--5 players)}
{During the action phase, you can place any number of people on the family singers space instead of on an action space. For each person you place on the space, you receive 1 bonus point.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{This is not an action space.}
\item \ecp{Family members placed on this card in round 14 do not count for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Waltzer}{Walzertðnzer}{ø10}{(3--5 players)}
{You can place 2 people one after another, as long as both action spaces are on the same board and adjoin one another (not diagonally).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Action spaces on minor improvements, or introduced into the game by the \cardref{Clay Digger}{Gruber}{I230} or \cardref{Master Forester}{Forstwirt}{E164}, are never adjacent to any other action space.}
\item \ecp{Using the Waltzer counts as two turns.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2227]{The cards with action spaces on the leftmost game board should be placed randomly at the start of the game. If they weren't, shuffle them when Waltzer is played. In a 3 player game, the cards fill the top 2 rows on the board.}% See also Astronomer.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Magnate}{Magnat}{ø11}{(3--5 players)}
{When you play this card, you immediately receive 2 stone. At the end of the game, the player(s) with the most building resources receive(s) 3 bonus points.}

\card{Child Prodigy}{Wunderknabe}{ø12}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you have family growth, you can immediately pay \changed{1 wood for 1 bonus point, or 2 wood for 2 bonus points.}}

\card{Governor}{Statthalter}{\v{C}01}{(1--5 players)}
{Immediately take the top 4 occupations from the face-down deck, and choose 2 of them. You may play one of them immediately (taking into account the requirements on the card) without cost, and add the other one to your hand. If you don't want to play any, add both occupations to your hand.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you play one of the cards you drew, that again activates the \cardref{Bread Paddle}{Brotschieber}{K111}, \cardref{Bookshelf}{B■cherregal}{K112}, \cardref{Patron}{Mðzen}{E192}, and another player's \cardref{Educator}{Ausbilder}{K271}, but not the \cardref{Perpetual Student}{Bummelstudent}{K275}.}
\item \ecp{If another player has the \cardref{Therapist}{Therapeut}{ø03}, he can use that to force you to play the other card that you selected to keep, even if he already used it to force you to play the Governor.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Weekend Worker}{Wochenendarbeiter}{\v{C}02}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you renovate your home, you may at the same time build 1 room. This costs you 1 reed, 1 of the old construction material of your home before renovating (wood or clay), and 2 of the new construction material (clay or stone).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may use cards such as the \cardref{Ladder}{Leiter}{I91}, \cardref{Straw-thatched Roof}{Strohdach}{I99}, and \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272} to change the cost of the new room.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Jack-of-all-trades}{Allesk—nner}{\v{C}03}{(4--5 players)}
{Immediately discard all the occupations that you have played. In every round, you can pay 1 food to use an occupation played by another player. You receive all benefits, except for those for playing the card and those at the end of the game. Discard the Jack-of-all-trades when you play another occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You lose all effects of your old occupations when you play this card.}
\item \ecp{Discarded occupations are removed from the game and do not count for determining future occupation costs or for requirements of improvements.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461546]{You pay the food to the general supply.}
\item \ecp{If you use the Jack-of-all-trades during your own or another player's turn, the effect of the occupation you choose lasts from the moment you pay the food until the end of that turn.}
\item \ecp{You may use the Jack-of-all-trades in another player's turn as a reaction to the placement of a person on an action space. For example, when someone places a person on the \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood} action space, you may use another player's \cardref{Wood Buyer}{Holzaufkðufer}{I234} to buy wood from him. If the current player takes an action space with 2 actions, you have to activate the Jack-of-all-trades before he chooses which actions to perform. For example, when he uses the \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} action space, you have to choose to use the \cardref{Field Worker}{Feldarbeiter}{I224} or \cardref{Master Baker}{Backðltester}{E149} before he chooses if he wants to sow or bake.}
\item \ecp{If the owner of an occupation and you both want to use the same occupation at the same time, the owner is the first to benefit. For example, if someone takes 1 stone, and you use another player's \cardref{Stone Buyer}{Steinaufkðufer}{I255}, that player may buy the stone first; and if you use another player's \cardref{Taster}{Vorkoster}{I260}, your first turn is after the Taster's owner's first turn.}
\item \ecp{If you use the Jack-of-all-trades during the harvest, the effect of the occupation you choose lasts until the end of the current harvest phase.} \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2368]{A harvest counts as part of the preceding round.}
\item \ecp{You may use another player's \cardref{Pig Breeder}{Schweinez■chter}{I252}, \cardref{Cattle Breeder}{Rinderz■chter}{K295}, \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269}, or \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} at the end of a round.}
\item \ecp{If another player has an occupation that places goods, food, fences, or fields on action spaces of future rounds, you cannot use that occupation to also get those goods. However, you can use all other occupations at the start of a round, including another player's \cardref{Hut Builder}{H■ttenbauer}{E178}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/461546]{If another player has an occupation that can be used only once, e.g.\ the \cardref{Farm Steward}{Hofverwalter}{I233}, you don't receive the benefits of this occupation when you use it for the second time either. Also, if you use another player's \cardref{Farmer}{Farmer}{E160} and build fences for the second time, you receive 1 cattle. Your use of the occupation does not affect the original owner in any way: he can still use a one-use occupation even after you have used it.}
\item \ecp{If you place goods on the Jack-of-all-trades, e.g.\ if you use another player's \cardref{Brush Maker}{B■rstenbinder}{E156} or \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, they are discarded when the effect of that occupation ends.}
\item \ecp{You may use another player's \cardref{Herald}{Herold}{Z327} to look at the round card deck at all times. You may also use it to change the order of the deck, but the original owner of the Herald finally decides the order.}
\item \ecp{You cannot use another player's \cardref{Ratcatcher}{Rattenfðnger}{E198}, \cardref{Layabout}{Lehnerich}{I244}, \cardref{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248}, \cardref{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184}, \cardref{Seed Trader}{Saatguthðndler}{Z332}, \cardref{Opinion Leader}{Meinungsmacher}{ø06}, \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}.}
\item \ecp{You may use another player's \cardref{Family Singers}{Sðngerfamilie}{ø09} for 1 bonus point.}
\item \ecp{You cannot use another player's \cardref{Chamberlain}{Kðmmerer}{I238} to reveal cards at the start of round 11; however, you can use it to use an action space of a later round.}
\item \ecp{When a player uses the \cardref{Juggler}{Jongleur}{I237}, you may use the Jack-of-all-trades to use another player's artist to receive 1 food from the owner of the Juggler.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Teacher of Nations}{Lehrer der Nationen}{\v{C}04}{(4--5 players)}
{All players can pay 1 food less whenever they play an occupation. Whenever one of the other players uses this discount, you receive 1 food from the general supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Does not lower the extra food cost of the \cardref{Lover}{Liebhaber}{K291} and \cardref{Chief}{Hðuptling}{E172}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hero}{Held}{\v{C}05}{(1--5 players)}
{You receive 3 food immediately. Once during the game, you can pay 1 wild boar to carry out a family growth action without placing one of your people. You must have room in your home. The newborn can start taking actions in the next round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Farm Steward}{Hofverwalter}{I233}, \cardref{Mother of Twins}{Zwillingsmutter}{Z336}, and \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267} when used.}
\item \ecp{Does not activate the \cardref{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127}.}
\item \ecp{You may pay for this with a wild boar that you receive from an action space or card, without having placed it in your farm.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/4083106]{If you use the Hero during the harvest after feeding your family, the new family member remains a newborn for the entire following round.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fortune Teller}{Wahrsagerin}{\v{C}06}{(1--5 players)}
{You immediately receive 1 stone from the general supply. Immediately look at the top 3 cards of the round card deck, and return them face down to the top of the deck, in any order you choose. You may look at the action card of the next round at any time in the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{When returning the cards to the deck, you need not return the cards to their own stage.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}{(4--5 players)}
{Place up to 3 food from your personal supply on this card. Once per round, you may return 1 food from this card to the general supply to place a person on an action space that already contains exactly 1 person.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can use an action space containing your own or another player's person.}
\item \ecp{You cannot use an action space already containing 2 persons, for example a family growth space containing a parent and child, or because of the \cardref{Field Warden}{Flursch■tze}{E163}.}
\item \cardtext{You may return food from this card to your personal supply at any time.} \ecp{Until you do, it is not part of your personal supply, and does not count for e.g.\ \cardref{Pilgrim}{?}{G045}.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/4124105]{If the start player action is used more than once in a round, the last player to use it will be the start payer next round.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/359723]{It is not allowed to use an empty accumulating action space such as \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood}, not even if it activates other improvements or occupations. It is allowed to use an empty accumulating action space that produces other resources directly, such as \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Bagpiper}{Dudelsackpfeifer}{\v{C}08}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive 2 food immediately. The person who took the occupation action immediately returns home, as if he has not been used this round. The action space ``Occupation'' is now unoccupied, and can be used again.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Use the returned family member again as soon as it's your turn again.}
\item \ecp{You can only return a person home if you use an action space with an ``occupation'' action. If you play the Bagpiper in another way, e.g.\ by using the \cardref{Puppeteer}{Puppenspieler}{I249} or the \cardref{School}{Schule}{\v{C}14}, you cannot return your family member home, but you do receive 2 food.}
\item \ecp{The person counts only once for the \cardref{Church Warden}{Gemeindevorsteher}{I227}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Only Child}{Einzelkind}{\v{C}09}{(3--5 players)}
{You receive wood immediately when you play this card: if played in round 9, 10, or 11, take 1 wood; if played in round 6, 7, or 8, take 2 wood; if played before round 6, take 3 wood. At the end of the game, you receive 3 bonus points if you have exactly 3 family members.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Guests \ecp{or the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138}} do not count as family member.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Informer}{Spitzel}{\v{C}10}{(1--5 players)}
{Immediately turn 1 of your occupations before you face down. You receive your choice of 5 food or 1 cattle from the general supply. You lose all effects of the face down occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The face down card still counts as played for determining future occupation costs and for requirements of improvements.}
\item \ecp[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1209]{You cannot choose to turn the Informer itself face down.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Robber}{Rðuber}{\v{C}11}{(4--5 players)}
{Once per round, you can skip placing a family member when it's your turn. Instead, you take your choice of 1 food or 1 wood from the general supply. You can only skip your turn if at least one other player still has at least one person left to place.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Later in this round, you can still place the person that you would have placed this turn.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Nicholas}{Nikolaus}{\v{C}12}{(3--5 players)}
{Immediately take 1 food from the general supply for each family member that has been born during the game so far, but no more than 6 food. All players with the least number of offspring (possibly including you) get 1 vegetable each.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Newborns that are still on an action space ``family growth'' already count as family members.}
\item \ecp{Guests and the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} are not offspring and do not count.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Alternative Designer}{?}{G001}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you build stables or fences, you may replace wood with the same amount of clay or stone. Whenever you build rooms, you may replace wood with the same amount of clay or stone, to a maximum of 2 clay and 2 stone.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/335780]{Can be used for every room you build, if you build more than 1 room; e.g.\ you can build 2 rooms for 2 wood, 4 reed, 4 clay, and 4 stone.}
\item \ecp{You may use other cards that change the costs of a room or a renovation together with the Alternative Designer for the same action, in any order.}
\item \ecp{You may also use this card for clay or stone rooms, e.g.\ if you also have \cardref{Brushwood Roof}{Reisigdach}{K136} or \cardref{Clay Supports}{Lehmstake}{E37}.}
\item \ecp{If you also have \cardref{Frame Builder}{Balkenschlðger}{K272}, you may use the cards in any order, e.g.\ to build wooden rooms for 3 wood and 2 reed, or clay rooms for 4 clay and 2 reed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Farmer}{?}{G002}{(1--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 1 bonus point for each of your pastures that cannot contain any more animals than it does. If all of your pastures qualify, you receive 1 additional bonus point.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{To receive the additional point, you need to have at least 1 pasture.}
\item \ecp{When calculating the capacity of your pastures, you have to take into account fenced stables and the \cardref{Drinking Trough}{Trðnke}{E59} and \cardref{Shepherd's Pipe}{Hornfl—te}{E29}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=522]{You can also get points for \cardref{Animal Yard}{Tierhof}{E58} and \cardref{Wildlife Reserve}{Tiergarten}{I102}.}
\item \ecp{You can only receive a point for \cardref{Night Pasture}{Hutanger}{M084} if all other players have 1 animal on this card (and you 3).}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=522]{If you have \cardref{Forest Pasture}{Waldweide}{K145}, you never receive a point for that card or the additional bonus point.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Animal Holder}{?}{G003}{(3--5 players)}
{If there are still 1/3/6/9 rounds to play, you immediately receive 1/2/3/4 wood. At the end of the game, each player who has the most animals receives 3 bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Minor improvements such as \cardref{House Goat}{Hausziege}{K120} and \cardref{Horse}{Pferd}{K135} do not count.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Apprentice}{?}{G004}{(3--5 players)}
{At the beginning of every harvest, you receive 1 food for every major improvement you own worth at least 2 points without counting bonus points.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you have purchased a major improvement as a minor improvement, e.g.\ with \cardref{Ceramics}{Keramik}{E33} or \cardref{Well Builder}{Brunnenbauer}{I220}, that improvement still counts for this card.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/479630]{Upgrades of major improvements (e.g.\ \cardref{Baker's Oven}{Backofen}{E14} and \cardref{Village Well}{Dorfbrunnen}{I66}) also count, even if they are minor improvements as well.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Architect}{?}{G005}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you extend your home, you receive 2 food for each new room. Whenever you build stables, you receive 1 food for each new stable.}

\card{Artisan}{?}{G006}{(1--5 players)}
{At most once per harvest, when you use an improvement to convert a building resource to food, you receive 2 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is not activated by occupations, such as \cardref{Turner}{Drechsler}{E158} and \cardref{Potter}{T—pfer}{E214}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Astronomer}{?}{G007}{(3--5 players)}
{When you play this card, you receive 2 food. Whenever 3/4/5 of your family members (or guests) use 3/4/5 adjacent action spaces (forming a vertical or horizontal line), you receive 1/3/5 bonus points. The action spaces must have the same \changed[dimensions]{size}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2227]{Bonus points from the Astronomer are counted at the end of the turn when all persons has been placed, and before they return home.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2227]{If you move persons ar the end of the turn, e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Pond Watchman}{?}{G046}, only their new location counts.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=453]{Action spaces on minor improvements, or introduced into the game by the \cardref{Clay Digger}{Gruber}{I230} or \cardref{Master Forester}{Forstwirt}{E164}, never count for the Astronomer.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2227]{The cards with action spaces on the leftmost game board should be placed randomly at the start of the game. If they weren't, shuffle them when Astronomer is played. In a 3 player game, the cards fill the top 2 rows on the board.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Auctioneer}{?}{G008}{(4--5 players)}
{Place 2 reed, 3 wood, 3 clay, and 2 stone on rounds 7, 9, 11 and 13, respectively. At the start of these rounds, all players simultaneously bid food for the resources. The highest bidder gets the resources and you get the food. If you win, pay your food to the \changed{general} supply. Ties are broken by this round's player order.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{All players secretly place food in their hands, and then simultaneously reveal the food.}
\item \ecp{This round's start player wins ties, even if another player has taken the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space this round.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Baker's Daughter}{?}{G009}{(3--5 players)}
{If another player plays the \cardref{Baker}{Bðcker}{E150} or \cardref{Master Baker}{Backðltester}{E149}, you may play this card immediately at no cost. You can use the \actionref{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain} and \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} action spaces even if another player has placed a person on the space. When you play this card, you can immediately take a \changed[``Bake bread'']{bread baking} action.}

\card{Bard}{?}{G010}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player uses the ``Traveling players'' action on an action space, you receive 1 food and 1 wood from the \changed{general} supply.}

\card{Carrot Cake Baker}{?}{G011}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you convert vegetables into food, you may additionally take \changed[the ``Bake bread'']{a bread baking} action. The Carrot Cake Baker can also convert 1 vegetable into 2 food at any time.}

\card{Carrot Farmer}{?}{G012}{(1--5 players)}
{Place 3 vegetables from the \changed{general} supply on this card. Whenever you use the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} action space, you may pay 1 food for one of the vegetables.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{The vegetables are not part of your personal supply until you buy them.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Clay Starter}{?}{G013}{(1--5 players)}
{When you play this card, if you only have 2 rooms in your wooden hut, immediately pay 1 food to renovate it to clay for free.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Has no effect if you have more than 2 rooms or live in a clay hut or stone house when you play this card.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Early Riser}{?}{G014}{(1--5 players)}
{When you play this card, you receive 1 sheep. For you, the breeding phase of the harvest precedes the field and feeding phases. You may immediately cook baby animals if you do not have room to keep them.}

\card{Family Counselor}{?}{G015}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever at the end of a work phase all of your adult family members were placed on the same \changed{game board}, you receive 1 food/1 grain/1 vegetable if it were 2/3/4+ adults.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Newborns do not count, unless they took an action because of \cardref{Adoptive Parents}{Adoptiveltern}{K267}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2327]{Guests count as family members for this card.}
\item \ecp{If you move a person, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Pond Watchman}{?}{G046}, the location of your family members after you've moved them counts.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=453]{Action spaces on minor improvements, or introduced into the game by the \cardref{Clay Digger}{Gruber}{I230} or \cardref{Master Forester}{Forstwirt}{E164}, are not on any game board.}
\item \ecp{(\MOOR) The \actionref{Infirmary}{Infirmary} is a separate game board; if all of your family members take that action, you receive the bonus from the Family Counselor.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fence Helper}{?}{G016}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player takes a \changed[``Build fences'']{fence building} action, you may pay that player 1 food to immediately take \changed[the ``Fences'']{a fence building action} too.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Pay costs normally.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1976]{Is activated whenever another player builds fences, including e.g.\ when someone uses the \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}, or plays the \cardref{Mini Pasture}{Miniweide}{E40}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fish Seller}{?}{G017}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action, you may use food that you take from that action space to buy up to 2 items. One building resource costs 1 food. One grain, sheep or wild boar costs 2 food. One vegetable or cattle costs 3 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The items can be the same or different.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=441]{Only the food that was lying on the action space can be used to buy animals. If you use e.g. the \cardref{Fishing Rod}{Angel}{E12} or \cardref{Fisherman}{Fischer}{E161}, the additional food cannot be used.}
\item \ecp{You may immediately convert the animals into food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for them in your farmyard. However, you may not use that food to buy more animals with the Fish Seller.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Fisherman's Apprentice}{?}{G018}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player uses the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action, you may pay that player 1 food to play an occupation.}

\card{Food Critic}{?}{G019}{(1--5 players)}
{The next time you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action, place 1 food from the \changed{general} supply on this card. Whenever you convert animals, vegetables, grain, or building resources to food, you may place that good on this card. At the end of the game, you receive 1/2/4/6 bonus points for 4/5/6/7+ different items on this card.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.}
\item \ecp{The markers on this card are not part of your personal supply. They do not count for \cardref{Storehouse Clerk}{Lagerhalter}{K287}, \cardref{Joinery}{Tischlerei}{A7}, etc.}
\item \ecp{There is no need to put food or a good on this card if it already contains that type of marker. The second marker of the same type has no effect.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Freeloader}{?}{G020}{(3--5 players)}
{Each round, your first family member may use an occupied action space. Your first family member can never take the \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} action space.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{You can't even take \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} if it is unoccupied.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2337]{If the first person you place is a guest marker, it counts as the first family member.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/359723]{It is not allowed to use an empty accumulating action space such as \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood}, not even if it activates other improvements or occupations. It is allowed to use an empty accumulating action space that produces other resources directly, such as \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hermit}{?}{G021}{(4--5 players)}
{At the end of the game, you receive 6 bonus points if this is the only occupation you have played.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you have played \cardref{Dance Instructor}{Tanzlehrer}{Z334} and returned it to your hand, it does not count as played, and you may still score points for the \cardref{Hermit}{?}{G021}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Glass Blower}{?}{G022}{(3--5 players)}
{If you have an oven, the Glassblower may convert 1/2 clay to 3/5 food in each harvest.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=582]{The clay is converted into food by this occupation, not by the oven. This does not activate the \cardref{Artisan}{?}{G006}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Glutton}{?}{G023}{(1--5 players)}
{In the feeding phase of the last harvest after feeding your family normally, you may pay 3 additional food for 1 bonus point, up to a maximum of 6 bonus points.}

\card{Grafter}{?}{G024}{(1--5 players)}
{During the breeding phase of harvest, if you have 2 or more grain in your \changed{personal} supply, you receive 1 grain from the \changed{general} supply. If you have 2 or more vegetables, you receive 1 vegetable from the \changed{general} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Vegetables and grains that are planted are not counted.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Businesswoman}{?}{G025}{(1--5 players)}
{When you play this card, immediately play up to 2 improvements (any combination of major and minor) by paying their costs.}

\card{Grain Farmer}{?}{G026}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you have at least 1/4/7/10 planted grain at the beginning of the field phase of a harvest, you receive 1/2/3/4 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=690]{The total number of grain on your fields (including \cardref{Acreage}{Ackerflðche}{K105}) is counted, not the number of grain fields.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Grain Lover}{?}{G027}{(3--5 players)}
{If there are still 7 full rounds to play, you may plow 1 field, which you may immediately sow with 1 grain from your \changed{personal} supply. At the end of the game, all players with the most total grain receive 2 bonus points each.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may plough a field and not sow it.}
\item \ecp{Sowing the grain counts as a sowing action, and activates e.g. the \cardref{Smallholder}{Kleinbauer}{K286}, \cardref{Seasonal Plants}{-}{G104.}, and another player's \cardref{Field Worker}{Feldarbeiter}{I224}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Grump}{?}{G028}{(3--5 players)}
{If there are still 1/3/6/9 rounds to play, you immediately receive 1/2/3/4 wood. At the end of the game, all players with the fewest family members receive 2 binus points each.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Guests and the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} do not count as family members.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Harbor Master}{?}{G029}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, you receive 1 additional reed. Whenever another player uses the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space, you receive 1 reed and 1 food from the \changed{general} supply.}

\card{Headmaster}{?}{G030}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever another player plays an occupation, place 1 food from the supply on this card. Whenever you play an occupation, you may pay any costs using food from this card. At the end of a 4/5 player game, you receive 1 bonus point for every 3/4 food on this card.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You may first receive the food from the Headmaster before using the \cardref{Educator}{Ausbilder}{K271}. The cost of using the Educator may also be paid with food from the Headmaster.}
\item \ecp{The food on this card is not part of your personal supply. It cannot be used for anything else than paying for occupations.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Helper}{?}{G031}{(3--5 players)}
{You can use any ``Renovate'', ``Build room(s)'' or ``Major Improvement'' action space, even if another player has already placed a person on it.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \apx[Head of the Family]{You may not use the same action space in the same round with 2 of your own people.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=925]{If the action space provides a choice of actions, you may choose either. For example, you may take the ``Traveling Players'' action on the \actionref{Build 1 Room or Traveling Players}{BuildX1XRoomXorXTravelingXPlayers} action space in the 5-player game, or play a minor improvement on the \actionref{Major/Minor Improvement}{MajorXMinorXImprovement} action space.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=925]{If the action space allows two actions, you may take both. For example, you may use the \actionref{Build Rooms and Stables}{BuildXRoomsXandXStables} action space to build both a room and a stable.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/359723]{It is not allowed to use an empty accumulating action such as ``Traveling Players'', not even if it activates other improvements or occupations.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=925]{You cannot use the Helper to take a ``minor improvement only'' action space, such as \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer}, even if you have the \cardref{Traveling Salesman}{Handelsreisender}{K281}. Similarly, the \cardref{Pulley}{-}{G097} does not make \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} a ``Build room(s)'' action space, etc.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hobbyist}{?}{G032}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player plays an occupation, you may pay 1 food to the general supply to play 1 minor improvement, or 2 food to build 1 major improvement.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Pay costs for the improvements normally.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Hoe Maker}{?}{G033}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you build at least 1 fence, you may also pay 1 food to plough 1 field.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=775]{Is activated by any fence building action, including e.g.\ \cardref{Mini Pasture}{Miniweide}{E40}, \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}, and \cardref{Paddocks}{-}{G090}.} 
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Inventor}{?}{G034}{(1--5 players)}
{All improvements with a printed cost of 4 or more resources cost you 1 less resource of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=784]{You may use other cards that change the costs of an improvement, e.g.\ \cardref{Stonecutter}{Steinschneider}{E211}, together with the Inventor for the same action.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Job Seeker}{?}{G035}{(4--5 players)}
{Once in play, this card does not count as an occupation for any purpose. Whenever, at the start of a round, you have fewer occupations than any 2 other players, you may pay 1 food to immediately play an occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Occupations played this way, e.g.\ the \cardref{Dance Instructor}{Tanzlehrer}{Z334}, may not be returned to the player's hand.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Late Bloomer}{?}{G036}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you have fewer family members than all of the other players and you have room in your home, you may immediately take a ``family growth'' action. You need room in your home for the offspring. Place the offspring in an empty room. This family member is not considered a newborn and may take an action the same round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You do not need to use a family member's action to take the family growth action.}
\item \ecp{Guests and the occupant of the Reed Hut are not counted in the size of the families.}% See Midwife
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=874]{You do not have to use this card immediately when all other players have more family members than you. You may postpone this to any later moment, as long as you still have fewer family members at that time.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Late Sleeper}{?}{G037}{(4--5 players)}
{At the start of each round, announce whether or not you will sleep late. If you sleep late, you place all of your people after everyone else has placed all of theirs, but you may also place a guest token.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{If you choose not to sleep late, you place your people normally.}
\item \ecp{You must choose whether to sleep late before the start of the work phase.}
