\item \ecp{If you sleep late, you place your people after all guests of other players, including the one from the \cardref{Keg}{Bierfass}{Z314}, but before moving a person (e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Pond Watchman}{?}{G046}).}% See Neutrality.
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=799]{If you play \cardref{Neutrality}{Neutralitðt}{ø16} and choose to sleep late the next round, Neutrality has no effect, and you do not receive bonus points.}
\item \ecp{If you sleep late and another player played Neutrality the previous round, both of you take alternating turns placing your people, in player order.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=799]{If you sleep late, you may not use the \cardref{Taster}{Vorkoster}{I260}. If you used the \cardref{Coffee House}{Kaffeehaus}{ø13} last round, it has no effect: you may not place that person first.}% See Neutrality
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/586610]{The guest does not need to be fed.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Master Baker's Apprentice}{?}{G038}{(1--5 players)}
{When you play this card, mark a revealed action space with an arrow marker. This action space now has the added text ``and/or bake bread''. Whenever another player bakes bread using this space, you receive 1 food from the general supply. When you play this card, you may also take \changed[the ``Bake bread'']{a bread baking} action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1925]{If you put the marker on \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread}, anyone may now take two consecutive baking actions on that space (using all of their ovens both times). If another player does that, you receive 2 food.}
\item \ecp{If the \cardref{Chamberlain}{Kðmmerer}{I238} has been played, and you play the Master Baker's Apprentice in round 11 or later, you may also put the marker on the round card of rounds 12 to 14.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mathematician}{?}{G039}{(4--5 players)}
{From round 6 \changed{on}, if there are wood spaces with the same amount of wood after refilling each round (at the end of phase 2), you can take 1 wood from one of those spaces. This also applies to clay action spaces. In 5 player games, this also applies to stone action spaces. You can take only 1 resource per round.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2429]{Is activated before the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} can distribute wood.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Miner}{?}{G040}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, you can take all the stone markers from one of the \actionref{1 Stone}{1XStone} action spaces (stage 2 or stage 4) in the returning home phase (phase 4).
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{When you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, place a claim marker on both action spaces.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Mooch}{?}{G041}{(3--5 players)}
{When you play this card, choose another player. Until the end of the next harvest, you may convert animals, vegetables, grain, and building resources to food as if you owned the chosen player's improvements in addition to yours.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The chosen player may use their improvements normally.}
\item \ecp{You may use the other player's baking improvements whenever you take a bread baking action.}
\item \ecp{When the other player plays an oven or another improvement that gives them a bread baking action, you may not bake bread at the same time. When they play \cardref{Barbecue}{Grillfest}{Z318}, you may not use it at the same time.}
\item \ecp{You may not use the other player's \cardref{Grain Distillery}{-}{M030}, because you cannot use the Mooch to convert fuel to food.}
\item \ecp{You may not use the other player's occupations, e.g.\ \cardref{Turner}{Drechsler}{E158} or \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}.}
\item \ecp{You may use your own \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162} if you don't have an oven but the other player does.}
\item \ecp{In the harvest, you can use the other player's \cardref{Windmill}{Bockm■hle}{E17} without paying for it.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Oldest Occupation}{?}{G042}{(4--5 players)}
{From round 5 \changed{on}, whenever any player uses the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space, they may pay you 2 food to immediately take a ``family growth'' action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{They must have room in their house.}
\item \cardtext{If you use \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer}, you may grow for free.}
\item \ecp{Other players may use the food from the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action to pay you.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2203]{Place the newborn on the person that used the Day Labourer action space. The action space cannot be used again with \cardref{Understudy}{?}{G056}.}
\item \ecp{Although one can now take a family growth action when using Day Labourer, that does not make Day Labourer a ``family growth action space'', e.g.\ for \cardref{Head of the Family}{Familienoberhaupt}{E159} or \cardref{Clapper}{Klapper}{K127}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2174]{If you also have the \cardref{Pulley}{-}{G097}, you may first use it to build a new room and then the Oldest Occupation to grow a family member there.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Opportunist}{?}{G043}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use your last action in a round to take one or more types of building resources that have not yet been taken this work phase, you receive 1 additional resource of one of those types.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reeds, and stone.}
\item \ecp{Only building resources that are taken directly from an action space are counted. Building resources received from other cards are not.}
\item \ecp{If you move a person at the end of a round, e.g.\ because of the \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} or \cardref{Pond Watchman}{?}{G046}, that counts as your last action.}% Compare Magician, which says "last person".
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pearl Seeker}{?}{G044}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space you receive 1 additional stone. Also, you can use food that you take from that action space to buy more stone. Each stone costs 2 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1984]{Only the food that was lying on the action space can be used to buy stone. If you use e.g. the \cardref{Fishing Rod}{Angel}{E12} or \cardref{Fisherman}{Fischer}{E161}, the additional food cannot be used.}% See Fish Seller
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pilgrim}{?}{G045}{(1--5 players)}
{You receive 2 food before you pay the costs of playing this occupation. At the start of a round, if you have no building resources, you may take 1 building resource from the \changed{general} supply; if you have no food, you may take 1 food from the \changed{general} supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2377]{Only resources and food in your personal supply count. Wood or food planted on \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78} or \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21} do not count.}
\item \cardtext{At any time, you may move resources from your personal supply to the general supply.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reeds, and stone.}
\item \ecp{If you receive food or building resources at the start of the round, e.g.\ because of \cardref{Rancher}{Landmann}{I340} or \cardref{Duck Pond}{Ententeich}{K114}, you may use the Pilgrim before you receive those food or resources. You can also use cards like \cardref{Greengrocer}{Gem■sehðndler}{E168} to spend food on resources, and then use the Pilgrim to get the food back. However, if you use e.g.\ the \cardref{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184} to buy a building resource for a food, you may only activate the Pilgrim once; either before the Grocer (to get a building resource) or after the Grocer (to get a food), not both. If you want to receive both food and a building resource, you have to receive them at the same time.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Pond Watchman}{?}{G046}{(4--5 players)}
{At the end of a work phase, after all other players have taken their actions, you may pay 1 food to move one of your people that used the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action this round to an \changed{unoccupied} wood accumulating action space and take that action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1985]{You may not move your person to the \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} action space, or to an action space that contains wood because of the \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2383]{You may move your person to the action space introduced by the \cardref{Master Forester}{Forstwirt}{E164}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2383]{If you have already used a family member on the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space before you play this card, you may move this family member at the end of the round.}
\item \ecp{Moving a person with the Pond Watchman counts as taking an action, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Opportunist}{?}{G043}, but not as placing your last person, e.g.\ for the \cardref{Magician}{Zauberk■nstler}{K311}, because this person has already been placed previously.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=1256]{If the \cardref{Acrobat}{Akrobat}{K269} or \cardref{Countryman}{Landwirt}{K289} also have been played, the family members are moved in player order, starting with the player left of the one who placed the last regular person. If you can move more than one person, you move them consecutively in an order of your choice.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Resource Collector}{?}{G047}{(1--5 players)}
{Place 1 wood, 1 clay, 1 reed, and 1 stone on the next 4 round spaces in any order you choose. At the start of those rounds, you receive the resource.}

\card{Ringmaster}{?}{G048}{(4--5 players)}
{When you use the ``Traveling Players'' action, you may either play a minor improvement or you may pay 1 grain to build a major improvement immediately afterward.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Pay costs for the improvement normally.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=486]{If you receive grain because of \cardref{Conjurer}{Gaukler}{E167} or \cardref{Magician}{Zauberk■nstler}{K311}, \ecp{or if you use the food from \actionref{Traveling Players}{TravelingXPlayers} to buy grain from the \cardref{Grocer}{Krðmer}{E184},} you may immediately use that grain to pay for a major improvement.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Seed Master}{?}{G049}{(1--5 players)}
{At any time, you may pay 1 food to convert 1 grain in your \changed{personal} supply to 1 vegetable. At any time, you may convert 1 vegetable in your \changed{personal} supply to 1 grain.}

\card{Singer}{?}{G050}{(1--5 players)}
{When you play this card, you receive 2 building resources of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{The building resources can be the same or different.}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stone Deliveryman}{?}{G051}{(3--5 players)}
{Place 1 stone on each of the spaces for rounds 8, 10, 12, and 14. At the start of these rounds, you receive the stone.}

\card{Stone Trader}{?}{G052}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use an action to take stone, you may immediately afterward pay 1 food to play an improvement that has a printed stone cost.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Pay costs for the improvement normally.}
\item \ecp{You can play either a minor or a major improvement.}
\item \ecp{Is activated when you use an action space on which stone is placed each round. You cannot use such an action space just to use this card if the action space contains no stone (e.g.\ when you have the \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}.)}
\item \ecp{Is activated by the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood} in 4-player games and the action space \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=722]{Is not activated when you receive stone because of a minor improvement or occupation.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Stonepiler}{?}{G053}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you build fences or stables, you may pay some or all of the cost in stone with each stone worth 2 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{If you have to pay an odd number of wood, you can round up the number of stone you pay, e.g.\ pay 2 stone for 3 fences.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Tax Collector}{?}{G054}{(3--5 players)}
{Whenever another player pays building recources to build a major improvement, you receive 1 resource of those paid (of your choice). You may pay 1 food to the general supply to receive another of the resources paid.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=694.0]{Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Truffle Digger}{?}{G055}{(4--5 players)}
{Whenever you use a family member's action to take wood that is on an accumulating action space and you have 1/2/3 wild boar, you receive 1/2/3 additional food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{Is not activated when you use the \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} action space in the 5-player game.}% Compare Wood Cart
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2333]{Is activated when you use an accumulating action space that contains wood because of the Wood Distributor.}
\item \ecp{If you use an action space that contains wood, and you leave all the wood on the action space because of \cardref{Basket}{Korb}{E34}, \cardref{Mushroom Collector}{Pilzsucher}{E196}, or \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253}, you still receive the food from the Truffle Digger.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=468]{You may first take a wild boar with \cardref{Pig Catcher}{Schweinsfðnger}{I253} before you use the Truffle Digger.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Understudy}{?}{G056}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever an action space is occupied by exactly one of your family members, you may use that action space again with a second family member.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Newborns count as family members,} \ecp{so you cannot use this card for a family growth action space.}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/359723]{It is not allowed to use an empty accumulating action space such as \actionref{3 Wood}{3XWood}, not even if it activates other improvements or occupations. It is allowed to use an empty accumulating action space that produces other resources directly, such as \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Vegetarian}{?}{G057}{(1--5 players)}
{For each grain or vegetable you convert to food (in any manner), you receive 1 additional food. You may not convert animals to food for the rest of the game.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=431]{You may no longer use a cooking improvement, the \cardref{Barbecue}{Grillfest}{Z318}, \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}, \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}, \cardref{Action Artist}{Aktionsk■nstler}{ø02}, or \cardref{Butcher's Block}{Schlachtbank}{M088} to convert animals to food. You may still receive food from the \cardref{Slaughterman}{Schlachter}{K299}, \cardref{Slaughterhouse}{Schlachthof}{I97}, \cardref{Milking Stool}{Melkschemel}{K133}, etc.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Village Farmer}{?}{G058}{(3--5 players)}
{If there are still 1/3/6/9 rounds to play, you immediately receive 1/2/3/4 wood. At the end of the game, all players who have the most plowed fields receive 3 bonus points each.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1934]{Fields on cards, such as \cardref{Bean Field}{Bohnenfeld}{E18} and \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, do not count. Fields with more than one stack of grain because of the \cardref{Scarecrow}{Vogelscheuche}{Z324} count as only 1 field.}% See Rake.
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wheedler}{?}{G059}{(1--5 players)}
{Whenever you receive food from an action space, you receive 1 additional food. This benefit does not apply to food gained due to an improvement or occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=971]{Is activated when you use a minor improvement that is an action space, e.g.\ the \cardref{Tavern}{Taverne}{I100} or \cardref{Spielefest}{Spielefest}{ø14}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=971]{Is activated when you use an action space that contains food because of the \cardref{Foreman}{Vorarbeiter}{K308}.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=971]{Is not activated when you use the \cardref{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\card{Wintercrafter}{?}{G060}{(1--5 players)}
{Between the field and feeding phases of each harvest, you may play a minor improvement or pay 2 food to build a major improvement.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \cardtext{Pay the costs of the improvement normally.}
\item \ruling[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=2368]{A harvest counts as part of the preceding round. If you also have the \cardref{Wood Carver}{Schnitzer}{K301}, you may use it if you didn't already in the round that preceded the harvest.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline

\section{Action spaces}

\action{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}
{Take all resources from this action space and put them in your supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Accumulating spaces are spaces with arrows, on which resources or food are placed at the start of every round.
\item \ecp{You cannot use an accumulating action space if there are no resources on it for any reason (e.g.~because of \cardref{Wood Distributor}{Holzverteiler}{K284} or \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}), unless you receive other benefits directly from the action space (as on \actionref{1 Reed, Stone, and Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood} in 5-player games, and \actionref{Starting Player}{StartingXPlayer} in the family game).}\end{explanationlist}}
}

\subsection{Fixed action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{Build room(s) and/or Build Stable(s)}{BuildXRoomsXandXStables}
{You may build rooms, or build stables, or both (in any order). You have to perform at least one of these actions.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may build multiple rooms and stables in one action.
\item \emph{Build Rooms} Each room costs 2 reeds and 5 wood/clay/stone, depending on the type of your hut or house. New rooms must be of the same material as your existing hut or house.
\item Each new room must be orthogonally adjacent to at least one existing room.
\item You may never move a room, nor remove one from your board.
\item \emph{Build Stables} Each stable costs 2 wood, and must be placed immediately on a farmyard space.
\item A stable can be placed on an unfenced empty farmyard space, or in a pasture. Each farmyard space can hold 1 stable.
\item A pasture can have as many stables as it has farmyard spaces. Each stable doubles the capacity of the pasture (so a pasture with 3 stables can store 16 animals per farmyard space).
\item You may never move a stable, nor remove one from your board.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Starting Player and/or 1 Minor Improvement}{StartingXPlayer}
{You can become the starting player, or play one minor improvement, or do both. You have to perform at least one of these actions.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you choose to become the new starting player, the playing order will change at the end of the current round, before a possible subsequent harvest.% See http://www.cliquenabend.de/index.php?page=artikel&artikel=agricolawerkstattbericht&seite=1#27
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/466016]{You can use this action space to become the new starting player even if you already are, without playing a minor improvement.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/501154]{If this action space is not used in a round, the starting player doesn't change.}
\item \ecp[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/article/4134924]{If this action space is used more than once in a round (e.g.~with \cardref{Bureaucrat}{B■rokrat}{\v{C}07}), the last player to use it will be the start payer next round.}
\item \ecp[http://play-agricola.com/forums/index.php?topic=1775.0]{You may take this action space in round 14, even if you don't play a minor improvement.}\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Take 1 Grain}{TakeX1XGrain}
{Take 1 grain from the general supply and place it in your own supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item No grain is placed on this action space; it does not accumulate from round to round.
\item You may not sow the grain immediately, even if you have empty fields.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField}
{Place 1 field tile on an unfenced, unused farmyard space of your choice.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may only place 1 tile per action.
\item If you already have fields, the new field must be orthogonally adjacent to at least one of the existing fields.
\item You may never move a field tile, nor remove one from your board.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{1 Occupation}{1XOccupation}
{Play 1 occupation card from your hand. If you do not yet have any occupations in front of you, this one is free; each additional occupation costs 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may only play 1 occupation per action.
\item \ruling[http://forum.lookout-games.de/index.php?topic=693.0]{In a solo game, if you have kept occupations from previous games, the first occupation played in the current game costs 1 food as well.}\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer}
{Take 2 food from the general supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item No food is placed on this action space; it does not accumulate from round to round.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{3 Wood}{3XWood}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item In the solo game, add only 2 wood to this action space every round.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{1 Clay}{1XClay}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{1 Reed}{1XReed}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{Fishing}{Fishing}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{Stage 1 action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{Fences}{Fences}
{Build as many fences as you want, for 1 wood per fence.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item A fence that has been built may not be moved or demolished.
\item At the end of any turn, there may not be any unfinished pastures.
\item Huts do not create a natural border for a pasture; a pasture must be surrounded by fences even along the side(s) of a hut. This also applies to the edges of the game board, fields and stables.
\item If you already have pastures, a new pasture must be orthogonally adjacent to at least one of the existing pastures.
\item An existing pasture may be divided into several pastures by adding fences.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{1 Major or Minor Improvement}{MajorXMinorXImprovement}
{You may play a minor improvement from your hand, or buy a major improvement.}

\action{1 Sheep}{1XSheep}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You can place the sheep on your farm, convert them to food, or return them to the general supply.
\item Sheep can be converted to food with a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}, \cardref{Cooking Corner}{Kochecke}{I85}, \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}, or \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.
\item You can take this action even if you have to return all of the animals to the general supply.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Sow and/or Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread}
{You may sow, bake bread, or both (in any order). You have to perform at least one of these actions.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \emph{Sowing} Take grain and/or vegetables from your supply and place them on empty fields in your farmyard. Place 2 grain from the general supply on each sown grain, and 1 vegetable from the general supply on each sown vegetable.
\item You may sow as few or as many grain or vegetables in one action as you want, but only one per empty field.
\item You need not sow all your empty fields, some may be left empty.
\item You may sow both grain and vegetables in the same turn.
\item \emph{Baking Bread} Take grain from your supply and use an appropriate improvement to convert it to food.
\item You cannot use grain that is on one of your fields.
\item You may convert as many grain into food as you want, unless the used improvement states a limitation.
\item You may use multiple improvements in the same baking action.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{Stage 2 action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{After Renovation also 1 Major or Minor Improvement}{RenovationXandXImprovement}
{Renovate your home, and optionally play a minor improvement from your hand or buy a major improvement.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you use this action space, the renovation is mandatory. Playing or buying an improvement is optional, and follows the renovation.
\item \emph{Renovate} Turn a wooden hut into a clay hut for 1 clay per room and 1 reeds in total, or a clay hut into a stone hut for 1 stone per room and 1 reeds in total.
\item You may not undertake both renovations (renovating to clay to stone) in one action.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{1 Stone}{1XStone}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{After Family Growth also 1 Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement}
{Grow your family, and optionally play a minor improvement from your hand.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you use this action space, the family growth is mandatory. Playing an improvement is optional, and follows the family growth.
\item You can only use this action space if the number of your rooms is, at the moment of using the action, at least one higher than the number of your family members.
\item \emph{Family Growth} Take a new family member marker, and put it on top of the marker that took this action.
\item The new family member can be used to take actions starting next round. In this turn, it is a ``newborn''; if there is a harvest after this round, you pay only 1 food to feed it.
\item You can have no more than 5 family members.
\item Guests and the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138} do not count as a family member.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{Stage 3 action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{1 Wild Boar}{1XWildXBoar}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You can place the wild boars on your farm, convert them to food, or return them to the general supply.
\item Wild boars can be converted to food with a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}, \cardref{Cooking Corner}{Kochecke}{I85}, \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}, or \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.
\item You can take this action even if you have to return all of the animals to the general supply.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Take 1 Vegetable}{TakeX1XVegetable}
{Take 1 vegetable from the general supply and place it in your own supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item No vegetables are placed on this action space; it does not accumulate from round to round.
\item You may not sow the vegetable immediately, even if you have empty fields.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{Stage 4 action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{1 Cattle}{1XCattle}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You can place the cattle on your farm, convert them to food, or return them to the general supply.
\item Cattle can be converted to food with a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}, \cardref{Cooking Corner}{Kochecke}{I85}, \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}, or \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.
\item You can take this action even if you have to return all of the animals to the general supply.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{1{ }Stone}{1XXXStone}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{Stage 5 action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{Plough 1 Field and/or Sow}{PloughXFieldXandXSow}
{You may plough 1 field, sow any number of fields, or both (in any order). You have to perform at least one of these actions.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \emph{Plough} See the \actionref{Plough 1 Field}{PloughX1XField} action space.
\item \emph{Sowing} See the \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} action space.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Family Growth even without space in your home}{FamilyXGrowthXwithoutXRoom}
{Grow your family, even if the number of your rooms is lower than, or equal to, the number of your family members.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If you have more rooms than family members, the newborn is considered to occupy a room immediately when it is born. If you only have one free room, you may not use this action space and a normal family growth in that order, unless you build more rooms first.
\item \emph{Family Growth} See the \actionref{Family Growth and Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement} (stage 2) action space.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{Stage 6 action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{After Renovation also Fences}{RenovationXandXFences}
{Renovate your home, and optionally build fences.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \emph{Renovation} See the \actionref{Renovation and Improvement}{RenovationXandXImprovement} (stage 2) action space.
\item \emph{Building Fences} See the \actionref{Fences}{Fences} (stage 1) action space.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{3 player action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{1 Occupation (2 food)}{1XOccupationXX2XfoodX}
{Play 1 occupation card from your hand. This occupation costs 2 food.}

\action{2 Wood}{2XWood}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{1{ }Clay}{1XXXClay}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{Take 1 Building Resource}{TakeX1XBuildingXResource}
{Take 1 Building Resource of your choice from the general supply, and place it in your personal supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Building resources are wood, clay, reed, and stone.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{4 player action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{1 Occupation (1 or 2 food)}{1XOccupationXX1XorX2XfoodX}
{Play 1 occupation card from your hand. If you have 0 or 1 occupations in front of you, this one costs 1 food; you pay 2 food if you already have more than one occupation.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may only play 1 occupation per action.
\item To determine the costs of the occupation, count all of the occupations in front of you, regardless of which action space you used to play them.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Take 1 Reed, 1 Stone and 1 Food}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXFood}
{Take 1 reed, 1 stone and 1 food from the general supply, and place them in your personal supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item No resources or food are placed on this action space; they do not accumulate from round to round.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Traveling Players}{TravelingXPlayers}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{1 Wood}{1XWood}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{2{ }Wood}{2XXXWood}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{2 Clay}{2XClay}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{5 player action spaces}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{1 Occupation or Family Growth}{1XOccupationXorXFamilyXGrowth}
{Either you may play 1 occupation from your hand, or (starting from round 5) you may grow your family. You have to do one of these actions if you use this space; you may not do both in the same turn.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Like all other action spaces, this one can be used only once per round. If one player chooses to play an occupation, another player cannot choose family growth on this action space.
\item \emph{Occupation} You may only play 1 occupation per action.
\item To determine the costs of the occupation, count all of the occupations in front of you, regardless of which action space you used to play them.
\item \emph{Family Growth} See the \actionref{Family Growth and Minor Improvement}{FamilyXGrowthXandXMinorXImprovement} (stage 2) action space.
\item You can only choose the family growth action if the number of your rooms is, at the moment of using the action, at least one higher than the number of your family members.
\item You may not play a minor improvement after the family growth.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{1 Reed, and Take 1 Stone and 1 Wood}{1XReedXXStoneXXandXWood}
{Take all reed from this action card, and 1 stone and 1 wood from the general supply, and put them in your personal supply.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item At the start of each round, add 1 reed to this action space from the general supply.
\item Stone and wood are not placed on this action space; they do not accumulate from round to round.
\item \ecp{You may take this action space even if it contains no reed (e.g.~because of the Bureaucrat). In this case, you receive only 1 stone and 1 wood.}\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Build 1 Room or Traveling Players}{BuildX1XRoomXorXTravelingXPlayers}
{Either you may build 1 room, or you may take all food from this action card and put them into your personal supply. You may not do both in the same turn.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item At the start of each round, add 1 food to this action space from the general supply.
\item Like all other action spaces, this one can be used only once per round. If one player chooses to build a room, another player cannot choose traveling players on this action space.
\item If this action space contains no food (e.g.~because of the Bureaucrat), you must build a room when you use this action space.
\item You may not build more than 1 room in one action when you use this action space.
\item \emph{Build Room} See the \actionref{Build Rooms and Stables}{BuildXRoomsXandXStables} action space.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Take 1 Sheep or 1 Wild Boar or 1 Cattle}{SheepXXWildXBoarXXorXCattle}
{Either take 1 sheep and 1 food from the general supply, or take 1 wild boar, or pay 1 food and take 1 cattle. You may only take 1 animal in one turn.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Place the animal in your farm, convert it to food, or return it to the general supply immediately.
\item The animal can be converted to food with a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2}, \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}, \cardref{Cooking Corner}{Kochecke}{I85}, \cardref{Butcher}{Metzger}{I247}, or \cardref{Meat Seller}{Fleischer}{E162}, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{4 Wood}{4XWood}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\action{3 Clay}{3XClay}
{See \actionref{Accumulating spaces}{AccumulatingXspaces}.}

\end{multicols}
\sectionline
\subsection{Farmer of the Moor actions}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{Infirmary}{Infirmary}
{Take 1 food, and remove the bedmarker from the person taking this action.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You may use this action space with persons without bed markers as well.
\item Any number of persons can be placed on this action space in the same turn.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Black Market}{BlackXMarket}
{Play 1 minor improvement by paying its cost and 1 fuel.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If the improvement has any requirements, you must meet them.
\item If you cannot play an improvement, you may not take this action.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Clandestine Work}{ClandestineXWork}
{Build 1 minor or major improvement by paying its cost, 1 fuel, and 1 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item If the improvement has any requirements, you must meet them.
\item If you cannot play an improvement, you may not take this action.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Cut Peat}{CutXPeat}
{Return a moor tile from your farmyard to the general supply, and receive 3 fuel.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Cannot be taken if you do not have any remaining moor tiles.
\item \ecp{Does not count as ``taking fuel''.}
\item If there is more than 1 tile on a farmyard space, you can only return the top one.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Fell Trees}{FellXTrees}
{Return a forest tile from your farmyard to the general supply, and receive 2 wood.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Cannot be taken if you do not have any remaining forest tiles.
\item \ecp{Does not count as ``taking wood''.}
\item If there is more than 1 tile on a farmyard space, you can only return the top one.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Hiring Fair}{HiringXFair}
{Receive 1 food from the general supply (2 food in a 3-player game).}

\action{Horse Coper}{HorseXCoper}
{Take 1 horse from the general supply. In a 2- or 5-player game, this costs 1 food.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item You can place the horse on your farm, convert it to food, or return it to the general supply immediately.
\item A horse can be converted to food with an appropriate improvement, without having to make room for it in your farmyard.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn}
{Return a forest tile from your farmyard to the general supply, and replace it with a field tile on the same space.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Cannot be taken if you do not have any remaining forest tiles.
\item If you already have fields, this action can only be used for forests that are adjacent to your existing fields. If none of your forests border your fields, you cannot take this action.
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/521479]{Does not count as ploughing.}
\item Cannot be used for a famryard space that contains more than 1 tile.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\end{multicols}
\section{Through the Seasons}

\begin{multicols}{2}
\action{Winter}{Winter season}
{In the replenishment phase, add 1 fewer clay and 1 fewer reed to every space that you add these resources to.

\noindent You have to pay 1 food for \ecp{every} field you plough.
\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{This includes fields from \cardref{Field Watchman}{Feldh■ter}{I225}, ploughs, the \cardref{Harrow}{Egge}{I68}, etc. If you have the \cardref{Stump-Jump Plough}{Australischer Springpflug}{Z313}, \cardref{Plough Maker}{Pflugmacher}{E195}, \cardref{Ploughman}{Pfl■ger}{K293} or \cardref{Plough Driver}{Pflughalter}{E194}, or play the \cardref{Field}{Acker}{E11}, you pay 2 food in total.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/393776
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/521479]{(\MOOR) This does not include the special action \actionref{Slash and Burn}{SlashXandXBurn}}
\end{explanationlist}

\noindent You cannot use the \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing} action space during winter until round 11.
\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ruling[http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/354065]{You can't use the \cardref{Net Fisherman}{Netzer}{I248} either.}
\end{explanationlist}
}

\action{Winter action space}{Winter}
{Pay 2 wood and 3 food to grow your family with 1 member, even if the number of your rooms is lower than or equal to the number of your family members.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item See the \actionref{Family Growth without Room}{FamilyXGrowthXwithoutXRoom} (stage 5) action space.\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Spring}{Spring season}
{In the replenishment phase, add 1 fewer wood and 1 more stone to every space that you add these resources to.

\noindent Whenever you build at least 1 fence, you may build an additional 2 fences for free.
\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You get free fences only once per turn.}
\item \ecp{You also receive free fences when you use \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}, \cardref{Fence Builder}{Zaunaufsteller}{I263}, \cardref{Fence Deliveryman}{Zaunlieferant}{I265}, and \cardref{Mini Pasture}{Miniweide}{E40}.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/407649
\item \ecp{The free fences are built in the same fence building action as all other fences, and in an order of your choosing. However, you may not use one of the free fences as the first fence you build in a turn.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/459498
\item \ecp{Only after building the extra fences, you need to follow the conditions for building fences (i.e.~no open pastures).}
\item \ecp{You may choose to build fewer than 2 extra fences; however, you cannot save the free fences to build them in other turns.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\action{Spring action space}{Spring}
{You may carry out a breeding phase, or sow any number of fields, or both
(in any order). You have to perform at least one of these actions.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \emph{Sowing} See the \actionref{Sow and Bake Bread}{SowXandXBakeXBread} action space.
\item \emph{Breeding phase} \ecp{You have to receive at least one animal and have room for it in your farm to be able to take this action.}
\item \ecp{You cannot convert animals into food during this breeding phase. You can convert animals into food between sowing and breeding, if you take both actions.}
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Shepherd}{Schðfer}{E203}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Summer}{Summer season}
{In the replenishment phase, add 1 more clay and 1 fewer stone to every space that you add these resources to, and 1 more food to \actionref{Fishing}{Fishing}.

\noindent You receive an additional grain if you use the \actionref{Day Labourer}{DayXLabourer} action space.

\noindent You may build 1 free stable for every room you build, \ecp{including when you use a card to do so.}
\begin{explanationlist}
\item Building the free stable activates the \cardref{Stockman}{Tierpfleger}{E213} and \cardref{Fence Overseer}{Zaunaufseher}{K312}.
\end{explanationlist}}

\action{Summer action space}{Summer}
{You receive 1 bonus point for each person that you have already placed in the current round, including the person you place on this action space.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item Only your own persons are counted.% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/376665
\item \ecp{You also receive bonus points for guests and the occupant of the \cardref{Reed Hut}{Schilfh■tte}{K138}.}
\item \ecp{The number of placed family members is counted, not the number of actions (which may be different because of e.g.\ the \cardref{Bagpiper}{Dudelsackpfeifer}{\v{C}08}).}
\item \ecp{If you had family growth this round, you do not receive a bonus point for the newborn that was placed on the person who took that action.}% http://www.boardgamegeek.com/thread/429766
\end{explanationlist}}
}

\action{Autumn}{Autumn season}
{In the replenishment phase, add 1 more wood and 1 more reed to every space that you add these resources to.

\noindent Every major improvement costs 1 building resource of your choice less.
\begin{explanationlist}
\item \ecp{You do not benefit from the season if you use a major improvement action for an upgrade without paying resources, e.g.~a \cardref{Fireplace}{Feuerstelle}{A1/A2} to a \cardref{Cooking Hearth}{Kochstelle}{A3/A4}, or when you use a minor improvement action to play a major improvement, e.g.~with the \cardref{Well Builder}{Brunnenbauer}{I220} or \cardref{Ceramics}{Keramik}{E33}.}
\end{explanationlist}}

\action{Autumn action space}{Autumn}
{You may carry out a field phase, or take 1 vegetable, or both (in any order). You have to perform at least one of these actions.
{\begin{explanationlist}
\item \emph{Field phase} Take 1 resource from each of your fields and put them in your personal supply.
\item \ecp{Activates the \cardref{Corn Storehouse}{Korndarre}{I86}, \cardref{Water Mill}{Wasserm■hle}{I103} (only for you), and \cardref{Gardener}{Gðrtner}{I226}, but not the \cardref{Milking Shed}{Molkerei}{I93}, \cardref{Spindle}{Spinnrocken}{E51}, \cardref{Butter Churn}{Stampfbutterfass}{E53}, \cardref{Milking Stool}{Melkschemel}{K133}, \cardref{Loom}{Webstuhl}{K146}, \cardref{Milking Hand}{Melker}{I246}, and \cardref{Cube Cutter}{W■rfelschnitzer}{Z335}.}
\item \ecp{You also harvest the \cardref{Copse}{Holzacker}{I78}, \cardref{Forester}{F—rster}{K278}, and \cardref{Vineyard}{Weinberg}{ø21}.}
\end{explanationlist}}
}
\end{multicols}
